Ambasaderi wa EU mu Rwanda , Nicola Bellomo yagize ati " Inkunga yacu ni imwe mu nkunga yagutse yiswe # TeamEurope .
Ni uburyo bwo kwerekana ubufatanye .
Bikubiye kandi mu ntego za EU mu gufasha ibihugu bya inshuti mu guhangana na icyorezo cya coronavirus .
Inkunga u Rwanda rwahawe izatangwa mu byiciro bibiri .
Icya mbere kizatangwamo miliyoni 36 za amayero , ikindi gitangwemo miliyoni 15 .
5 za amayero mu gihe cya imyaka ibiri ya ingengo ya imari , 2019 / 2020 na 2020 / 2021 .
Uretse miliyoni 52 za amayero zahawe Guverinoma ya u Rwanda , EU yatanze indi nkunga ya miliyoni 1 .
8 za amayero agenewe imiryango itegamiye kuri Leta ikorana bya hafi na inzego za ibanze mu guhangana na ingaruka za coronavirus ku mibereho myiza ya abaturage .
Ambasaderi wa Umuryango wa Ubumwe bwa u Burayi mu Rwanda , Nicola Bellomo , aherutse gushima uko u Rwanda rurimo guhangana na icyorezo cya Coronavirus , yizeza ko uyu muryango uzakomeza gufatanya na rwo muri uru rugamba no mu zindi gahunda za iterambere .
Yakomeje ashimira ingamba u Rwanda rwafashe mu gukumira no guhangana na icyorezo cya Coronavirus , zirimo gahunda ya guma mu rugo , gukaraba intoki , guhana intera na izindi nyinshi .
Ambasaderi Bellomo yavuze ko bishimira ubufatanye burambye hagati ya EU na u Rwanda , bushingiye nanone ku bufatanye hagati ya imigabane ya Afurika na u Burayi .
Yavuze kandi ko muri ibi bihe bya Coronavirus barimo gukorana na u Rwanda mu kurebera hamwe uko inkunga yakwifashishwa guhangana na iki cyorezo .
Mu mwaka wa 2020 / 21 , u Rwanda ruteganya kuzakoresha ingengo ya imari ingana miliyari 3245 .
7 Frw ivuye kuri 3017 .
1 Frw yakoreshejwe mu mwaka wa ingengo ya imari ushize .
Minecofin iherutse gutangariza abagize Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ko ingengo ya imari ya 2020 / 21 , izibanda mu guhangana na ingaruka icyorezo cya Coronavirus , cyagize mu bukungu na imibereho myiza ya abaturage , ikazakoreshwa mu gushyira mu bikorwa gahunda ya igihugu yo kuzahura ubukungu izakoreshwamo agera muri miliyari 882 Frw mu myaka ibiri ya ingengo ya imari , ni ukuvuga uyu wa 2019 / 20 na utaha wa 2020 / 21
uzatangira muri Nyakanga .
Mu nyandiko ya igenamigambi ryo kuzahura ubukungu bwashegeshwe na ingaruka za Coronavirus , gahunda ya imibereho myiza ya abaturage izatwara 133 616 548 506 Frw .
Kwita ku batishoboye , gushyigikira ibikorwa bya ubuvuzi , ubuhinzi , gutera inkunga ibigo bya leta , imishinga ya ibikorwa remezo , inkunga ya leta mu kigega cyo kuzahura ubukungu na izindi ngamba , bizitabwaho mu kuzahura ubukungu .
Prime Life Insurance yatangije " Ikimina cyacu " " " " , ubwishingizi buzorohereza Abanyarwanda kwizigamira
Sosiyete ya Ubwishingizi ya Prime Life Insurance yatangije ku mugaragaro ubwishingizi bwitwa Ikimina cyacu bwitezweho gusobanurira neza Abanyarwanda akamaro ko kwizigamira no kuborohereza kubigeraho .
Sosiyete ya Ubwishingizi ya Prime Life Insurance yatangije ku mugaragaro ubwishingizi bwitwa Ikimina cyacu bwitezweho gusobanurira neza Abanyarwanda akamaro ko kwizigamira no kuborohereza kubigeraho .
Ikimina cyacu ni gahunda Prime Life Insurance yatekerejeho igendeye ku buryo bwa gakondo bwa Abanyarwanda bwo kwizigamira busanzwe buzwi nka ibimina , ariko yo ibushyira mu buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga kandi burushaho gutanga umutekano ku mafaranga ya ababugannye .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Prime Life Insurance , Habarurema Innocent , yavuze ko Ikimina cyacu cyatangijwe nyuma yo kubona hakiri imbogamizi mu buryo bwo kwiteganyiriza butekanye , bworohereza abaturage kandi bukanabungukira .
Yashimangiye ko basanze bakwiye gushyiraho ubu buryo kugira ngo barusheho kugira uruhare mu iterambere rya Abanyarwanda .
Yakomeje ati " Igituma bagomba kugana Prime Life Insurance mu buryo bwa umwihariko , ni uko noneho bafite umutekano wizewe wa amafaranga yabo kandi bakayabonaho na inyungu .
Ikindi akaba ashobora kuyategurira umushinga runaka wa igihe kigufi cyangwa kirekire .
Kumenya amafaranga ufitemo na inyungu zayo ubirebera muri telefoni yawe .
Ku wifuza kwinjira muri ubu buryo bwo kwiteganyiriza abikora yifashishije telefoni igendanwa aho yandika * 177 # , agahitamo ahanditse " Ubuzima no Kwizigamira " " " " ubundi agakurikiza amabwiriza .
Ku watangiye gukoresha ubu buryo buri mwaka yungukirwa 3 % bya amafaranga bya ubwiteganyirize bwe , kandi mu gihe yamaze gutanga ubwiteganyirize bwa amezi atatu akaba yabikuzaho agera kuri 50 % , amezi atandatu 70 % naho nyuma ya umwaka akabikuza 100 % .
Habarurema yagiriye inama Abanyarwanda ko kwizigama bitakabaye bikorwa na usaguye , ahubwo ni ukureba kure .
Umwe mu bamaze ukwezi batangiye gukoresha Ikimina Cyacu , Habanabariho Théoneste avuga ko kuri we amaze kubibonamo inyungu nyinshi .
Yagize ati " Iki kimina iyo ukigiyemo uba wizigamye kandi ufite na ubwishingizi icya rimwe , kuko tuzi ahahise ariko uko ejo bizagenda ntabyo tuzi , niyo mpamvu nyamukuru kuri njyewe nahisemo iki kimina .
Abanyarwanda bibukijwe kugira umuco wo kwiteganyiriza no kwigira ku bihe igihugu kimazemo iminsi kubera icyorezo cya COVID - 19 .
Umuyobozi wa Inama ya Ubutegetsi ya Prime Life Insurance , Ceaser Nkusi Nkwesi , yavuze ko " Kwizigamira ntabwo bisaba amafaranga menshi , bisaba gusa gufata icyemezo ukabifata nka igikorwa cya ingirakamaro mu buzima bwawe kigufasha mu bihe biri imbere , cyane cyane ibitunguranye bisaba amafaranga .
Uwayobotse ikimina cyacu mu gihe yitabye Imana , Prime Life Insurance iha umuryango we umusanzu yari amaze kugezamo na inyungu zawo hakaniyongeraho na impozamarira ingana na 5 % ya ubwizigame bwose .
Uretse ubu bwiteganyirize bwa Ikimina Cyacu , Prime Life Insurance Ltd ifite ubundi buryo bwo kwiteganyiriza burimo guteganyiriza amashuri ya abana mu byiciro byose , Ubwishingizi bwa umuryango , guteganyiriza iza bukuru , ubwishingizi bwa abakozi mu ngeri zose , ubwishingizi bwo gutabara ndetse na ubwishingizi ku nguzanyo .

Umubare wa abatunze miliyoni 1 $ wikubye gatatu mu myaka 20 ishize
Reporo ya Ikigo cyitwa Boston Consulting Group ( BCG ) , ku butunzi bwa abatuye Isi , yerekanye ko umubare wa abatunze miliyoni imwe ya amadolari kuzamura wiyongereye , aho wikubye gatatu mu myaka 20 ishize .
Reporo ya Ikigo cyitwa Boston Consulting Group ( BCG ) , ku butunzi bwa abatuye Isi , yerekanye ko umubare wa abatunze miliyoni imwe ya amadolari kuzamura wiyongereye , aho wikubye gatatu mu myaka 20 ishize .
Iyi raporo yasohotse kuri uyu wa Kane , yerekanye ko mu mpera za 2019 , abarenga miliyoni 24 ku Isi yose , buri umwe afite ubutunzi bubarirwa nibura muri miliyoni imwe ya amadolari cyangwa kurenzaho ugereranyije na miliyoni 8 .
9 bari bayitunze mu 1999 , bivuze ko bikubye hafi gatatu .
Mu myaka 20 ishize kandi , ubutunzi bwa abantu ku giti cyabo ku Isi yose bwikubye hafi gatatu buva kuri miliyari ibihumbi $ 80 mu 1999 bugera kuri miliyari ibihumbi $ 226 , mu mpera za 2019 .
Uteranyije ubutunzi bwa abatunze miliyoni ya amadolari ku Isi yose , bungana na 50 % , bya ubutunzi bwa Isi yose mu 2019 .
Abenshi mu batunze nibura miliyoni 1 $ , ni abo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Mu 2019 , mu Bushinwa , abatunze nibura miliyoni 1 $ , bikubye inshuro 29 , ugereranyije na 1999 .
Ibiciro ku isoko byiyongereyeho 10 , 1 % muri Mata 2019
Ikigo cya igihugu gishinzwe ibarurishamibare mu Rwanda ( NISR ) , cyatangaje ko muri Mata 2020 , ibiciro bikomatanyirijwe hamwe mu mijyi no mu byaro , byiyongereyeho 10 , 1 % , ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ikigo cya igihugu gishinzwe ibarurishamibare mu Rwanda ( NISR ) , cyatangaje ko muri Mata 2020 , ibiciro bikomatanyirijwe hamwe mu mijyi no mu byaro , byiyongereyeho 10 , 1 % , ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ihinduka rya ibiciro mu Rwanda muri Werurwe 2020 , ryari ku kigereranyo kingana na 13 , 1 % , ugereranyije na ukwezi nka uku kwa 2019 .
Itangazo ryashyizwe ahagaragara na NISR , kuwa 10 Gicurasi 2020 , rigaragaza ko bimwe mu byatumye ibiciro byiyongeraho 10 , 1 % mu kwezi kwa Mata 2020 ni ibiciro bya ibiribwa na ibinyobwa bidasembuye byazamutseho 18 , 7 % na ibiciro bya ibinyobwa bisembuye na itabi byazamutseho 21 , 3 % .
Ku rundi ruhande ariko , iyo ugereranyije ukwezi kwa kane ( Mata 2020 ) na ukwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) ibiciro byagabanutseho 1 , 8 % , ukomatanyije mu mijyi no mu byaro .
NISR iti " Iri gabanuka ahanini ryatewe na ibiciro bya ibiribwa na ibinyobwa bidasembuye byagabanutseho 3 % na ibiciro bya amazu , amazi , amashanyarazi , gazi na ibindi bicanwa byagabanutseho 3 , 3 % " " " " .
Uko ibiciro byazamutse mu mijyi no mu byaro
NISR yatangaje ko ibiciro mu mijyi byiyongereyeho 8 % mu kwezi gushize kwa Mata 2020 ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ihinduka rya ibiciro mu kwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) ryari ku kigereranyo kingana na 8 , 5 % .
Ikomeza igira iti " Bimwe mu byatumye ibiciro byiyongeraho 8 % mu kwezi kwa Mata , ni ibiciro bya ibiribwa na ibinyobwa bidasembuye byazamutseho 15 , 8 % , ibiciro bya ibinyobwa bisembuye na itabi byazamutseho 17 , 4 % na ibiciro bya amazu , amazi , amashanyarazi , gazi na ibindi bicanwa byazamutseho 6 , 5 % " " " " .
Iyo ugereranyije Mata 2020 na Mata 2019 , usanga ibiciro bya ibintu bitarimo ibiribwa na ibikomoka ku ngufu byarazamutseho 4 , 6 % .
Wagereranya ukwezi kwa kane ( Mata 2020 ) na ukwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) , ibiciro byagabanutseho 0 , 2 % .
Iri gabanuka ahanini ryatewe na ibiciro bya ibiribwa na ibinyobwa bidasembuye byagabanutseho 2 , 1 % .
NISR ivuga ko muri Mata 2020 , ibiciro mu byaro byiyongereyeho 11 , 7 % ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ihinduka rya ibiciro mu byaro mu kwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) ryari ku kigereranyo kingana na 16 , 5 % .
NISR yagize iti " Bimwe mu byatumye ibiciro byiyongeraho 11 , 7 % mu kwezi kwa Mata ni ibiciro bya ibiribwa na ibinyobwa bidasembuye byazamutseho 20 % na ibiciro bya ibinyobwa bisembuye na itabi byazamutseho 23 , 2 % " " " " .
Ugereranyije ukwezi kwa kane ( Mata 2020 ) na ukwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) , ibiciro byagabanutseho 3 % .
Iri gabanuka ahanini ryatewe na ibiciro bya ibiribwa na ibinyobwa bidasembuye byagabanutseho 3 , 4 % na ibiciro bya amazu , amazi , amashanyarazi , gazi na ibindi bicanwa byagabanutseho 8 % .
Banki zavuguruye inguzanyo za miliyari 255 Frw mu korohereza abakiliya mu bihe bya Coronavirus
Banki Nkuru ya u Rwanda yatangaje ko amabanki amaze kuvugurura inguzanyo 7952 zifite agaciro ka miliyari 255 Frw , mu korohereza abakiliya bayo kwishyura , nyuma ya ingaruka ingamba zafashwe mu gukumira Coronavirus zagize ku bukungu bwabo .
Banki Nkuru ya u Rwanda yatangaje ko amabanki amaze kuvugurura inguzanyo 7952 zifite agaciro ka miliyari 255 Frw , mu korohereza abakiliya bayo kwishyura , nyuma ya ingaruka ingamba zafashwe mu gukumira Coronavirus zagize ku bukungu bwabo .
Ku wa 18 Werurwe nibwo Banki Nkuru ya u Rwanda yatangaje ingamba zirimo kwemerera amabanki gusubiramo amasezerano ya inguzanyo yagiranye na abakiliya , kugira ngo azorohereze abayabereyemo imyenda mu gihe cyo kwishyura .
Nka Banki ya Kigali kimwe na izindi za ubucuruzi zashyizeho igihe gishobora kugera ku mezi atatu umuntu ashobora guhabwa atishyura inguzanyo yahawe cyangwa inyungu zayo , igihe bigaragara ko ibikorwa bye byagizweho ingaruka na ibi bihe bikomeye .
Imyanzuro ya Akanama ka Komite ishinzwe politiki ya ifaranga yateranye kuri uyu wa 29 Mata 2020 , igaragaza ko kugeza ku wa 10 Mata , amabanki yavuguruye inguzanyo 7952 mu 8667 za abari basabye koroherezwa , zifite agaciro ka miliyari 255 Frw .
BNR kandi yari yagabanyije igipimo cya amafaranga ya ubwizigame banki zitajya munsi kiba 4 % kivuye kuri 5 % kugira ngo nazo zifashe izindi nzego za ubucuruzi zazahungabanywa na COVID - 19 .
Mu zindi mpinduka Banki Nkuru ya Igihugu yakoze , harimo ko yagabanyije inyungu ku nguzanyo ihabwa amabanki ivanwa kuri 5 % ishyirwa kuri 4 .
5 % , hagamijwe kuzifasha kugira ngo zikomeze gutanga amafaranga mu baturage bayakeneye muri ibi bihe , no mu bukungu bwa igihugu muri rusange .
Ikigega cya Miliyari 100 Frw , imwe mu ngamba zigiye kwifashishwa mu kuzahura ubukungu bwa u Rwanda
Guverinoma ya u Rwanda igeze kure gahunda igamije kuzahura ubukungu nyuma ya uko inzego hafi ya zose mu gihugu zigizweho ingaruka na icyorezo cya Coronavirus , kubera ibikorwa byafunzwe mu kwirinda ko gikwirakwira .
Guverinoma ya u Rwanda igeze kure gahunda igamije kuzahura ubukungu nyuma ya uko inzego hafi ya zose mu gihugu zigizweho ingaruka na icyorezo cya Coronavirus , kubera ibikorwa byafunzwe mu kwirinda ko gikwirakwira .
Ubukungu byitezwe ko bushobora kuzamuka ku kigero cya 2 % aho kuba 8 % Ikigega cya miliyari 100 Frw kizatangira mu cyumweru kimwe kiri imbere Ibigo bito na ibiciriritse bigiye gufashwa kubona ingwate
Ku Isi yose ubukungu bukomeje kuzahara ari nayo mpamvu za leta zafashe ingamba zitandukanye zo kwivana mu bibazo .
Nka Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ziherutse gutangaza ko muri iki gihembwe hagati ya Mata na Kamena izaguza miliyari $ 2 , 999 , kubera ihungabana rya ibikorwa na ingengo na ingengo ya imari .
Banki ya Isi iherutse gukora ikigereranyo yerekana ko ubukungu bwa Afurika buzasubira inyuma mu buryo bukomeye ku nshuro ya mbere mu myaka 25 biturutse kuri Coronavirus .
Imibare ya Banki ya Isi yo kuwa 9 Mata igaragaza ko ubukungu bwo muri Afurika yo munsi ya Ubutayu bwa Sahara , bwagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus ndetse ko buzamanuka ku kigero cya - 2 .
1 % buvuye kuri 2 .
4 % bwariho mu 2019 .
Ikigega Mpuzamahanga cya Imari ku Isi , IMF , nacyo giherutse gutanga ikigereranyo ko umusaruro mbumbe wa Isi muri uyu mwaka uzamanuka ku mpuzandengo ya - 3 % naho uwa ubukungu bwa ibihugu byateye imbere kurusha ibindi bumanuke ku kigero cya - 6 % .
Minisitiri wa Imari na Igenamigambi , Dr Ndagijimana Uzziel , ati " Ni ibintu bikomeye bidaheruka mu mateka ya Isi .
Muri Afurika yo munsi ya Ubutayu bwa Sahara , hateganyijwe ko ubukungu buzamanuka - 1 .
6 % [ … ] natwe rero birumvikana ko ubukungu bwacu butazagenda uko busanzwe buteganyijwe .
Dr Ndagijimana yavuze ko icyorezo cya Coronavirus cyagize ingaruka ku ngeri zose atanga urugero nko ku bukerarugendo aho amahoteli na indege byahagaze mu kwirinda ko iki cyorezo cyakomeza gukwirakwira .
Raporo ya Ishami rya Ubukerarugendo mu Rugaga rwa Abikorera , PSF , iherutse kugaragaza ko muri Werurwe bwagize igihombo cya Miliyari 34 .
9 Frw , bitewe na inama zasubitswe na ibindi bikorwa bya ubukerarugendo byahagaritswe .
Ibi bihombo byaje bisanga urwego rwa ubukerarugendo mu Rwanda rufite inguzanyo za miliyari 87 .
7 Frw , aho urwego rwa amahoteli arirwo rwihariye inguzanyo nini kuko rufite izingana na miliyari 83 .
Minisitiri Dr Ndagijimana yavuze ko ubu igipimo cya ubukungu bwa u Rwanda kigaragaza ko butazazamuka ku kigero cya 8 % nka uko byari byitezwe , aho ubu imibare yagiye ivugururwa ikava kuri 5 .
1 % , nyuma biramanuka bigera kuri 3 .
5 % " ubu turi hafi kuri 2 % nubwo bitari byarangira neza " " " " .
Yavuze ko ibi bipimo bidashingira ku buryo ubukungu bwa igihugu bumeze ahubwo harebwa no ku ruhando mpuzamahanga .
Ati " Uko ibintu bihinduka ku Isi , niko imibare igenda isubira inyuma " " " " .
Hagiye gutangizwa ikigega cya miliyari 100 Frw cyo mu kuzahura ubukungu
Mu ngamba zigamije kuzahura ubukungu , u Rwanda rwashyize ingufu mu buhinzi , hategurwa ibihembwe bya ihinga biri imbere ku buryo abahinzi bahabwa amafumbire na imbuto kugira ngo hazaboneke umusaruro mwiza bityo igihugu gikomeze kwihaza mu biribwa kinasagurira amasoko .
Ikindi ni ukwihutisha imishinga yari yaratangiye itanga akazi , cyane iya ibikorwa remezo , nka inyubako na ibindi .
Ati " Hari imishinga ya imihanda , iya amazi , iya amashanyarazi , kugira ngo amafaranga agere ku bantu " " " " .
Hari kandi gukomeza gushyira ingufu muri gahunda zo gufasha abatishoboye yaba mu kubaha imirimo , kubaha inkunga ku badashobora gukora na inguzanyo iciriritse ishobora kwifashishwa mu gukora imirimo ibyara inyungu .
Indi gahunda yihariye igamije gufasha abashoramari na abikorera mu byiciro bitandukanye bagizweho ingaruka na iki cyorezo , aho leta yashyizeho gahunda yo gutangiza ikigega kibafasha kubona amafaranga yo gukoresha .
Ati " Ni ikigega cyafasha amabanki gutanga inguzanyo iciriritse yafasha ibyo byiciro byose kugira ngo bigaruke mu kazi byongere bikore , bibyare umusaruro uzagire ingaruka mu kuzamuka ka ubukungu muri rusange .
Yakomeje atangaza ko " Icyo kigega cyaranogejwe , harimo inkunga yihariye ku mahoteli kuko bigaragara ko ubukerarugendo bizamara igihe kugira ngo bwongere buzanzamuke kuko ntibiterwa na uko ibihe byifashe mu Rwanda ahubwo uko byifashe ku Isi hose .
Dr Ndagijimana yavuze muri icyo kigega hashyizwemo ingamba zihariye zifasha amahoteli kuvugurura amasezerano ya inguzanyo afite mu mabanki akaba igihe kirekire na inyungu zikagabanuka , ndetse ku buryo mu gihe yatangiye gufungura , abona amafaranga aciriritse kugira ngo imirimo yongere ikore .
Yavuze ko icyo kigega " kizafasha ubucuruzi ubwo aribwo bwose bwagizweho ingaruka , hari ibipimo bizagenderwaho kugira ngo ababirimo babone amafaranga aciriritse ku gihe cyiza noneho bongere bakore bihutishe imirimo " " " " .
Ibigo bito na ibiciriritse nabyo biri mu bizahabwa inguzanyo na ingwate kuko ingwate zikunze kuba ikibazo kuri bene ibyo byiciro .
Ni ikigega biteganyijwe ko gishobora kujyamo nka Miliyari 100 Frw avuye muri leta , ariko hagakomeza gushakwa na abandi bashyiramo amafaranga kugira ngo cyaguke .
Ati " Turateganya ko mu gihe cya icyumweru kimwe cyaba gitangiye " " " " .
Mu kugabanya icyuho kiri hagati ya ibyoherezwa mu mahanga na ibitumizwayo , u Rwanda rurateganya gukomeza guteza imbere ibikorerwa mu Rwanda , abanyarwanda bagakangukira kubigura kugira ngo bisimbure ibyo hanze .
Leta ntiteganya kugabanya imirimo
Kuva icyorezo cya COVID - 19 cyatangira , ibigo byinshi cyane ibya abikorera , byafashe ingamba zitandukanye zigamije gutuma bidafunga imiryango kubera igabanuka rya amafaranga byinjizaga .
Ibyinshi byahagaritse abakozi , ibindi byumvikana nabo bagabanyirizwa imishahara .
Dr Ndagijimana avuga ko abikorera bagerageje guhangana na iki cyorezo , ku buryo na abagabanya imirimo na imishahara , bagerageje kwita ku nyungu za abakozi .
Ba nyakabyizi nibo Dr Ndagijimana asanga barahuye na ikibazo gikomeye , ariko ko bishingiye ku ngamba leta yafashe mu kuzahura ubukungu , hari icyizere ko ibibazo bizakemuka vuba .
Yavuze ko nta gahunda ihari yo kuba leta yagabanya imirimo ati " turacyafite ubushobozi bwo guhemba abakozi " " " " .
Ku barimu , Minisitiri wa Imari na Igenamigambi , yavuze ko aba leta bazakomeza guhembwa nka abandi bakozi ariko ko ku bo mu mashuri yigenga bazafashwa binyuze mu buryo bwo koroshya inguzanyo na ubundi bwashyizweho .
Uruganda rwa Kinazi rwasabye abantu kwita ku buziranenge igihe bagiye kugura ifu ya ubugari
Uruganda rutunganya ifu ikomoka ku myumbati rwa Kinazi ( Kinazi Cassava Plant ) , rwatangaje ko rukora ibishoboka byose ngo ifu yarwo igere ku isoko ifite ubuziranenge , ariko rusaba abantu kujya bashishoza mu gihe bagiye guhaha kuko hari abashobora kunyura ku ruhande bakabagurisha itujuje ubuziranenge ku buryo yabagwa nabi .
Uruganda rutunganya ifu ikomoka ku myumbati rwa Kinazi ( Kinazi Cassava Plant ) , rwatangaje ko rukora ibishoboka byose ngo ifu yarwo igere ku isoko ifite ubuziranenge , ariko rusaba abantu kujya bashishoza mu gihe bagiye guhaha kuko hari abashobora kunyura ku ruhande bakabagurisha itujuje ubuziranenge ku buryo yabagwa nabi .
Tariki 7 Kamena buri mwaka , Isi yizihiza umunsi mpuzamahanga wahariwe ubuziranenge bwa ibiribwa , buri wese asabwa kugira uruhare mu guharanira ubwo buziranenge .
Ishami rya Umuryango wa Abibumbye ryita ku Buzima ku Isi , OMS , ritangaza ko ibiribwa bitujuje ubuziranenge bihitana abantu bagera ku bihumbi 420 buri mwaka .
OMS igaragaza ko abana bari munsi ya imyaka itanu aribo bibasirwa cyane na ibi biribwa , kuko abapfa bagera ku bihumbi 125 buri mwaka .
Kugeza ubu imyaka umunani irashize uruganda rwa Kinazi rufite icyicaro mu Ntara ya Amajyepfo mu Karere ka Ruhango rugeza ifu ku banyarwanda na abanyamahanga .
Uru ruganda rusaba abantu gukomeza gukoresha ifu yarwo ariko banirinda izindi fu bashobora kugura kandi zitujuje ubuziranenge ku buryo byanabaviramo gupfa .
Umuyobozi wa Uruganda , Mbabazi Christian , mu kiganiro yahaye IGIHE , yavuze ko kugeza ubu uru ruganda ruhagaze neza kuko rwakira umusaruro wa abaturage kuva mu bice bitandukanye bya Amajyepfo mu Turere dutanu , ariko ubu bageze no mu Burasirazuba mu Karere ka Bugesera , aho batangiye gukorana na abaturage baho bakabagezaho umusaruro .
Ati " Uruganda rufite ubushobozi bwo kwakira toni 120 za umusaruro wa abaturage ku munsi murumva ko ari mwinshi , ibi byanatumye tuva mu Majyepfo tujya no mu Burasirazuba ariko dukomeje gukangurira na ibindi bice bya igihugu guhinga imyumbati bakagemurira uruganda , kuko usanga uruganda rugikora ku kigero cya 35 % gusa .
Ubuziranenge buhagaze gute ?
Mbabazi yavuze ko ku bijyanye na ubuziranenge hari byinshi leta yakoze harimo gushyiraho ibigo bishinzwe ubwo buziranenge ku rwego rwa igihugu , ibi bikaba aribyo bigenzura ibyo bakora , bikaba ari nabyo bibaha ibyangombwa .
Ati " Ibyo bigo byose bikorana na Minisiteri ya Ubucuruzi na Inganda ku buryo bashobora no kuba baguhana mu gihe basanze ukora ibitujuje ubuziranenge cyangwa bakaba banagufungira .
" Nka ubu mu gice cyacu cya abakora ifu hari abandi usanga nabo bakora iya imyumbati , twe nka Kinazi turi banini ariko hari abandi bato kandi badafite ibyo byangombwa .
Abo iyo bakoze nta byangombwa cyangwa nta buziranenge nibwo usanga bakoze ibyo bashatse na igiciro bakaba bakigira gito , ariko bikarenga aho kuko abantu barya ibintu bihumanye .
Tujya tuganira na leta bakatubwira ko babikurikirana kandi nkeka ko uko ibintu biza bizagenda bikosoka .
Hari ibyago ku muntu warya ibitujuje ubuziranenge
Mbabazi yavuze ko abantu bakwiye kujya bagenzura ifu bagiye kugura , bakareba niba yujuje ibisabwa ndetse ifite na ibirango bitangwa na Ikigo gishinzwe Ubuziranenge .
Ati " Twebwe nka uruganda ibyo dukwiye gukora turabikora no ku rwego rwa igihugu ni uko , hano mu ruganda dufite itsinda ku buryo nta kintu cyasohoka kitabanje kugenzurwa ko cyujuje ubuziranenge , icyo dusaba abantu ni ukurya ifu yacu ariko bakwiye kumenya ko ushobora kurya ibihumanye bikaba byakugiraho ingaruka .
Uru ruganda ruvuga ko nubwo rutarabona abantu barwiyitirira ariko hari bamwe bumva ko bashobora kuba bafata ifu ya Kinazi , bakayipfunyika mu bindi bipfunyiko byabo , bakaba bayigurisha ku mafaranga menshi mu mahanga kuko isanzwe ari nziza .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe ubuziranenge muri uru ruganda , Ngabonzima Viateur , yavuze ko mu ruganda bagenzura isuku ya abantu , imashini na ibindi byose .
Ati " Ifu ya uruganda rwa Kinazi yahawe ikirango cya ubuziranenge gitangwa na Ikigo gitsura ubuziranenge , RSB , twanarenze imbibi ku buryo ifu yacu yemewe na ikigo cya Abanyamerika kigenzura ubuziranenge bwa ibiribwa , ubu ishobora gucuzwa ku isoko rya Amerika .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe umusaruro winjira muri uru ruganda , Rutagungira Eve Nicolas , we yavuze ko uruganda rukorana neza na abaruzanira imyumbati , kuva rwatangira mu 2012 .
Kugeza ubu uruganda rwa Kinazi rufite isoko mu Rwanda no ku mugabane wa u Burayi , ibijya hanze bikaba biri ku kigero kirenze 40 % , aho ruteganya no kwagura rukajya muri Amerika kuko naho hari isoko rinini .
Uru ruganda rutangaza ko ifu yarwo idakorwamo ubugari gusa , ahubwo ishobora kuvangwa na andi mafu igakorwamo keke , Capati , Pizza na ibindi .
COVID - 19 : Amabwiriza yagenaga amafaranga ntarengwa SACCO zemerewe kubikuriza abanyamuryango yakuweho
Banki Nkuru ya u Rwanda , BNR , yakuyeho amabwiriza yari yashyizeho agena amafaranga ntarengwa amakoperative yo kubitsa no kugurizanya ( SACCOs ) yemerewe kubikuriza abanyamuryango bayo .
Banki Nkuru ya u Rwanda , BNR , yakuyeho amabwiriza yari yashyizeho agena amafaranga ntarengwa amakoperative yo kubitsa no kugurizanya ( SACCOs ) yemerewe kubikuriza abanyamuryango bayo .
Izo ngamba zari zashyizweho ku wa 24 Werurwe 2020 nyuma ya iminsi ibiri ibikorwa byinshi bihagaritswe , abaturage bagasabwa kuguma mu ngo hirindwa ikwirakwira rya icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Izo ngamba zavugaga ko nta SACCO yemerewe kurenza amafaranga ibihumbi 150 , abikuzwa na umunyamuryango umwe usanzwe , mu cyumweru .
SACCO kandi ntabwo yari yemerewe kubikuriza arenze ibihumbi 500 Frw mu cyumweru ku mucuruzi wa ibiribwa cyangwa ucuruza ibikoresho bya ibanze mu gihe aho SACCO ikorana na amatsinda , buri tsinda ryari ryemerewe kubikuza amafaranga yo kugabana ku buryo buri munyamuryango wa itsinda atarenza ibihumbi 50 mu cyumweru .
Nyuma ya uko inama ya abaminisitiri yateranye kuwa 30 Mata 2020 yemereye bimwe mu bikorwa gukomeza , BNR yakuyeho ayo mabwiriza .
Itangazo ryashyizweho umukono na Guverineri wa BNR , John Rwangombwa rigira riti " Ibipimo ntarengwa byihariye byo kubikuza byari byashyizweho na itangazo ryo kuwa 24 Werurwe 2020 bikuweho kugira ngo abanyamuryango ba ayo makoperative babashe gukora imirimo yabo nta nzitizi .
BNR yasabye SACCO gukomeza gukurikiza amategeko na amabwiriza asanzwe agenga urwego rwa imari iciriritse .
Uko ikoranabuhanga ryunguye bamwe rigahombya abandi kubera Coronavirus
Icyorezo cya Coronavirus kimaze kwandurwa na abarenga miliyoni enye kigahitana abasaga ibihumbi 287 , ku Isi yose , kiravumirwa ku gahera na abakora ibikorwa bya ubucuruzi , nubwo bamwe mu bafite ibigo bya ikoranabuhanga bakomeje kubyinira ku rukoma .
Icyorezo cya Coronavirus kimaze kwandurwa na abarenga miliyoni enye kigahitana abasaga ibihumbi 287 , ku Isi yose , kiravumirwa ku gahera na abakora ibikorwa bya ubucuruzi , nubwo bamwe mu bafite ibigo bya ikoranabuhanga bakomeje kubyinira ku rukoma .
Bitewe na ingamba zitandukanye zo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Coronavirus , ibihugu bitandukanye byafashe cyane cyane gahunda ya guma mu rugo , abaturage benshi barifashisha ikoranabuhanga mu gusaba serivisi , kugura no gutuma ibicuruzwa ndetse no kuganira no gukora inama .
Bitewe no gukorera mu rugo , ibigo bitanga serivisi za ikoranabuhanga rifasha abantu kuganira no kuba bakora inama ari benshi byarungutse .
Urugero ni nka Zoom ikomeje gufasha abantu benshi gukora inama .
Nubwo hari ibibazo bya umutekano byakomeje kuvugwa kuri Zoom , ntibyabujije abayikoresha ndetse na igiciro cyayo kwiyongera , aho cyikubye inshuro zirenga ebyiri kuva mu Ukuboza .
Umubare wa abakoresha Zoom wavuye kuri miliyoni 10 ku munsi ugera kuri miliyoni 200 .
Ikoreshwa mu nzego zose kuva ku bakora inama za abaminisitiri kugeza ku bashumba bifuza kuvugana uko umukamo uhagaze na ibindi .
Hari kandi abakoresha ubundi buryo .
Muri Werurwe , Microsoft Teams , yavuze ko abayikoresha mu kuganira , gukora inama na irindi tumanaho bageze kuri miliyoni 44 , rikaba ari izamuka rya 40 % .
Teamviewer nayo ikoreshwa mu kuganira no gukora inama , nayo itangaza ko irimo gukoreshwa cyane muri iyi minsi mu buryo budasanzwe naho ubuyobozi bwa Slack , buvuga ko abayikoresha umunsi ku munsi bakomeje kwiyongera .
Uburyo bwo kureba filime na indi myidagaduro , bwakuruye benshi muri iki gihe cya guma mu rugo .
Urubuga rwa Netflix kuri ubu rwabaye ubuzima kuri bamwe mu bakunda imyidagaduro cyane cyane abakunda kureba filime , ni rumwe mu zungutse cyane .
Netflix ni Ikigo cya Abanyamerika cyerekana amashusho binyuze kuri internet .
Yerekana ibiganiro byo mu bihugu bitandukanye biciye kuri internet birimo nka filime mbarankuru na iz ubundi bwoko , ariko bigasaba kubanza kuba umufatabuguzi .
Netflix irebwa mu bihugu 190 hirya no hino ku Isi , aho ifite abakiliya basaga miliyoni 182 .
Yabonye abayikoresha bashya bagera kuri miliyoni 16 muri ibi bihe bya Coronavirus .
Uburyo bwo kwerekana amashusho bwa Disney + , ni irindi koranabuhanga ryungutse kubera Coronavirus , kuko nko mu mpera za Werurwe bwatangijwe mu bindi bihugu birimo na u Bwongereza .
Icyo gihe Disney + yari ifite abakiriya barenga miliyoni 33 , ubu ifite abagera kuri 55 , bituma ihanganye ku isoko na Netflix .
Ikigo Spotify , gifasha abantu kubona umuziki , filime na ibindi muri guma mu rugo cyabonye abakiliya miliyoni 130 baguze ifatabuguzi .
Ibigo bifite ikoranabuhanga rifasha abantu kubona imyitozo ngororamubiri bakora muri iki gihe cya Coronavirus , biri mu byungutse cyane .
Urugero ni ClassPass , urubuga rutuma abantu babona imyitozo bakora .
Uru rubuga ruvuga ko abarukoresha biyongereye cyane .
Urundi rubuga rwa Peloton , rwerekana amashusho ajyanye no kunyonga igare .
Nubwo byasabye ko Peloton ifunga studio zayo nyuma yo kugaragaramo uwanduye Coronavirus , ibyo yinjije byazamutseho ibirenga 60 % .
Ushyira amashusho kuri YouTube , Joe Wicks , na we yungukiye kuri Coronavirus kuko yaciye agahigo akajya no mu gitabo Guinness World Record kubera kwerekana amashusho ya imyitozo ngororamubiri igihe kirekire ndetse ibigo bikomeye muri siporo biravugwa ko byatangiye kumurwanira .
Urubuga Amazon rwo guhahiraho , na rwo rwagize ibihe byiza mu gihe cya Coronavirus .
Uru rubuga rwashinzwe na Jeff Bezos , umuherwe wa mbere ku Isi , agaciro karwo kageze kuri miliyari 24 za amadolari muri Coronavirus .
Agaciro ka imigabane ya Amazon ku isoko karazamutse cyane .
Amazon yahaye akazi abandi bantu 175 000 bo kuyifasha guhaza abakiliya babaye benshi muri iki gihe cya guma mu rugo .
Agaciro ka ibyacurujwe kageze kuri miliyari 75 .
5 za amadolari ni ukuvuga ko kiyongereyeho 27 % mu mezi ya Coronavirus .
Abantu bareba filime kuko ntaho barimo kujya .
Nko mu Bwongereza , kugurisha imodoka byasubiye hasi ku rwego ruto ruheruka kubaho mu 1946 .
Sosiyete itwara abantu , Uber , yagabanyije abakozi mu biro byayo .
Aba ariko ntabwo barimo abashoferi bikorera ndetse na bo barimo guhangana na iki cyorezo .
Mu bindi bigo bya ikoranabuhanga byungutse kubera Coronavirus , ni ibicuruza imikino ( Gaming ) , aho abantu benshi bayihugiraho .
BRD yabaye banki ya mbere yo mu Rwanda igenzuwe na Fitch Ratings , ihabwa inota rya B +
Banki ya u Rwanda Itsura Amajyambere , BRD , yabaye iya mbere yo mu Rwanda igenzuwe na Ikigo Mpuzamahanga gikurikirana ibijyanye na imyenda na Ubushakashatsi mu bya Imari , Fitch Ratings , iyiha inota rya B + rigaragaza ko imari yayo ihagaze neza ndetse na ahazaza hayo hameze neza .
Banki ya u Rwanda Itsura Amajyambere , BRD , yabaye iya mbere yo mu Rwanda igenzuwe na Ikigo Mpuzamahanga gikurikirana ibijyanye na imyenda na Ubushakashatsi mu bya Imari , Fitch Ratings , iyiha inota rya B + rigaragaza ko imari yayo ihagaze neza ndetse na ahazaza hayo hameze neza .
Ubusanzwe Fitch yatangaga amanota kuri za Guverinoma nka u Rwanda .
Nko mu 2016 Fitch Ratings yahaye u Rwanda inota rya B + ishingiye ku kuba izamuka rya ibiciro ku masoko ryari riri hasi kandi u Rwanda rukaba rwarabashaga kurigumisha ku gipimo gikwiye bigendanye na iterambere rya ubukungu .
Hiyongereyeho kuba amafaranga ya umwenda rwari rufite yari make ugereranyije na icyiciro ruherereyemo .
Ku wa Mbere wa iki cyumweru , iki kigo gikorera muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , cyahaye BRD inota rya B + bitewe na uburyo iyi banki ifite ubushobozi bwo kuba itahungabana biturutse ku nguzanyo yatanze no kuba ari banki ifite ibigo cyangwa ibigega biyishyigikiye cyangwa se nayo ubwayo ifite imikorere ihamye .
Iri nota ryahawe BRD rigaragaza intambwe iyi banki imaze gutera , uburyo imaze kwaguka ndetse na intumbero yayo mu kuba banki ihagaze neza mu mutungo .
BRD itangaza ko rizagira uruhare rukomeye mu kuyifasha kureshya abandi bafatanyabikorwa mu rwego rwa imari ku buryo byagira uruhare mu iterambere rya u Rwanda .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa BRD , Kampeta Sayinzoga , yavuze ko kuba iyi banki yahawe iri nota bizayifasha kugera ku ntego yayo yo guhindura imibereho ya Abanyarwanda .
Ati " Twavuye kure kandi dutewe imbaraga na iri gereranya rije mu bihe bikomeye .
Rishingiye ku bufasha bukomeye BRD yahawe na abafatanyabikorwa bayo mu kuyihindura banki ihamye .
Abakozi ba BRD bari gukora ubutaruhuka kugira ngo bagere ku byo abafatanyabikorwa bayo bayitezeho no gukoresha neza igishoro .
BRD ni banki ya leta yashinzwe muri Kanama 1967 nubwo yahawe ibyangombwa bitangwa na Banki Nkuru ya u Rwanda muri Kanama 2009 .
Ifite imari shingiro igera kuri miliyari 7 .
Ifitwemo imigabane na inzego zitandukanye zirimo Guverinoma ya u Rwanda ifite 97 % binyuze mu Kigega Agaciro Development Fund gifitemo imigabane ingana na 55 % na Ikigo cya Igihugu cya Ubwiteganyirize , RSSB , gifitemo imigabane ingana na 42 % .
Iri mu rugendo rwo gufasha u Rwanda muri Gahunda ya Igihugu yo kwihutisha Iterambere ( NST1 ) ndetse no gushyira mu bikorwa Intego za iterambere rirambye .
Imikorere yayo yagiye ihinduka mu myaka ishize ibasha gukuraho ibihombo yakunze kugira aho byagabanutse ku kigero cya 77 % mu 2019 ugereranyije na imyaka ibiri yari yarabanje .
Ibi byaturutse mu kuvugurura uburyo inguzanyo zatangwagamo .
Yanogeje kandi uburyo bwo gukurikirana abakiliya bayo byanayifashije mu kugabanya inguzanyo zitishyurwa aho zavuye kuri 19 .
34 % mu 2018 zigera kuri 7 .
52 % mu mpera za 2019 .
BPR Plc yatanze miliyoni 100 Frw zo gufasha abagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus
Banki ya Abaturage ya u Rwanda ( BPR Plc .
yatanze miliyoni 100 Frw zo gufasha abaturage bahungabanyijwe na ingamba zafashwe zo gukumira icyorezo cya Coronavirus , inorohereza abakiliya bayo barimo na abagizweho ingaruka .
Banki ya Abaturage ya u Rwanda ( BPR Plc .
yatanze miliyoni 100 Frw zo gufasha abaturage bahungabanyijwe na ingamba zafashwe zo gukumira icyorezo cya Coronavirus , inorohereza abakiliya bayo barimo na abagizweho ingaruka .
Amezi abiri agiye gushira u Rwanda rufashe ingamba zidasanzwe zigamije gukumira icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Nubwo ingamba zorohejwe , hari imwe mu miryango yagizweho ingaruka kuko hari ibikorwa byahagaritswe ku buryo imibereho ya bamwe yahindutse .
Ubuyobozi bwa BPR bwatangaje ko buzi neza ingaruka imiryango imwe na imwe yagiye ihura nazo kubera ingamba zo guhashya Coronavirus , ariyo mpamvu biyemeje gutanga inkunga yabo ya miliyoni 100 Frw .
Itangazo iyo banki yashyize hanze rigira riti " COVID - 19 na ingaruka zayo ku bantu no ku bucuruzi zaratunguranye .
Banki izirikana ko hari bamwe mu banyamuryango bacu bahuye na ingorane mu mibereho yabo ya buri munsi .
" Tunejejwe no gutangaza ko nka umuryango mugari wa BPR twahaye Guverinoma ya u Rwanda umusanzu wa miliyoni 100 Frw , mu buryo bwo kunganira Leta muri gahunda irimo zo gufasha abagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus .
BPR yatangaje ko uretse gufasha abatishoboye , hanafashwe izindi ngamba zigamije gufasha abakiliya bayo bagizweho ingaruka na COVID - 19 .
Zimwe mu ngamba zafashwe harimo gushyiraho uburyo bwa ikoranabuhanga bufasha abakiliya gukoresha konti zabo bitabaye ngombwa ko bajya gutonda imirongo ku mashami ya banki , bikaba byakongera ibyago byo kwandura Coronavirus .
Iyi banki yasabye abakiliya gukomeza gukoresha ubwo buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga burimo telefoni igendanwa bakanze * 150 # , gukoresha application ya banki na serivizi zayo ziboneka hakoreshejwe internet .
BPR ikomeza ivuga ko guhererekanya amafaranga bikozwe muri ubwo buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga nta kiguzi umukiliya acibwa , bikazamara amezi atatu .
Abakiliya bashobora no kugana abahagarariye iyi banki ( agents ) bari hirya no hino mu gihugu begereye aho batuye , bagahabwa serivisi za banki
BPR Plc ivuga ko abakiliya bari basanzwe bayifitemo inguzanyo bemerewe igihe kiri hagati ya amezi atatu na atandatu batishyura bitewe na imbogamiziri buri mukiliya yagiye ahura nazo .
Abakiliya ba BPR imishahara yabo yakoreshejwe mu gufasha Abanyarwanda guhangana na Coronavirus , bemerewe gusaba inguzanyo ingana na umushahara wabo wa ukwezi batabonye , ikazatangira kwishyurwa nyuma ya ukwezi kandi bemererwa kuba bayishyura mu gihe cya amezi 12 .
BPR kandi ivuga ko abigomwe umushahara batazabasha kwishyura inguzanyo bari basanzwe bishyura , bazahabwa igihe cya ukwezi batishyura kuko bizwi ko batazahembwa .
Iyi nguzanyo [ personal loan ] yishyurwa kugera ku mezi 12 bitewe na ubushake bwa umukiliya .
BPR isobanura ko iyi nguzanyo nshya umukiliya aba ahawe ayishyura ku nyungu ingana na iyo yari asanzwe yishyuriraho inguzanyo yari afite .
Abaye adafite inguzanyo ahabwa ku nyungu isanzwe ya banki .
BPR yanatekereje ku bakozi bakorera ibigo ariko ibikorwa byabo bikaba byarahagaze bityo bikaba bitazabasha kubahemba kandi bari basanzwe bafite inguzanyo .
Aba bemerewe kutishyura inguzanyo mu mezi atatu mu gihe ibyo bigo bikisuganya ngo byongere gutangira ibikorwa bibahembe .
Ibisabwa ku batanze umushahara wa ukwezi kwa kane bifuza inguzanyo ni ukwandikira BPR Plc kuri email [ email protected ] ukavuga amazina na ibyo usaba .
Ku bakorera ibigo bifite ikibazo cyo kubahemba muri iki gihe bakwandika basaba guhabwa amezi yo gusubika kwishyura inguzanyo .
Umukoresha na we ashobora kwandikira BPR Plc asaba ko ifasha abakozi be batazabasha kwishyura inguzanyo kuko atazabahemba .
Aba banyuza ubusabe bwabo kuri email [ email protected ] , bagasaba kwemererwa kutishyura inguzanyo mu gihe cya amezi atatu .
Ku bakeneye ibindi bisobanuro kuri izi ngamba banki yashizeho zo gufasha abakiliya muri iki gihe cya Covid - 19 cyangwa ikindi kibazo kuri serivisi za banki , bashobora guhamagara umurongo wa banki ku 1500 .
Miliyari hafi 900 Frw zizakenerwa mu kuzahura ubukungu bwa u Rwanda nyuma ya Coronavirus
Gahunda yo kuzahura ubukungu nyuma ya icyorezo cya Coronavirus igaragaza ko u Rwanda rushobora kuzakoresha agera muri miliyari 882 Frw mu myaka ibiri ya ingengo ya imari , ni ukuvuga uyu turimo wa 2019 / 20 na utaha wa 2020 / 21 uzatangira muri Nyakanga .
Gahunda yo kuzahura ubukungu nyuma ya icyorezo cya Coronavirus igaragaza ko u Rwanda rushobora kuzakoresha agera muri miliyari 882 Frw mu myaka ibiri ya ingengo ya imari , ni ukuvuga uyu turimo wa 2019 / 20 na utaha wa 2020 / 21 uzatangira muri Nyakanga .
Icyorezo cya Coronavirus cyatumye ibikorwa byinshi bifungwa , ndetse na ubwo Guverinoma iheruka gufata umwanzuro ko bimwe bifungurwa nyuma ya iminsi isaga 40 , byasabwe gukoresha abakozi bake , kandi bigafungura hagati ya saa kumi na imwe za mu gitondo na saa mbili za ijoro .
Minisiteri ya Imari na Igenamigambi yakoze gahunda igamije kuzahura ubukungu bwa u Rwanda , zirimo gushyigikira ibikorwa bya ubuvuzi , kwita ku batishoboye , gutera inkunga ibigo bya leta , inkunga ya leta mu kigega cyo kuzahura ubukungu na izindi ngamba zigamije guhangana na ingaruka za Coronavirus .
Bumwe mu buryo burimo kwifashisha mu korohereza ibigo byagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus , harimo uburyo bwo kuvanaho imwe mu misoro , aho kubara avansi ya umusoro ku nyungu za ibigo na iz abantu ku giti cyabo , bizashingira ku byacurujwe uyu mwaka .
Ibinyabiziga bikora imirimo ibyara inyungu nabyo bizishyura avansi ya umusoro ku nyungu hashingiwe ku mubare wa amezi ya umwaka bizaba byarakozemo iyo mirimo ibyara inyungu , ndetse udupfukamunwa dukorerwa mu Rwanda natwo twasonewe umusoro ku nyungu , mu rwego rwo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Coronavirus .
Imisoro yinjira izagabanukaho arenga miliyari 200 Frw
Komiseri mu Kigo cya Imisoro na amahoro , ushinzwe Imisoro ya Imbere mu gihugu , Kayigi Aimable , yabwiye itangazamakuru ko ibibazo na ingamba bijyanye na Coronavirus bizagabanya ingano ya umusoro winjiraga mu gihugu uhereye hagati ya Werurwe ubwo u Rwanda rwafungaga ibikorwa kugeza muri uku kwezi kwa Gicurasi ubwo bimwe muri byo bitangiye gufungurwa .
Yakomeje ati " Mu mibare twari dufite , twabonaga ingaruka bishobora kuzagira ku mafaranga leta yinjizaga , bishobora kugera nko kuri miliyari nka 234 Frw ku bijyanye na umusoro .
Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Minisiteri ya Imari na Igenamigambi Ushinzwe Imari ya Leta , Richard Tusabe , avuga ko Leta yiyemeje guhara uyu musoro mu kwifatanya na Abanyarwanda bafite ibikorwa byahungabanye kubera COVID - 19 mu bijyanye na ubukungu na imibereho ya abaturage .
Ati " Sinavuga ngo tugarukiye aha , turakomeza dusuzume , nibigenda neza vuba turasubira mu buzima busanzwe , nibitagenda neza vuba nabyo turakomeza dufatanye kwiga ingamba zashyirwaho , zose zigamije kubungabunga ubuzima bwa umunyarwanda .
Hagiye gushingwa ikigega cya miliyari 100 Frw
Minisitiri wa Imari na Igenamigambi , Dr Ndagijimana Uzziel , aheruka kuvuga ko mu ngamba zigamije kuzahura ubukungu , u Rwanda rwashyize ingufu mu buhinzi , hategurwa ibihembwe bya ihinga biri imbere , ku buryo abahinzi bahabwa amafumbire na imbuto kugira ngo hazaboneke umusaruro mwiza , bityo igihugu gikomeze kwihaza mu biribwa kinasagurira amasoko .
Ikindi ni ukwihutisha imishinga yari yaratangiye itanga akazi , cyane iya ibikorwa remezo , nka inyubako na ibindi .
Ati " Hari imishinga ya imihanda , iya amazi , iya amashanyarazi , kugira ngo amafaranga agere ku bantu " " " " .
Hari kandi gukomeza gushyira ingufu muri gahunda zo gufasha abatishoboye yaba mu kubaha imirimo , kubaha inkunga ku badashobora gukora na inguzanyo iciriritse ishobora kwifashishwa mu gukora imirimo ibyara inyungu .
Indi gahunda yihariye igamije gufasha abashoramari na abikorera mu byiciro bitandukanye bagizweho ingaruka na iki cyorezo , aho leta yashyizeho gahunda yo gutangiza ikigega kibafasha kubona amafaranga yo gukoresha .
Ati " Ni ikigega cyafasha amabanki gutanga inguzanyo iciriritse yafasha ibyo byiciro byose kugira ngo bigaruke mu kazi byongere bikore , bibyare umusaruro uzagire ingaruka mu kuzamuka ka ubukungu muri rusange .
" Icyo kigega cyaranogejwe , harimo inkunga yihariye ku mahoteli kuko bigaragara ko ubukerarugendo bizamara igihe kugira ngo bwongere buzanzamuke kuko ntibiterwa na uko ibihe byifashe mu Rwanda ahubwo uko byifashe ku Isi hose .
Dr Ndagijimana yavuze muri icyo kigega hashyizwemo ingamba zihariye zifasha amahoteli kuvugurura amasezerano ya inguzanyo afite mu mabanki akaba igihe kirekire na inyungu zikagabanuka , ndetse ku buryo mu gihe yatangiye gufungura , abona amafaranga aciriritse kugira ngo imirimo yongere ikore .
Yavuze ko icyo kigega " kizafasha ubucuruzi ubwo aribwo bwose bwagizweho ingaruka , hari ibipimo bizagenderwaho kugira ngo ababirimo babone amafaranga aciriritse ku gihe cyiza noneho bongere bakore bihutishe imirimo " " " " .
Ibigo bito na ibiciriritse nabyo biri mu bizahabwa inguzanyo na ingwate kuko ingwate zikunze kuba ikibazo kuri bene ibyo byiciro .
Ni ikigega biteganyijwe ko gishobora kujyamo nka Miliyari 100 Frw avuye muri leta , ariko hagakomeza gushakwa na abandi bashyiramo amafaranga kugira ngo cyaguke .
Ati " Turateganya ko mu gihe cya icyumweru kimwe cyaba gitangiye " " " " .
Mu kugabanya icyuho kiri hagati ya ibyoherezwa mu mahanga na ibitumizwayo , u Rwanda rurateganya gukomeza guteza imbere ibikorerwa mu Rwanda , abanyarwanda bagakangukira kubigura kugira ngo bisimbure ibyo hanze .
U Rwanda rwahawe inguzanyo iciriritse ya miliyari 93 Frw yo gufasha urwego rwa ingufu
Guverinoma ya u Rwanda na Banki ya Isi byasinye amasezerano ya inkunga ya inyongera ya miliyoni 100 za amadolari , ni ukuvuga miliyari 93 .
1 Frw yo gushyigikira icyiciro cya gatatu cya umushinga wo guteza imbere urwego rwa amashanyarazi , Third Rwanda Energy Sector Development Policy Operation ( DPO ) .
Guverinoma ya u Rwanda na Banki ya Isi byasinye amasezerano ya inkunga ya inyongera ya miliyoni 100 za amadolari , ni ukuvuga miliyari 93 .
1 Frw yo gushyigikira icyiciro cya gatatu cya umushinga wo guteza imbere urwego rwa amashanyarazi , Third Rwanda Energy Sector Development Policy Operation ( DPO ) .
Iyi nkunga ni inguzanyo iciriritse izafasha Guverinoma ya u Rwanda kuvugurura ingengo ya imari hagamijwe kwitegura no guhangana na ingaruka zatewe na icyorezo cya Coronavirus mu rwego rwa ingufu .
Icyiciro cya gatatu cya umushinga wo guteza imbere urwego rwa amashanyarazi , ni icya nyuma mu mushinga mugari wagombaga gutwara miliyoni 375 za amadolari , inguzanyo ya mbere yo gutangiza uwo mushinga ikaba yaratanzwe mu Ukuboza 2017 , iya nyuma yatanzwe umwaka ushize .
Uwo mushinga ugomba kurangirana na 2020 , ugamije gufasha mu iterambere rya urwego rwa amashanyarazi mu Rwanda nkuko biri muri gahunda ya Igihugu ya Iterambere , NST1 , mu ntego yo kugeza amashanyarazi kuri bose bitarenze mu 2024 .
Minisitiri wa Imari na Igenamigambi , Dr .
Uzziel Ndagijimana , yavuze ko inkunga bahawe izafasha mu guharanira ko serivisi za amashanyarazi zikomeza gutangwa nta kirogoya .
Yagize ati " Nubwo ingaruka za COVID - 19 byitezwe ko zizarangira , urwego rwa ingufu byitezwe ko ruzahura na ibibazo nyamara gukomeza gutanga serivisi za amashanyarazi birakenewe cyane kugira ngo serivisi rusange zikomeze , bigabanye icyuho mu isubira inyuma rya ubukungu kandi abatishoboye bakomeze kwatabwaho .
Umuyobozi wa Banki ya Isi , Ishami rya u Rwanda , Yasser El Gammal , yavuze ko yizeye ko inkunga yatanzwe izafasha u Rwanda gusubira vuba mu murongo wa iterambere rya ubukungu .
Ati " Nizeye ko kubera ubuyobozi bwiza , ukwihangana kwa Abanyarwanda , ingamba zafashwe na Guverinoma , inkunga ya Banki ya Isi na abandi bafatanyabikorwa mu iterambere izafasha u Rwanda kwigobotora iki cyorezo rusubire mu nzira nziza .
Mu mpera za uyu mushinga mu Ukuboza 2020 byitezwe ko ingo 61 % mu Rwanda zizaba zigerwaho na amashanyarazi , bitange icyizere ku kugera ku 100 % mu mwaka wa 2024 .
Uyu mushinga kandi kunoza imicungire ya amashanyarazi hagabanywa ingano itakara , kugabanya igiciro no kongera umusaruro wa ikigo kiyacuruza na ibindi .
Imikorere ya ikigega kigamije kuzahura ubukungu bwa u Rwanda bwazahajwe na Coronavirus
Banki Nkuru ya u Rwanda , BNR , yashyizeho umurongo na uburyo ikigega cyo kuzahura ubukungu bwa u Rwanda kizakora .
Ni ikigega gifite hafi miliyoni 200 za amadorali , ni ukuvuga hafi miliyari 186 za amanyarwanda .
Banki Nkuru ya u Rwanda , BNR , yashyizeho umurongo na uburyo ikigega cyo kuzahura ubukungu bwa u Rwanda kizakora .
Ni ikigega gifite hafi miliyoni 200 za amadorali , ni ukuvuga hafi miliyari 186 za amanyarwanda .
Iki kigega kigamije gutera inkunga ibikorwa bya abikorera byahungabanyijwe na icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Minisitiri wa Imari na Igenamigambi , Dr Uzziel Ndagijimana , aherutse gutangaza ko ari ikigega kizafasha amabanki gutanga inguzanyo iciriritse ibyo byiciro byose kugira ngo bigaruke mu kazi byongere bikore , bibyare umusaruro uzagire ingaruka mu kuzamuka ka ubukungu muri rusange .
Muri iki kigega hashyizwemo ingamba zihariye zifasha amahoteli kuvugurura amasezerano ya inguzanyo afite mu mabanki akaba igihe kirekire na inyungu zikagabanuka , ndetse ku buryo mu gihe yatangiye gufungura , abona amafaranga aciriritse kugira ngo imirimo yongere ikore .
Imikorere ya iki kigega ireba amabanki 16 ya ubucuruzi na ibigo bya imari biciriritse .
Banki Nkuru ya Igihugu niyo izagicunga , gusa amafaranga ku bakiliya azajya atangwa na amabanki .
Ku ikubitiro leta yemeye gushyiramo miliyari 100 Frw ariko hagakomeza gushakwa abandi bashyiramo amafaranga kugira ngo cyaguke .
Usibye ku mahoteli , kizafasha mu gutanga igishoro ku bucuruzi bwagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus kugira ngo bukomeze gukora no kudahagarika abakozi , hari kandi inguzanyo ku bucuruzi buto na ubuciriritse nabwo bwibasiwe na COVID - 19 .
Banki Nkuru ya Igihugu izacunga imikorere yacyo , izaguriza amabanki kugira ngo nayo agurize abakiliya bayakeneye .
Gusaba inguzanyo bizakorwa binyuze muri banki zibishinzwe , nazo zizajya zikurikirana ikibazo , nyuma zohereza kuri BNR ibyifuzo bya abasabye gufashwa kugira ngo bisuzumwe biganishe no ku cyemezo cya nyuma .
Nyuma yo kwemezwa , amabanki azatanga amafaranga kuri konte ya uwayasabye hanyuma ibyakozwe bigaragarizwe BNR ari nayo izatuma amafaranga agera kuwasabye .
Umuyobozi wa Urugaga rwa Abikorera mu Rwanda , Robert Bapfakurera , aherutse kuvuga ati " nka ubukerarugendo , amahoteli , byagize ibibazo bikomeye kuko barafunze burundu , nubwo [ mu Rwanda ] ibibazo [ bya coronavirus ] byarangira ntabwo ibibazo bizaba byarangiye ahandi hose kuko ubukerarugendo bukorana na amahanga , bakeneye gufashwa cyane .
Raporo ya Ishami rya Ubukerarugendo mu Rugaga rwa Abikorera , PSF , yagaragazaga ko muri Werurwe bwagize igihombo cya miliyari 34 .
9 Frw , bivuye ku nama zasubitswe na ibindi bikorwa bya ubukerarugendo byahagaritswe .
Ibi bihombo byaje bisanga urwego rwa ubukerarugendo mu Rwanda rufite inguzanyo za miliyari 87 .
Imibare ya Banki ya Isi yo kuwa 9 Mata igaragaza ko ubukungu bwo muri Afurika yo munsi ya Ubutayu bwa Sahara , bwagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus ndetse ko buzamanuka ku kigero cya - 2 .
1 % buvuye kuri 2 .
4 % bwariho mu 2019 .
Ikigega Mpuzamahanga cya Imari ku Isi , IMF , nacyo giherutse gutanga ikigereranyo ko umusaruro mbumbe wa Isi muri uyu mwaka uzamanuka ku mpuzandengo ya - 3 % naho uwa ubukungu bwa ibihugu byateye imbere kurusha ibindi bumanuke ku kigero cya - 6 % .
Minisitiri wa Imari na Igenamigambi , Dr Ndagijimana Uzziel , ati " Ni ibintu bikomeye bidaheruka mu mateka ya Isi .
Muri Afurika yo munsi ya Ubutayu bwa Sahara , hateganyijwe ko ubukungu buzamanuka - 1 .
6 % [ … ] natwe rero birumvikana ko ubukungu bwacu butazagenda uko busanzwe buteganyijwe .
Minisitiri Dr Ndagijimana yavuze ko ubu igipimo cya ubukungu bwa u Rwanda kigaragaza ko butazazamuka ku kigero cya 8 % nka uko byari byitezwe , aho ubu imibare yagiye ivugururwa ikava kuri 5 .
1 % , nyuma biramanuka bigera kuri 3 .
5 % " ubu turi hafi kuri 2 % nubwo bitari byarangira neza " " " " .
Indi nkuru wasoma : Ikigega cya Miliyari 100 Frw , imwe mu ngamba zigiye kwifashishwa mu kuzahura ubukungu bwa u Rwanda
Ishoramari mvamahanga ku Isi yose rizagabanukaho 40 % mu 2020
Raporo ya Inama ya Loni ishinzwe ubucuruzi na iterambere ( UNCTAD ) , yagaragaje ko ishoramari mvamahanga ( FDI , Foreign Direct Investment ) , rizagabanukaho 40 % muri uyu mwaka ku isi yose kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Raporo ya Inama ya Loni ishinzwe ubucuruzi na iterambere ( UNCTAD ) , yagaragaje ko ishoramari mvamahanga ( FDI , Foreign Direct Investment ) , rizagabanukaho 40 % muri uyu mwaka ku isi yose kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Iyi raporo yatangajwe kuri uyu wa Kabiri , yerekana ko ishoramari mvamahanga rizagabanuka rikava kuri miliyari 1540 za amadolari ryariho mu 2019 rikagera munsi ya miliyari 1000 za amadolari , bikaba ari ubwa mbere kuva mu 2005 .
Ishoramari mvamahanga byitezwe ko rizagabanuka hagati ya 5 - 10 % mu mwaka utaha hanyuma ryongere kuzamuka mu 2022 .
Umunyamabanga Mukuru wa UNCTAD , Mukhisa Kituyi , yabwiye itangazamakuru ati " Ubukungu bwa Isi yose buri ahantu habi harenze uko byagenze mu 2008 , ubwo habagaho ibibazo bya ubukungu " " " " .
Yavuze ko icyorezo cya Coronavirus cyagize ingaruka mu byo abantu bashyira ku isoko , ibyo abaguzi bakenera ndetse no kuri gahunda za ishoramari mvamahanga .
Ibihugu bikennye bizagirwaho ingaruka cyane na igabanuka rya ishoramari mvamahanga .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe ishoramari muri UNCTAD , James Zhan , yagize ati " Ubukungu buri mu nzira ya amajyambere byitezwe ko buzasubira hasi mu bijyanye na ishoramari mvamahanga kubera ko buryishingikiriza mu musaruro ndetse no mu byo rikenera " " " " .
RwandAir yatangiye gutwara amafi yo muri Tanzania iyageza mu Burayi
Sosiyete ya RwandAir yatangaje ko indege zayo zatangiye gutwara amafi aturutse i Mwanza muri Tanzania ziyajyanye i Bruxelles mu Bubiligi .
Sosiyete ya RwandAir yatangaje ko indege zayo zatangiye gutwara amafi aturutse i Mwanza muri Tanzania ziyajyanye i Bruxelles mu Bubiligi .
Intego ya izo ngendo ni ukugeza ayo mafi ku isoko ryo mu Burayi nka uko biri mu itangazo RwandAir yashyize kuri Twitter .
Today we inaugurated our cargo flight from Mwanza to Brussels which will be transporting fish to Europe .
For more information about our cargo operations please contact [ email protected ] pic .
com / 2iY23zuePp
— RwandAir ( @ FlyRwandAir ) May 12 , 2020
Umwaka ushize muri Werurwe nibwo u Rwanda na Tanzania byemeranyije ubufatanye mu kugeza ibicuruzwa ku masoko akomeye , arimo ayo muri Tanzania ndetse no ku mugabane wa u Burayi .
Ibihugu byombi byemeranyije ishyirwaho rya ndege za imizigo zizajya ziva ku kibuga cya Indege cya Mwanza zijya ku masoko ya i Burayi , bikaba byaragombaga gutangira kuwa 1 Nyakanga 2019 .
Gutwara amafi yo muri Tanzania akagezwa mu Burayi , ni amahirwe ku barobyi na abacuruzi ba amafi bo muri icyo gihugu bari bamaze igihe bifuza uburyo buborohereye bwo kugeza umusaruro wabo ku masoko yo mu mahanga , bakagorwa na igiciro cya urugendo .
Ubusanzwe abacuruzi ba amafi bajyaga babanza kugeza umusaruro wabo ku bibuga bya indege bya Entebbe muri Uganda na Nairobi muri Kenya , kugira ngo indege ziwugeze ku masoko yo hanze , ibintu bavuga ko byabahendaga .
Ihuriro rya abarobyi muri Tanzania ritangaza ko hari umusaruro wa amafi wangirikaga kubera kubura uko bawugeza ku isoko mpuzamahanga .
Nko muri Werurwe umwaka ushize , hari umusaruro wa amafi ufite agaciro gasaga miliyari eshanu za amashilingi ya Tanzania bagombaga kugeza ku masoko ya Israel no mu Buyapani , babuze uko bagezayo kubera guhenda ka urugendo .
Uko umusaruro mbumbe wa u Rwanda wiyongereyeho miliyari zirenga 3000Frw mu myaka itanu
Nubwo u Rwanda kimwe na Isi yose bihanganye na icyorezo cya Coronavirus , mbere yacyo ubukungu bwarwo bwakomeje kwiyongera mu nkingi zose bwubakiyeho , aho ubuhinzi , inganda , serivisi na ibindi bitahwemye kuzamuka umwaka ku wundi kandi uruhare rwabyo mu musaruro mbumbe wa igihugu rukigaragaza .
Nubwo u Rwanda kimwe na Isi yose bihanganye na icyorezo cya Coronavirus , mbere yacyo ubukungu bwarwo bwakomeje kwiyongera mu nkingi zose bwubakiyeho , aho ubuhinzi , inganda , serivisi na ibindi bitahwemye kuzamuka umwaka ku wundi kandi uruhare rwabyo mu musaruro mbumbe wa igihugu rukigaragaza .
Imibare Ikigo cya Igihugu cya Ibarurishamibare ( NISR ) , cyatangaje kuwa 24 Werurwe 2020 , igaragaza ko mu 2019 , umusaruro mbumbe wa u Rwanda ( GDP ) , wiyongereye ku rugero rwa 9 .
4 % , ugera kuri miliyari 9105 Frw uvuye kuri miliyari 8189 Frw wariho mu 2018 .
Muri uyu musaruro mbumbe , ubuhinzi bwagize uruhare rwa 24 % inganda zigira uruhare rwa 18 % , Serivisi zingana 49 % mu gihe ibindi bisigaye byagize uruhare ku kigero cya 9 % .
Iri zamuka rya ubukungu riratanga icyizere ko nta gihindutse ibyo u Rwanda ruteganya ko nibura mu 2035 ruzaba rufite ubukungu buciriritse bishoboka .
Icyo gihe birasaba ko ubukungu bwaba bwihuta ku 10 % , bigatuma umunyarwanda yazaba yinjiza asaga miliyoni 10 Frw ku mwaka .
Rirashimangira kandi imbaraga leta ya u Rwanda ikomeje gushyira mu guteza imbere ubukungu .
Mu 1994 , izamuka rya ubukungu bwa u Rwanda , ryasubiye inyuma kuri - 41 .
9 % , umusaruro mbumbe wa umuturage wari amadolari 146 ku mwaka .
Nubwo inzira ikiri ndende , aho iterambere rya ubukungu bwa u Rwanda rigeze harivugira kuko nko mu myaka itanu ishize umusaruro mbumbe wavuye kuri miliyari miliyari 5 956 Frw mu 2015 , ugera kuri miliyari 9105 Frw .
Usubije amaso inyuma , usanga umusaruro mbumbe wa u Rwanda mu myaka itanu ishize ( 2015 - 2019 ) , wariyongereyeho miliyari 3149 Frw .
Iri zamuka rishingiye ahanini kuri gahunda yo guteza imbere ubuhinzi , ishoramari muri serivisi zitandukanye , ubucuruzi , inganda na ibindi bicumbi bya ubukungu .
Izamuka rya umusaruro mbumbe mu myaka itanu
Mu 2015 umusaruro mbumbe wa u Rwanda wazamutseho 6 .
9 % , aho wanganaga na miliyari 5 956 Frw zikaba zari zivuye kuri miliyari 4 915Frw mu 2014 .
Mu 2016 umusaruro mbumbe wageze kuri miliyari 6 , 618 Frw , aho wazamutse ku kigero cya 5 .
9 % ugereranyije na umwaka wabanje .
Mu 2017 umusaruro mbumbe wageze kuri miliyari 7 597 ukaba warazamutse 6 .
1 % , mu 2018 wageze kuri miliyari 8189 Frw uzamutse ku kigero cya 8 .
6 % ugereranyije na umwaka wabanje wa 2017 .
Ubwo hatangazwa umusaruro mbumbe wa 2018 , Minisitiri wa Imari na Igenamigambi , Dr Uzziel Ndagijimana , yavuze ko iterambere rya ubuhinzi , inganda , ibikorerwa mu Rwanda na serivisi byazamuye ubukungu cyane .
Yagize ati " Ngira ngo muzi gahunda ya Made in Rwanda no korohereza ibikorwa bikorerwa mu Rwanda , biragenda rero bitanga umusaruro , umusaruro wa inganda urazamuka cyane " " " " .
Minisitiri Ndagijimana yavuze ko mu bitanga umusaruro harimo ibikorwa bya ubwubatsi byaba imihanda na inganda .
Icyo gihe ibikorwa bya ubwubatsi byazamutseho 20 % , mu nganda zitunganya ibintu bitandukanye cyazamutseho kuri 13 % , umusaruro wa inganda zitunganya ibiryo ni 10 % , izitunganya imyenda ni 26 % na 38 % ku musaruro wa inganda zikora ibikoresho bikoze mu byuma .
Mu 2019 , umusaruro mbumbe wageze kuri miliyari 9105 Frw uvuye kuri miliyari 8189 Frw wariho mu 2018 .
Bisobanuye ko hiyongereyeho miliyoni 916Frw mu mwaka umwe .
Urwego rwa serivisi rwashinze imizi
Mu 2015 , urwego rwa serivisi rwazamutse ku kigero cya 7 % rugira uruhare mu musaruro mbumbe wose rwa 47 % .
Mu 2016 serivisi zazamutse ku kigero cya 6 % .
Muri uwo mwaka serivisi zishingiye kuri hoteli na restaurant zazamutse ku rugero rwa 11 % bitewe na gahunda yo kwakira inama na ibikorwa bitandukanye .
Imirimo ya ubwikorezi yazamutse ku rugero rwa 8 % ahanini bitewe na ubwikorezi bwo mu kirere bwazamutse ku rugero rwa 15 % .
Mu 2017 , serivisi zazamutse ku kigero cya 8 % naho uruhare rwazo mu musaruro mbumbe rugera kuri 46 % .
Mu 2018 umusaruro wa serivisi wazamutse ku rugero rwa 9 % naho mu 2019 uzamuka ku rugero rwa 8 % ndetse zigira uruhare rwa 49 % muri GDP .
Mu 2016 , uwari Minisitiri wa imari na igenamigambi , Claver Gatete yavuze ko gahunda ya leta ijyanye no kwakira inama mpuzamahanga yagize uruhare runini mu kuzamura umusaruro mbumbe wa igihugu nka aho ibijyanye na hotel na restaurant zabigizemo uruhare runini .
Guhera muri Nyakanga 2018 kugeza Gashyantare 2019 , u Rwanda rwari rumaze kwinjiza miliyoni 52 za amadolari ( asaga miliyari 46 Frw ) avuye mu gutegura no kwakira inama mpuzamahanga .
Mu mwaka wa ingengo ya imari ushize ( 2018 / 2019 ) igihugu cyari cyihaye intego yo kwinjiza miliyoni 74 za amadolari mu bikorwa byo gutegura no kwakira inama mpuzamahanga , avuye kuri miliyoni 42 zinjijwe mu 2017 .
Kugeza ubu muri Kigali hari ibyumba bya hoteli za inyenyeri ebyiri kugeza kuri eshanu bisaga 5000 , washyiramo ibindi byumba bya inzu zigezweho zishobora gucumbikira abantu Kigali ifite bikagera ku 10 000 .
Ubucuruzi budandaza na ubugurisha ibintu icyarimwe bwa ibyakorewe mu Rwanda bukomeje kongera umusaruro wa serivisi , aho mu 2019 bwiyongereye ku kigero cya 16 % .
Ubwikorezi bwazamutse ku kigero cya 12 % ahanini bitewe na ubwikorezi bwo mu kirere bwazamutse ku kigero cya 17 % .
Serivisi za imari zazamutse ku kigero cya 8 % naho serivisi za hoteli na za restaurant zizamuka ku gipimo cya 10 % .
Inganda zifatiye runini ubukungu
Kuva mu 2015 , urwego rwa inganda rwagize ingufu nyinshi cyane mu bukungu bwa igihugu kuko ari bwo gahunda ya Made in Rwanda , yatangiraga gushyirwa mu bikorwa mu buryo buhamye .
Icyo gihe umusaruro wa inganda wazamutse ku kigero cya 7 % .
Muri buri turere kandi hashyizweho ibyanya byihariye bya inganda , ndetse no mu Mujyi wa Kigali , iki cyanya gishyirwa i Masoro mu Karere ka Gasabo .
Mu 2016 inganda zazamutse ku kigero cya 7 % , gahunda ya Made in Rwanda igira uruhare rukomeye cyane kuko inganda zikora imyenda , inkweto na ibindi bituruka ku ruhu byiyongereye ku rugero rwa 10 % , izikora ibyo kurya ziyongera ku rugero rwa 8 % , naho inganda zikora ibikoresho bya ubwubatsi harimo isima ziyongeraho 21 % .
Mu 2017 inganda zazamutse ku kigero cya 4 % , mu 2018 zizamuka ku 10 % naho mu 2019 umusaruro uzamuka kuri 16 % .
Mu 2019 , izamuka rya umusaruro wa inganda ryatewe ahanini na ibikorwa bya ubwubatsi , inganda zitunganya ibintu bitandukanye na ubucukuzi bwa amabuye ya agaciro .
Kuri ubu mu Rwanda habarirwa inganda nto na iziciriritse zirenga 800 zirimo inganda zitari zisanzwe mu Rwanda nka izikora telefoni , iziteranya imodoka , izikora ibiribwa na izindi .
Ubuhinzi bukomeje gutera imbere
Imibare ya NISR , yerekana ko mu 2015 , ubuhinzi bwazamutseho 5 % , ndetse bugira uruhare rwa 33 % mu musaruro mbumbe .
Mu 2018 , umusaruro wa ubuhinzi wazamutse ku rugero rwa 6 % , mu 2019 , wazamutse ku kigero cya 5 % , naho umusaruro wabwo ugira uruhare rwa 24 % mu musaruro mbumbe .
Ubuhinzi nka kimwe mu bitunze abanyarwanda benshi , bwakunze guhura na imbogamizi zirimo kuba bushingiye ku mvura , yaboneka bukagenda neza yabura bukagenda nabi .
Ibi byatumye leta ishyira imbaraga muri gahunda yo kuhira aho kugeza ubu hegitari zirenga ibihumbi 68 zuhirwa .
Gukoresha inyongeramusaruro , guhuza ubutaka no guhinga igihingwa cyatoranyijwe byitaweho cyane .
Leta ya u Rwanda kandi yashyize imbere no gushyiraho inganda zongerera agaciro umusaruro ukomoka ku buhinzi na ubworozi .
Umuyobozi wa NISR , Yusuf Murangwa avuga ko uyu mwaka wagenze neza kuruta uko byari byitezwe .
Ati " Ubuhinzi nabwo ntabwo bwakoze nabi 5 % nubwo haba hifuzwa ko biba byiza kurushaho " " " " .
Mu 2019 , ibihingwa ngandurarugo byiyongereye ku kigero cya 4 % , ibihingwa byoherezwa mu mahanga byiyongera 5 % bitewe na ikawa yiyongereye ku kigero cya 7 % na icyayi cyiyongereye ku kigero cya 3 % .
Kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus , ubukungu ku Isi hose buzagabanuka , ubwa u Rwanda byitezwe ko buzazamuka ku gipimo cya 2 % mu mwaka wa 2020 buvuye kuri 9 .
4 % bwazamutseho umwaka ushize .
Icyakora kubera ingamba zafashwe mu kuzahura ubukungu , biteganyijwe ko ubukungu bwa u Rwanda mu mwaka wa 2021 buzazamuka ku gipimo cya 6 .
3 % na 8 % mu 2022 .
Amazon igiye kugura imigabane ya miliyari ebyiri za amadorali muri Airtel
Ikigo gikomeye mu bucuruzi bukorerwa ku Ikoranabuhanga cyo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , Amazon cyatangiye urugendo rukiganisha ku isoko ryagutse rya u Buhinde , kinyuze mu kugura imigabane ya Ikigo cya Itumanaho cya Bharti Airtel , kinafite ishami rikorera mu Rwanda .
Ikigo gikomeye mu bucuruzi bukorerwa ku Ikoranabuhanga cyo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , Amazon cyatangiye urugendo rukiganisha ku isoko ryagutse rya u Buhinde , kinyuze mu kugura imigabane ya Ikigo cya Itumanaho cya Bharti Airtel , kinafite ishami rikorera mu Rwanda .
Ibiganiro byo kugura imigabane ya Bharti Airtel ntibiragera kure , ariko abasesenguzi bavuga ko bigenze uko impande zombi zibyifuza , byazamura cyane ubukungu bwa ikoranabuhanga rya u Buhinde .
Biteganyijwe ko ubwumvikane bwa ibi bigo bushobora gutuma imigabane ingana na 5 % ya Bharti Airtel ijya mu maboko ya Amazon Inc .
hashingiwe ku buryo isoko rihagaze muri iyi minsi .
Bharti Airtel iri ku mwanya wa gatatu mu bigo bitanga serivisi za itumanaho mu Buhinde igaragaza guhangana gukomeye hagati yayo na ikigo cya mbere cya Reliance Jio .
Abantu batifuje ko imyirondoro yabo ijya ahagaragara babwiye Reuters ko uburyo Reliance Jio yakoresheje kugira ngo ibe iyoboye ibindi bigo bya itumanaho mu Buhinde na Bharti Airtel yabushobora .
Ku ikubitiro Amazon yari yifuje kugura imigabane iri hagati ya 8 - 10 % ya Bharti Airtel .
Gusa ngo kuko ibiganiro bikiri mu itangira [ … ] bishoboka ko na amasezerano yahinduka cyangwa agaseswa .
Amazon iteganya ko yahita ireba ubundi buryo bujyanye no guhererekanya amafaranga bwazajya bufasha abakiliya ba Bharti Airtel kubona ibicuruzwa byayo bibahendukiye .
Umuvugizi wa Amazon yanze kugira icyo avuga kuri aya makuru , kuko ikigo ahagarariye kitatangaza amakuru ajyanye na ibyo bazakora cyangwa batazakora mu gihe kiri imbere .
Gusa itangazo ryasohowe na Bharti Airtel rivuga ko isanzwe ikorana na ibigo bya ikoranabuhanga bitandukanye bishaka kugeza ibicuruzwa byabyo na serivisi bitanga ku bakiliya .
Imigabane ya Bharti Airtel ku isoko rya imari na imigabane , kuri uyu wa Kane , tariki ya 4 Kamena 2020 yazamutseho 6 % nyuma yo gutangazwa kwa amakuru ya ibiganiro hagati yayo na Amazon .
Mu byumweru bitandatu bishize ikigo cya Jio gihanganye na Bharti cyabonye miliyari 10 za amadorali kiyakuye mu bashoramari barimo na Facebook .
Alphabet Inc ya Google na yo iri gushaka uburyo bwo gushora imari muri Vodafone Idea ya kabiri mu Buhinde mu gutanga serivisi za itumanaho .
Amazon iri kwirukira ku isoko rya ikoranabuhanga mu Buhinde bitewe no kuba riri kwaguka cyane kuko umubare wa abatuye iki gihugu uri kwiyongera , ukaba ugeze kuri miliyari 1 , 3 .
Amazon iteganya gushora miliyari 6 , 5 za amadorali mu bikorwa byo gucururiza kuri internet , ndetse ngo ikaba izoroherwa no gukoresha internet ya Bharti ku giciro gito mu gihe ibigo byombi bizaba byemeranyije amasezerano byifuza .
Mu Ukuboza 2017 nibwo Bharti Airtel ibarizwamo Airtel Rwanda yaguze imigabane yose ya Sosiyete ya Itumanaho ya Tigo Rwanda ibarizwa muri Millicom International Cellular SA .
Amasezerano ya ubugure yasinyiwe i New Delhi mu Buhinde , yahaye Airtel Rwanda kwegukana 100 % bya imigabane yose ya Tigo Rwanda .
Bharti Airtel ni ikigo gikomeye ku Isi mu bijyanye na itumanaho gifite abakiliya barenga miliyoni 403 mu bihugu 18 bya Afurika na Aziya gikoreramo .
Icyayi cya u Rwanda cyinjije asaga miliyari 25 Frw mu mezi atatu ya 2020
Mu mezi atatu abanza ya 2020 , u Rwanda rwohereje mu mahanga icyayi kingana na toni 9 .
3 zifite agaciro ka amafaranga asaga miliyari 25 Frw , yiyongereye ku kigero cya 27 % ugereranyije na ayinjiye mu gihe nka iki mu mwaka wari wabanje , naho ingano ya ibyoherejwe yo yiyongera kuri 15 % .
Mu mezi atatu abanza ya 2020 , u Rwanda rwohereje mu mahanga icyayi kingana na toni 9 .
3 zifite agaciro ka amafaranga asaga miliyari 25 Frw , yiyongereye ku kigero cya 27 % ugereranyije na ayinjiye mu gihe nka iki mu mwaka wari wabanje , naho ingano ya ibyoherejwe yo yiyongera kuri 15 % .
Imibare itangazwa na Ikigo cya Igihugu gishinzwe guteza Imbere Ibyoherezwa mu Mahanga bikomoka ku Buhinzi , NAEB , igaragaza ko hagati ya Mutarama na Werurwe 2020 , icyayi cyoherejwe mu mahanga ari ibiro 9 .
436 bifite agaciro ka amadolari 27 .
861 ni ukuvuga asaga miliyari zisaga 25 .
Imibare yo mu 2019 igaragaza ko mu mezi atanu ya mbere ya uyu mwaka wa ingengo ya imari watangiye muri Nyakanga 2019 , inyungu yavuye mu buhinzi bwa icyayi yari yazamutseho 8 % igera kuri miliyoni $ 36 .
08 , ni ukuvuga asaga miliyari 33 .
Kuva muri Nyakanga kugeza mu Ugushyingo 2019 , umusaruro wa icyayi cya u Rwanda wazamutseho 12 % naho icyoherejwe mu mahanga cyiyongereyeho 4 % , ugereranyije na igihe nka icyo mu mwaka wa 2018 .
Hagati ya Nyakanga na Ugushyingo 2019 habonetse umusaruro wa toni 12 .
017 za icyayi , ziruta toni 10 .
769 zabonetse mu gihe nka icyo mu mwaka wa 2018 .
Icyo gihe byagaragazwaga kandi ko icyayi cya u Rwanda cyatunganyijwe cyiyongereyeho 4 % , kiva kuri toni 12 .
180 zabonetse mu 2018 zigera kuri toni 12 .
617 mu 2019 .
Mu gihe nka icyo kandi mu 2019 , icyayi cyoherejwe mu mahanga cyinjije $ 36 , 088 , 761 , bingana na izamuka rya 8 % , zivuye kuri $ 33 , 562 , 294 mu mwaka wabanje .
Imibare ya NAEB igaragaza ko intego ari uko mu mwaka wa 2024 , icyayi cya u Rwanda kizaba cyinjiriza igihugu miliyoni 209 za amadolari .
Minisitiri wa Imari na Igenamigambi , Dr Uzziel Ndagijimana , aherutse gutangaza ko kubera Coronavirus , muri iki gihe ibyoherezwa mu mahanga bishobora kuzagabanuka , ariko ko mu gihe iki cyorezo kizaba cyarangiye , ibintu bishobora kujya mu buryo .
Yavuze ko ku isoko muri iki gihe ibiciro bya ikawa bihagaze neza nubwo ubu atari igihe cya umusaruro , gusa ibya icyayi byo biri kugenda bigabanuka ku isoko .
Mu kugabanya icyuho kiri hagati ya ibyoherezwa mu mahanga na ibitumizwayo , u Rwanda rurateganya gukomeza guteza imbere ibikorerwa mu Rwanda , Abanyarwanda bagakangukira kubigura kugira ngo bisimbure ibyo hanze .
Minisitiri Dr Ndagijimana yavuze ko ubu igipimo cya ubukungu bwa u Rwanda kigaragaza ko butazazamuka ku kigero cya 8 % nka uko byari byitezwe , aho ubu imibare yagiye ivugururwa ikava kuri 5 .
1 % , nyuma biramanuka bigera kuri 3 .
5 % " ubu turi hafi kuri 2 % nubwo bitari byarangira neza " " " " .
Umwuka wa intambara ukomeje gututumba hagati ya Amerika na Iran
Nyuma ya igitero cyagabwe na Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika mu rukerera rwo kuri uyu wa Gatanu , kigahitana Gen Qasem Soleimani , wari usanzwe ayobora umutwe udasanzwe wa ingabo zirinda abategetsi bakomeye muri Iran ; impungenge na ubwoba bwa intambara bikomeje kwiyongera ku batari bake bakurikiranira hafi politiki ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , ndetse na abatuye mu burasirazuba bwo hagati .
Nyuma ya igitero cyagabwe na Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika mu rukerera rwo kuri uyu wa Gatanu , kigahitana Gen Qasem Soleimani , wari usanzwe ayobora umutwe udasanzwe wa ingabo zirinda abategetsi bakomeye muri Iran ; impungenge na ubwoba bwa intambara bikomeje kwiyongera ku batari bake bakurikiranira hafi politiki ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , ndetse na abatuye mu burasirazuba bwo hagati .
Iki gitero cyategetswe na Perezida wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , Donald Trump , cyanahitanye Abu Mahdi al - Muhandis , wari umuyobozi wungirije wa umutwe bivugwa ko ufashwa na Iran witwa ( Popular Mobilization Forces ) , ibiro bya ubutasi bya Amerika ( CIA ) byemeje ko ariwo wateguye ukanagaba igitero kuri Ambasade ya Amerika mu mujyi wa Bagdad mu minsi ishize .
Gen Qasem Soleimani na Abu Mahdi al - Muhandis barasiwe ku kibuga cya indege cya Iraq i Bagdad , bari mu modoka hamwe na abandi bantu batanu .
Umuyobozi wa ikirenga muri Iran , Ayatollah Ali Khamenei , wahise ategeka iminsi itatu ya icyunamo mu gihugu hose , yavuze ko hateganyijwe kwihorera gukomeye ku bishe Gen Qasem Soleimani .
Perezida wa Iran , Hassan Rouhani , na we yashimangiye ko igihugu cye kizakora ibishoboka byose kikihorera , aho yunganiwe na minisitiri wa ububanyi na amahanga muri Iran , Javad Zarif , wavuze ko igitero cya Amerika ari icya iterabwoba .
Ati " Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika zizirengera ingaruka za ubujiji bwazo .
Gen Qasem Soleimani yakundwaga kandi agafatwaga na abanya - Iran benshi nka umwe mu bantu bashobora kurinda ubusugire bwa igihugu cyabo .
Ubuhangange bwe kandi bwareberwaga mu ishusho ya uko yafatwaga nka nomero ya kabiri mu bafata ibyemezo muri Iran .
Abasesenguzi bavuga iki kuri uyu mwuka wa intambara ?
Abademokarate benshi bavuga ko icyemezo cya Trump gishobora gutuma intambara yeruye irota , kandi bakamunenga ko yagifashe atabanje kugisha inama Inteko Ishinga Amategeko .
Kuba Soleimani yari umwanzi wa Amerika hari abademokarate babyemeza ariko bakavuga ko kwica umuntu wa kabiri ukomeye muri Iran kandi bigakorwa nta bwumvikane na Inteko ishinga amategeko ari ikosa rishobora gushyira akarere kose Iran ihereremo mu ntambara .
Joe Biden wabaye Visi perezida wa Amerika ku ngoma ya Barrack Obama , we yeruye avuga ko Trump yakojeje agati mu ntozi .
Andrew Yang uteganya kwiyamamaza ku mwanya wa umukuru wa igihugu , ahagarariye ishyaka rya abademokarate yagize ati " Uko mbibona turashaka intambara na Iran ariko nsanga byaba byiza turebye kure tukirinda gushyira abaturage bacu batuye muri kariya karere mu kaga ko kwibasirwa na abanzi bacu .
Elizabeth Warren , na we wifuza kuzahagararira ishyaka rya abademokarate mu matora , yavuze ko icyemezo cya Trump kitarimo ubushishozi .
Ati " Soleimani yari umwicanyi , wahitanye ubuzima bwa abantu benshi barimo na amagana ya abanyamerika , ariko iki cyemezo kitarimo ubushishozi cyazamuye umwuka wa intambara hagati yacu na Iran , kandi gishobora gutuma hapfa abantu benshi mu karere ko mu burasirazuba bwo hagati Iran iherereyemo .
Icya ingenzi cyari gikwiye ni ukwirinda indi ntambara .
Minisitiri wa ububanyi na amahanga wa u Burusiya , busanzwe ari umuterankunga wa mbere wa Iran , yavuze ko igitero cya Amerika kirongera ibibazo mu burasirazuba bwo hagati .
Ku rundi ruhande ariko aba republicains bo bavuga ko kwica uwo mugabo byari amahitamo akwiye kuko yari afite amaraso ya abanyamerika mu biganza bye , kandi yari imbogamizi ikomeye ku mutekano wa abanyamerika babarizwa mu karere ko mu burasirazuba bwo hagati na inyungu zabo .
Lindsey Graham , umusenateri uhagarariye leta ya Carolina ya Epfo yagize ati " Wakoze bwana Perezida kubwo guhagararira Amerika .
Iki gikorwa cya Perezida Trump na ingabo zacu , ni igisubizo nyacyo ku bushotoranyi bwa Iran bwari burangajwe imbere na Gen Soleimani na abamushyigikiye .
Yongeyeho ati " Niba Iran ikomeje gutera Amerika na abadushyigikiye , bagomba kubyishyura ku kiguzi kinini , kirimo no gusenya amariba yabo ya peteroli .
Kuri leta ya Iran , niba mushaka kuguma mu bucuruzi bwa peteroli , mureke Amerika na abadushyigikiye , kandi muhagarike gutera inkunga imitwe ya iterabwoba hirya no hino ku isi .
Hari amakuru avuga ko iki gitero cyahitanye Gen Soleimani , ingabo za Israel zaba zakigizemo uruhare .
Nta muyobozi na umwe muri Israel wari wagira icyo avuga kuri iki gitero kuko abaminisitiri bose babujijwe kugira icyo babivugaho kuko bishobora gukururira akaga icyo gihugu .
Umutwe wa Hezbollah ubarizwa muri Liban , ukaba ushyigikiwe na Iran wahamagariye isi yose guhuriza hamwe bagahorera urupfu rwa Gen Soleimani .
Umuyobozi wa uyu mutwe , Sayyed Hassan Nasrallah , yagize ati " Intego ya Leta Zunze Ubummwe za Amerika mu karere ntikwiye kugerwaho binyuze mu cyaha gikomeye cyo kwicwa abajenerali .
Minisitiri wa intebe wa Israel wari mu ruzinduko mu Bugereki , yahise arusubika rutarangiye nyuma yo kumva urupfu rwa Gen Soleimani , mu gihe Naftali Bennett , wari wamusigariyeho yahise atumiza inama ya igitaraganya yigaga ku mutekano i Tel Aviv , ndetse na za ambasade na ibiro bihagarariye inyungu za ibindi bihugu bahabwa umuburo wo ku rwego rwo hejuru .
Minisitiri wa ububanyi na amahanga wa u Bufaransa , Amelie de Montchalin , yavuze ko igihugu cye kizakomeza gukora uko gishoboye mu guteza imbere ituze na umutekano mu karere ka uburasirazuba bwo hagati nyuma ya ibitero bya Amerika .
Ati " Ibiri kuba nibyo twatinyaga , umwuka mubi hagati ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika uri kwiyongera .
Mu minsi ishize Gen Soleimani yari yaravuze ijambo ryarakaje Amerika , aho yagize ati " Ndakubwiye wowe Trump umukinnyi wa urusimbi , ndakubwiye , umenye ko turi hafi yawe kuruta uko ubikeka .
Uzatangiza intambara , ariko nitwe dufite ubushobozi bwo kuzayisoza .
Ibibazo hagati ya leta ya Washington na Tehran byazamutse nyuma yuko Donald Trump akuye igihugu cye mu masezerano yo muri 2015 arebana no kubuza Iran gucura intwaro za kirimbuzi .
Aya masezerano yabuzaga Iran kwigwizaho ibitwaro bya kirimbuzi mu gihe cya imyaka 10 , yafatwaga na benshi nka intambwe ikomeye yatewe na Perezida Barack Obama muri politiki ya ububanyi na amahanga .
Kuva mu gitondo cyo kuri uyu wa Gatanu , abantu benshi biraye mu mihanda yo mu murwa mukuru Tehran , bigaragambya bamagana urupfu rwa Gen Soleimani .
Ikindi kibazo kimaze kwigaragaza , ni izamuka rikomeye rya igiciro cya ibikomoka kuri peteroli hirya no hino ku masoko mpuzamahanga , ibigaragaza ko nubwo intambara ya amasasu itaratangira mu buryo bweruye , ariko iya ubukungu yo yahise yaduka .
Ikindi kimenyetso cya umugambi wa Uganda mu gutera icyuhagiro RNC
Mu gihe umubano wa u Rwanda na Uganda utifashe neza , Uganda ikomeje ibikorwa byayo byo gushyigikira imitwe ibangamiye umutekano wa u Rwanda , aho ibinyamakuru bya Kampala bikomeje ubuvugizi ku mitwe ya iterabwoba irimo na RNC .
Mu gihe umubano wa u Rwanda na Uganda utifashe neza , Uganda ikomeje ibikorwa byayo byo gushyigikira imitwe ibangamiye umutekano wa u Rwanda , aho ibinyamakuru bya Kampala bikomeje ubuvugizi ku mitwe ya iterabwoba irimo na RNC .
Kimwe mu bikorwa bishya , ni ikinyamakuru Daily Monitor kuri uyu wa 2 Kanama cyateruye kivuganira abarwanashyaka ba RNC baba mu Bwongereza , ko bashaka gutaha iwabo nubwo bashinjwa ibyaha bikomeye bya iterabwoba , ariko iki kinyamakuru cyagaragaje ko uyu mutwe ugizwe na impirimbanyi za demokarasi zishaka impinduka .
Ni ibikorwa bidasiba kandi byiyongera ku kuba Perezida Yoweri Museveni aheruka kwiyemerera ko yahuye na umwe mu barwanashyaka ba RNC , Charlotte Mukankusi ushinzwe dipolomasi muri uwo mutwe .
Iyi mikoranire ya Uganda ishyigikiye abagamije guhungabanya umutekano wa u Rwanda yagarutsweho kenshi , ko Uganda yahaye rugari umutwe wa RNC ari naho ukorera ibikorwa byo gushaka abayoboke mu banyarwanda baba muri icyo gihugu , ku bufatanye na urwego rwa gisirikare rushinzwe ubutasi , CMI , abatemeranyije na uwo mugambi bagakorerwa iyicarubozo rikomeye .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Uganda , Maj Gen Frank Mugambage , yavuze ko RNC ari umutwe wa iterabwoba , ku buryo ibyo uvuga byose bidakwiye guhabwa agaciro .
Ni mu gihe abawugize bakabaye bakurikiranwa ku bikorwa uyu mutwe wakoze na indi migambi mibisha ufite ku Rwanda .
Mu banenze iyi mikorere yo gukeza RNC kandi harimo Yolande Makolo , wibajije niba ubu ari uburyo bushya Uganda izanye nyuma ya imigambi iheruka kuyipfubana yo gushyigikira umutwe witwaje intwaro wagabaga ibitero unyuze mu ishyamba rya Nyungwe .

Uganda ikomeje ibikorwa bibangamiye abanyarwanda , byanatumye u Rwanda rubuza abaturage barwo kujya muri icyo gihugu kubera iyicarubozo bakorerwayo , kugeza igihe ikibazo cya umutekano wabo kizakemukira .
Ku wa 22 CMI yataye muri yombi abakirisitu ba ADEPR Kibuye bagera kuri 40 mu murwa mukuru Kampala , ubu bafunzwe mu buryo butemewe na amategeko kuko bataragezwa imbere ya inkiko ngo bamenyeshe ibyo baregwa , banisobanure .
Ni abanyarwanda biyongera ku bandi bafungiwe muri icyo gihugu , banangiwe gusurwa na abahagarariye u Rwanda muri Uganda .
Ni mu gihe Itegeko Nshinga rya Uganda riteganya ko nta muntu ugomba gufungwa igihe kirenze amasaha 48 uhereye igihe yafatiwe , ataragezwa imbere ya urukiko .
Abarwanashyaka ba Parti Socialiste bakomeje gucikamo ibice bapfa uruhare rwa u Bufaransa muri Jenoside
Mu ntangiriro za Gicurasi uyu mwaka , abarwanashyaka 23 ba Parti socialiste ( PS ) mu Bufaransa bahoze muri Guverinoma ya François Mitterand , bandikiye umunyamabanga wa mbere wa iryo shyaka Olivier Faure , bamusaba kwihaniza umukandida wabo mu matora ya abadepite ba u Burayi , washinje Mitterand na ubutegetsi bwe uruhare muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Gabon iri mu bihugu 44 byashyize umukono ku masezerano ashyiraho isoko rusange rya ibihugu bihurira mu Muryango wa Afurika Yunze Ubumwe , AU , azwi nka AfCFTA .
Ibihugu 22 bisabwa kuyemeza burundu ngo ashyirwe mu bikorwa byarabonetse ndetse biteganyijwe ko mu kwezi gutaha azatangizwa ku mugaragaro .
Agaruka kuri ayo masezerano , Perezida Kagame yabwiye abanyamakuru ko ibihugu byose bya Afurika bizi akamaro kayo ku buryo na ibitarayasinya bizabikora .
Ati " Na ibihugu bitarayemeza burundu si uko bitabona inyungu cyangwa ngo bibone ko ari ngombwa ahubwo biracyafite ingorane mu bijyanye na amategeko na ibindi bya tekiniki bagomba kubanza gukemura mbere yo kuyashyira mu bikorwa .
Yagarutse kandi ku muti watuma amakimbirane ahora agaragara hirya no hino muri Afurika acika , avuga ko bisaba ubufatanye bwa ibihugu bigize uwo mugabane .
U Rwanda na Gabon bisanzwe bifitanye umubano mwiza .
Byombi bihuriye mu Muryango wa Ubukungu bwa Ibihugu bya Afurika yo Hagati , CEEAC .
U Rwanda na Gabon basinyanye amasezerano ya imikoranire mu 1976 , aza kuvugururwa mu 2010 .
Bifitanye ubuhahirane buhagaze neza dore ko indege ya RwandAir ikorera ingendo mu Mujyi wa Libreville .
Muri Kamena 2016 ibihugu byombi byakuyeho amafaranga yacibwaga umuntu ukoresheje umurongo wa telefoni mu guhamagara hagati yabyo .
