Icyumweru u Rwanda rwahereyemo isomo Uganda bigacura inzigo itarasibangana
Ushobora kuyita intambara ya iminsi itandatu .
Impamvu si uko yamaze iminsi itandatu gusa ingabo za u Rwanda ziha isomo iza Uganda ( UPDF ) , haniyongeraho ko ihuza amatariki neza na intambara ya iminsi itandatu Israel yamaze ihata ikibatsi ingabo za ibihugu bya Abarabu .
Ushobora kuyita intambara ya iminsi itandatu .
Impamvu si uko yamaze iminsi itandatu gusa ingabo za u Rwanda ziha isomo iza Uganda ( UPDF ) , haniyongeraho ko ihuza amatariki neza na intambara ya iminsi itandatu Israel yamaze ihata ikibatsi ingabo za ibihugu bya Abarabu .
Hano itandukaniro rya uko amateka ya u Rwanda ari aya ejo bundi mu 2000 , mu gihe aya Israel hari mu 1967 .
Mu cyumweru nka iki mu 2000 , bya umwihariko uhereye tariki ya 5 kugera tariki ya 10 Kamena , ingabo za u Rwanda zasakiranye na iza Uganda , UPDF ihahurira na uruva gusenya .
Amateka ya umubano wa u Rwanda na Uganda ushatse wayahera mu 1981 - 1986 ubwo Yoweri Museveni yari mu rugamba rwakuyeho ubutegetsi bwa Milton Obote .
Igisirikare cyamufashije cyarimo ahanini impunzi za Abanyarwanda barimo na Perezida Paul Kagame wayoboye ubutasi icyo gihe ndetse akanaza kuyobora urugamba rwo kubohora u Rwanda nyuma ya urupfu rwa Fred Rwigema wishwe rugikubita .
Kuba abanyarwanda bafashije Yoweri Museveni kugera ku butegetsi baratangije urugamba rwo kubohora u Rwanda baturutse muri Uganda byatumye Museveni yishyiramo ko u Rwanda igihugu cye kirufiteho ijambo , mbese ko ba basirikare bari muri NRA bazakomeza guhabwa amategeko aturutse i Kampala na igihe bageze mu gihugu cya inkomoko .
Nyuma yo kubohora u Rwanda no guhagarika Jenoside , Inkotanyi zamenesheje abayikoraga bahungira mu mashyamba ya Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo yitwaga Zaire , hakurikiraho urugamba rwo gucyura impunzi zari zarabaye ingwate yabo muri ayo mashyamba .
Uganda yatumiwe muri urwo rugamba nka inshuti ariko igahora ishaka ko ibikorwa bya indashyikirwa bya Ingabo za u Rwanda biyitirirwa , mu gihe Abanyarwanda bagejeje Museveni ku butegetsi bo ayo mateka bari barayasize i Kampala .
Imvano ya intambara ya Kisangani
Nyuma haje urugamba rwo gukuraho Mobutu Sese Seko no kugeza Kabila ku butegetsi .
U Rwanda rwafatanyije na Uganda ariko icyo gihugu kiza kwibanda cyane ku gusahura imitungo kamere , kandi mu mutwe kigahorana ko ahari Umunyarwanda na umunya - Uganda , umuturanyi wo mu majyaruguru aza mbere .
Mu Ntambara ya II ya Congo , Ingabo za Uganda zaritabiriye ariko RDF ifata bwangu imijyi itandukanye mu Burasirazuba na Amajyepfo ya Iburasirazuba bwa RDC harimo Umujyi wa Kisangani na ikibuga cya indege cya Bangoka giherereye ku bilometero 12 mu nkengero zawo .
UPDF ku rundi ruhande yo yibanze ku duce dukungahaye ku mabuye ya agaciro two mu Majyaruguru ya Iburasirazuba bwa RDC .
Mu gihe imirwano yari ihagaritswe bya agateganyo , UPDF nta mujyi yari yagafashe wo kuba igumyemo .
Abayobozi ba ingabo za Uganda basabye u Rwanda kubaha Kisangani kubera ko rwari rufite na indi mijyi nka Goma , Bukavu , Kindu , Uvira na indi .
Abayobozi ba ingabo za u Rwanda barabyanga .
Icyo gisubizo ntabwo cyakiriwe neza na abayobozi ba ingabo za Uganda .
Mu nama yabereye i Goma yarimo uwari uhagarariye Mwalimu Julius Nyerere , Kahinda Otafiire wari ukuriye itsinda rya Uganda mu biganiro , yabwiye itsinda rya u Rwanda ati " muraduha Kisangani cyangwa twembi tuyibure .
Nka uko Colonel Akhram Hossein wo mu ngabo za Loni yabitangarije Ikinyamakuru Liberation , mu rukerera rwo ku wa 05 Kanama 2000 nibwo ingabo za Uganda zigera ku 7000 zitwaje ibitwaro biremereye , zatunguye iza u Rwanda zizimishaho ibisasu .
Kuva ubwo rurambikana , Igisirikare cya u Rwanda gikora ku ntwaro zacyo kirasa kitababariye ingabo za Uganda , gitwika ibifaru bya UPDF karahava , ingabo za Uganda zihatakariza abasirikare babarwa ko bageraga mu 2000 .
Muri iyo mirwano , Ingabo za Uganda zaharaniraga kwambuka ikiraro kiri ku mugezi wa Tshopo gitandukanya Kisangani ya Amajyepfo yarimo Ingabo za u Rwanda na iy Amajyaruguru yarimo iza Uganda , ariko ingabo za u Rwanda zizibera ibamba .
Mu kiganiro na abanyamakuru , Col Karenzi Karake ( ubu ni Rtd Lieutenant General ) wari uyoboye Ingabo za u Rwanda i Kisangani , yabwiye The Washington Post ku wa 12 Kanama 2000 , ko ibyabaye hagati ya ingabo za ibihugu byombi nta gishimishije kirimo .
Yakomeje ati " Ariko ni bo baturasheho .
Twatsinze urugamba kuko abasirikare bacu bazi icyo barwanira .
Tugiye gusohoka muri Kisangani tutitaye ku byo Abanya - Uganda bashaka .
Icyo gihe yari amaze kwitegereza toni za ibisasu , imbunda na ibindi bikoresho ingabo za Uganda zari zimaze kuhasiga zihunga .
Umunsi urugamba rwahagaze , Gen James Kazini wari uyoboye Ingabo za Uganda i Kisangani yabanje guhamagara Col Karenzi ku cyombo amusaba ko imirwano yahagarara , ndetse Ingabo za Uganda zisubira inyuma ibilometero bisaga icumi hanze ya Kisangani .
Col Danilo Paiva wo mu ngabo za Loni i Kisangani , ni we watangaje bwa nyuma ko agahenge kabonetse , nyuma ya ubuhuza bwa Perezida wa Zambia , Frederic Chiluba wari ukubutse Kampala na Kigali kubonana na ba Perezida Museveni na Paul Kagame bakaganira ku buryo haboneka umuti urambye kuri aya makimbirane .
Kuva iyo ntambara yarangira mu myaka 19 ishize , Museveni ahorana ikidodo ku bisobanuro yasabwa ku bana ba Uganda yashoye mu ntambara idafututse akanayitsindwa , abanya - Uganda bakahagwa ari benshi .
Ibi byatumye arushaho kwijundika ibi bya cyane u Rwanda .
Uganda yasabye u Bwongereza inkunga yo gutera u Rwanda
Ku wa 28 Kanama 2000 nibwo Museveni yandikiye Umunyamabanga wa Leta wa u Bwongereza ushinzwe iterambere mpuzamahanga , Claire Short , ibaruwa amusaba ko Uganda yahabwa inkunga yisumbuye ikava kuri Miliyoni 113 $ ikagera kuri Miliyoni 139 za Amadolari , mu rwego rwo kwigaranzura igisirikare cya u Rwanda .
Muri urwo rwandiko , Uganda yavugaga ko u Rwanda rwamaze gutegura umutwe wa ingabo ugizwe na abasirikare 100 .
000 wo guhirika ubutegetsi bwa Museveni .
Ibi ariko uwari Minisitiri wa Ububanyi na Amahanga wa u Rwanda , Ambasaderi André Bumaya yabiteye utwatsi , abwira PanaPress ikorera i Dakar muri Senegal ko ahubwo ari Uganda yari mu macenga yo gushaka gutera u Rwanda .
Yagize ati " Ntituri mu myiteguro yo gutera Uganda na mba , u Rwanda rushishikajwe no gukemura ibibazo rwasigiwe na jenoside , bityo rero nta mwanya rufite wo kurwana intambara za amafuti " " " " .
Uganda yakurikijeho guhimba ikinyoma cya uko u Rwanda rwateraga inkunga umutwe wa PRA ( Peoplea s Redemption Army ) , byavugwaga ko wari uyobowe na Col Samson Mande na Antony Kyakabale ngo bashakaga guhirika ubutegetsi bwa Yoweri Kaguta Museveni .
Museveni ntarakira ugutsindwa
Mu kiganiro kirekire Perezida Kagame yagiranye na ikinyamakuru Jeune Afrique cyasohotse ku wa 23 Werurwe 2019 ubwo yaganiraga na Umunyamakuru François Soudan , yabajijwe niba bidashoboka ko Museveni yaba atarakira kuba Ingabo za u Rwanda zaratsindiye ize i Kisangani mu myaka 20 ishize .
Aha yashingiraga ku bushotoranyi budasiba bwa Uganda ku Rwanda , burimo na iyicarubozo rikomeje gukorerwa abaturage barwo muri icyo gihugu cya abaturanyi .
Mu gusubiza yagize ati " Twabatsinze ubugira gatatu , ni ukuri , ahari ushobora kuba ufite ukuri .
Ariko nta gushidikanya hari ibindi bisobanuro .
Ubushake bwo gushaka kugenzura u Rwanda , kuducisha bugufi ?
Birashoka .
Perezida Kagame yavuze ko yubaha Museveni nka Perezida wa Uganda ariko ntabwo ari Perezida wa u Rwanda nta nubwo azigera aba we .
Bigomba gukemuka .
Ntabwo dukunda abantu baduha amabwiriza , aho yaba aturutse hose , ibyo urabizi neza .
Umukuru wa Igihugu yakomeje agira ati " Mu ngano , u Rwanda ni igihugu gito , ariko mu ntekerezo no mu rwego rwa Politiki ni igihugu cya rutura .
Yanavuze ko nta muhuza ukenewe kugira ngo ibibazo bya u Rwanda na Uganda bikemuke ahubwo ko byose bishingiye kuri Museveni .
Ati " Izingiro rya ikibazo riri muri Uganda , riri mu biganza bya Museveni .
Imyaka ibiri irihiritse Umunyarwanda Rutagungira atoterezwa mu buroko bwa Uganda
Amagana ya Abanyarwanda ari gutoterezwa mu buroko bwa Uganda bazira ubusa .
Bamwe barashimuswe , abandi bafatwa mu buryo bunyuranye na amategeko , baratotezwa na ibindi .
Amagana ya Abanyarwanda ari gutoterezwa mu buroko bwa Uganda bazira ubusa .
Bamwe barashimuswe , abandi bafatwa mu buryo bunyuranye na amategeko , baratotezwa na ibindi .
Muri ayo magana , harimo umucuruzi Rutagungira René .
Uyu mucuruzi wa Umunyarwanda wakoreraga i Kampala yafashwe tariki 7 Kanama 2017 .
Imyaka ibiri iruzuye afungiwe ubusa mu buryo bunyuranye na amategeko mu Kigo cya Gisirikare cya Makindye nyamara ari umusivile .
Rutagungira uheruka mu rukiko muri Gicurasi uyu mwaka , bivugwa ko agifunzwe na igisirikare nta wemerewe kumugeraho , nta na amakuru atangwa ya aho urubanza rwe rugeze .
Umuryango we urahangayitse cyane .
Yafunzwe ashinjwa kuba intasi nyamara nta bimenyetso na bimwe byigeze bitangwa bimuhamya icyaha .
Abanyamategeko be bakomeje gusaba ko yarekurwa , bavuga ko yahohotewe kandi afunzwe mu buryo bunyuranyije na amategeko ariko Leta yavuniye ibiti mu matwi .
Itotezwa yakorewe ryamaze kumwangiza ku mubiri , mu mutwe no mu mibereho muri rusange .
Ubwo aheruka mu rukiko byarigaragazaga ko yananutse cyane ndetse adashobora guhagarara adafite icyo yishingikirijeho .
Si ubwa mbere Abanyarwanda bajya cyangwa baba muri Uganda , baba inzirakarengane za ukutubahiriza amategeko gukorwa na inzego zishinzwe umutekano muri Uganda .
Umwe mu basesenguzi mu bya umutekano i Kigali yagize ati " Imana niyo yonyine izi umubare wa inzirakarengane za Abanyarwanda bashimutwa na Urwego rushinzwe ubutasi mu Gisirikare ( CMI ) na Urwego rushinzwe Umutekano wa Imbere ( ISO ) .
Ikimenyetso cya iyo mikorere idahwitse ya Guverinoma ya Uganda ni umunsi uwahoze ari Minisitiri wa Umutekano , Gen Henry Tumukunde yavaga mu biro bye , akajya mu Kigo cya Gisirikare cya Makindye gukubita no gutoteza Rutagungira .
Ibyo ni ibigaragaza ko Rutagungira yashimuswe , akanafungwa ku mategeko yatanzwe na Tumukunde .
Ibyabaye kuri Rutagungira ni kimwe na ibyabaye kuri Emmanuel Rwamuco , umucuruzi wakoreraga i Mbarara ndetse na inshuti ye Augustin Rutayisire bafashwe muri Gicurasi umwaka ushize bakabanza gufungirwa i Mbarara , bakahakubitirwa bikomeye mbere yo kujyanwa i Kampala .
Aba bagabo bashimuswe ku mategeko yatanzwe na Mukama Moses Kandiho , umuvandimwe wa Brig Gen Abel Kandiho uyobora Urwego rushinzwe Ubutasi mu Gisirikare .
Mukama Kandiho usanzwe ashinzwe umutekano muri Mbarara yahamagaye ushinzwe ibikorwa byo kurwanya umwanzi mu gace ka Mbarara , Maj Mushambo , akihagera amwereka abo Banyarwanda bari bafashwe ababeshyera ko bafatanywe intwaro .
Ababibonye biba bavuga ko nta na umwe muri abo bagabo wari ufite intwaro .
Ahubwo bari bafite miliyoni 140 za amashilingi ya Uganda bari bagiye kubitsa kuri Banki i Mbarara .
Mukama Kandiho na Mushambo bafashe ayo mafaranga barayatwara , bafata imbunda baziha ku ngufu Rwamucyo na Rutayisire babajyana muri gereza .
Aba bagabo ubu bari kuborera muri Gereza ya Luzira , nta cyizere na mba cya uko bazahabwa ubutabera .
Abanyarwanda nka abo iyo bari mu buroko , bafatwa nabi bikabije , uburenganzira bwabo bugahonyorwa , bagatotezwa , bakicishwa inzara .
Nka Rutagungira we , umwe mu bavandimwe be yavuze ko nyuma yo gukubitishwa kenshi amashanyarazi no gushyirwa mu mazi ya urubura , ubu ibiganza bye nta kintu bishobora gufata kuko byagagaye .
Amategeko ya Uganda avuga ko ukekwaho icyaha adakwiriye kumara amasaha arenga 48 ataragezwa imbere ya urukiko ngo yisobanure ku byo ashinjwa .
Nyamara iyo bigeze ku Banyarwanda bamara amezi ndetse na imyaka bafunzwe bitubahirije amategeko , bafungiwe ahantu hatazwi cyangwa mu buroko bwa CMI .
Ubuhamya bwa abagira amahirwe bakava muri ayo menyo ya rubamba bakajugunywa ku mupaka , bwuzuyemo ibindi bintu bibi byinshi bakorerwa .
Kuri ubu ikigezweho , ni ukubakubita kugeza bataye ubwenge no kubapfuka amaso bakabajyana mu bihuru kubajugunyayo .
Vuba aha , tariki 23 Kamena , Eric Rugorotsi yajugunywe mu mugezi witwa Umuyanja uherereye Ntungamo .
Yahajugunywe na abakozi ba Urwego rushinzwe Umutekano wa Imbere mu Gihugu ( ISO ) , ategekwa koga agakiza ubuzima bwe cyangwa agahitamo kurohama .
Yabwiwe ko naramuka ahuye na polisi cyangwa urundi rwego rushinzwe umutekano aza kuvuga ko yarekuwe na abakozi ba ISO .
Ikindi Rugorotsi yahishuye ni uko abamutotezaga ari abantu bavuga Ikinyarwanda neza cyane .
Ibyo ni ibishimangira ibyo Guverinoma ya u Rwanda ihora ivuga bya uko ubutegetsi bwa Uganda bukorana cyane na Umutwe wa Iterabwoba wa RNC .
Icyo wamenya ku itegeko rya ubwenegihugu ryateje imvururu mu Buhinde
Leta ya u Buhinde iherutse gushyiraho itegeko ryemerera ubwenegihugu abaturage bava mu bihugu bituranye na bwo , bo mu madini yose usibye abo mu idini ya Islam .
Leta ya u Buhinde iherutse gushyiraho itegeko ryemerera ubwenegihugu abaturage bava mu bihugu bituranye na bwo , bo mu madini yose usibye abo mu idini ya Islam .
Impuguke mu mategeko zo zivuga ko iri tegeko rihabanye cyane na itegeko Nshinga rya iki gihugu , riteganya ko amadini yose angana imbere ya amategeko .
Iri tegeko rishya rigenga uburyo bwo kubona ubwenegihugu mu Buhinde , rije nyuma yo kuvugurura iryari risanzwe ryo mu mwaka wa 1955 , ryemereraga ba nyamuke bafatwaga nabi bo mu madini ya aba - Hindus , Sikhs , Buddhists , Jains , Parsis , na abakirisitu bava mu bihugu nka Bangladesh , Afghanistan na Pakistan , ariko ntirigire icyo rivuga ku bayisilamu .
Iri tegeko ryageze mu nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya u Buhinde bigizwemo uruhare cyane na ishyaka riri ku butegetsi rya aba - Hindu [ Bharatiya Janata Party ] , ryemejwe na perezida wa iki gihugu Ram Nath Kovind , tariki ya 12 Ukuboza , 2019 .
Amashyaka atavuga rumwe na ubutegetsi avuga ko iri tegeko rishya ririmo ivangura , kuko rirobanura idini ya Islam mu gihugu gituwe na abasaga miliyari 1 .
3 bizwi neza ko gitanga ubwisanzure ku madini yose .
Aba - Islam bo mu Buhinde bangana hafi na 15 % bya abaturage bose .
Abanenga iri tegeko bavuga ko byakozwe mu mugambi wa igihe kirekire wa Guverinoma iyobowe na Minisitiri wa intebe Narendra Modi , kuva yajya ku butegetsi mu myaka itandatu ishize .
Ibirego bitandukanye bigaragaza ukutishimira iri tegeko , byatangiye koherezwa mu rukiko rwa ikirenga .
Umuvugizi wa ishyaka rikomeye ritavuga rumwe na ubutegetsi [ Congress party ] , Sanjay Jha , yatangarije Al Jazeera ko iri tegeko riri mu mugambi wa politiki yo kurema amacakubiri ya ishyaka Bharatiya Janata Party , BJP .
Ati " Politiki ya BJP ni uguhoza u Buhinde mu mwuka mubi no kuzamura uburakari bwa abaturage cyane cyane mu gihe cya amatora .
Mu kwezi gushize , Amit Shah , Minisitiri wa umutekano wa imbere mu gihugu , akaba umwe mu byegera bya Narendra Modi , yatangaje ko igihugu cya u Buhinde kigiye gutangira kubarura abaturage bose , hagamijwe kureba abimukira bava mu bihugu bituranyi badafite ibyangombwa .
Muri Kanama 2019 , ibarura nka iryo ryiswe ryakorewe muri leta ya Assam iherereye mu majyaruguru ashyira uburasirazuba bwa u Buhinde , aho abaturage hafi miliyoni ebyiri bakuwe ku rutonde rwa abenegihugu .
Minisitiri Amit Shah aherutse kwita abimukira ba abanya - Bangladeshi intozi na abacengezi , kandi ko ari imbogamizi ku mutekano wa igihugu .
Ishyaka rye ryamaganiye kure iyakirwa rya impunzi za aba - Rohingya bo muri Myanmar .
, rivuga ko bagomba gusubizwa mu gihugu cyabo , nubwo ubwo bwoko bufatwa nka nyamuke bukanabamo benshi ba abayisilamu , buri kwicirwa muri Myanmar .
Uyu mushinga wa itegeko bwa mbere wagejejwe mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko muri Nyakanga 2016 , uvugurura ingingo irebana na ubwenegihugu yo 1955 , ivuga ko idini rikwiye kuba ishingiro ryo guhabwa ubwenegihugu , kuko mbere iryo tegeko ntiryateganyaga idini nka imwe mu ngingo fatizo zo gutanga ubwenegihugu .
Gusa nyuma yo kwemezwa na abagize inteko Ishinga Amategeko , umutwe wa abadepite , iri tegeko ntiryabashije kugezwa imbere ya sena ya u Buhinde , kubera imyigaragambyo yaberaga muri leta zo mu majyaruguru ashyira uburasirazuba , ndetse na igitutu cya abatavuga rumwe na ubutegetsi .
Ubu itegeko rishya rishyiraho umwihariko kuri leta zo mu majyaruguru ashyira uburasirazuba zari zaragaragayemo imyigaragambyo , rikavuga ko rizashishikariza ibihumbi bya aba - Hindus bava muri Bangladesh guhungira mu Buhinde .
Nkuko biteganywa na itegeko rishya , abimukira badafite ibyangombwa bagomba kuba bamaze imyaka itandatu ku butaka bwa u Buhinde kugira ngo bemererwe ubwenegihugu , mu gihe itegeko ryo mu 1955 ryo ryasabaga kuba umuntu amaze imyaka 12 .
Gusa abanyamategeko bavuga ko iri tegeko rishya rihonyora ingingo ya 14 ya itegeko Nshinga rya u Buhinde , itanga uburenganzira bungana imbere ya amategeko .
Abarinenga bavuga ko rimeze nka irya Trump wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ukumira aba - islam bo mu bihugu bimwe na bimwe kwaka ubuhungiro .
Perezida Kagame yifuza kuzasimburwa na umugore ( Video )
Perezida Paul Kagame yatangaje ko politiki yo guteza imbere abagore imaze gutanga umusaruro mwiza mu iterambere rya igihugu , akifuza na we yazasimburwa na umugore ku kuyobora u Rwanda .
Perezida Paul Kagame yatangaje ko politiki yo guteza imbere abagore imaze gutanga umusaruro mwiza mu iterambere rya igihugu , akifuza na we yazasimburwa na umugore ku kuyobora u Rwanda .
Yabigarutseho kuri uyu wa Kane tariki 19 Ukuboza ubwo yagaragazaga uko igihugu gihagaze mu ijambo yagejeje ku bitabiriye inama ya 17 ya Umushyikirano .
Imbere ya ibihumbi byitabiriye iyo nama , Perezida Kagame yavuze ko guteza imbere abagore byahinduye byinshi mu buzima bwa igihugu ku buryo bisigaye binigaragaza ku rwego mpuzamahanga .
Yagize ati " Mwabonye muri iyi minsi ibijyanye na uburinganire abagore na abagabo ku Isi yose ibihugu ijana na mirongo turi mu ba mbere 10 , mu bya ukuri hari aho bagera ngirango abantu bakarambirwa u Rwanda bagashaka kurugabanyiriza ubundi twagakwiye kuba turi mu ba mbere batanu ariko turi mu ba mbere 10 nabyo turabyemera .
Perezida Kagame yagaragaje ko uwo mwanya atari mwiza cyane kuko u Rwanda rwigeze kuza mu bihugu bitandatu bya mbere mu guteza imbere uburinganire bwa abagabo na abagore , gusa agaragaza ko na aho ruri atari habi .
Yavuze ko politiki ya uburinganire na ubwuzuzanye ijya kujyaho , akamaro kayo kagaragaraga kandi na abandi bamaze kubibona .
Ati " Iyi politiki imaze imyaka twayikoze tuyemera kandi twumva akamaro kayo kandi ifite umusaruro ugaragarira na abandi babona ko bikora ariko dukore na ibindi tugera mu ba mbere batanu .
Hari akazi ko gukora kenshi bafatanyije na abagabo .
Abadamu bamaze kugira aho bagera , dushyiremo umuvuduko dufatanye mu bucuruzi mu buyobozi , ubutabera , abashinzwe umutekano , abashinzwe byose .
Ashingiye ku byagezweho ku bufatanye na abagore , Perezida Kagame yavuze ko yifuza ko umunsi umwe umugore yazayobora u Rwanda .
Ati " Njye nifuza rimwe ko uyu mwanya mwampaye ubukurikira uzatwarwa na umugore , abagabo bari hano niba ndi bubakire simbizi ariko nabo bashobora kuba ari byo bashaka .
Perezida Kagame yasabye abanyarwanda gukomeza kongera imbaraga mubyo bakora , kuko hari byinshi byagezweho benshi batumvaga ko byashoboka .
Kuva mu 2003 Itegeko Nshinga rigena ko mu myanya yose itorerwa mu buyobozi no muri guverinoma , abagore bagomba kugiramo 30 % .
Perezida wa Urwego Ngishwanama rwa inararibonye mu Rwanda , Rutaremara Tito yigeze gusobanura ko gushyira abagore mu buyobozi ari " ubushake bwa politiki bujyanye na ibibera mu Rwanda .
Nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , abagore banganaga hafi na 70 % bya abaturage bose .
Muri Guverinoma , abagore bangana na 50 % , mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko mu Mutwe wa Abadepite mu Rwanda bangana na 61 .
3 % bavuye kuri 14 % mu 1994 .
U Rwanda nirwo ruyoboye ibindi bihugu byo ku Isi mu kugira abagore benshi mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko .
Mu bucamanza ni 49 .
6 % mu gihe mu buyobozi bwa inama njyanama za uturere abagore ari 41 % .
Mu burezi abakobwa bitabira amashami ya imibare , ubumenyi na ikoranabuhanga bavuye kuri 56 .
7 % muri 2015 bagera kuri 63 .
9 % muri 2018 , na ho abitabira amashuri ya imyuga na ubumenyingiro bavuye 41 .
8 % muri 2015 bagera kuri 43 .
8 % muri 2018 , mu gihe abagore bigisha muri aya mashuri bavuye kuri 32 .
9 % muri 2010 bakagera kuri 42 .
7 % muri 2018 .
Abagore 59 .
99 % bafite ubutaka basangiye na abo bashakanye mu gihe 24 .
63 % bafite ubutaka bihariye .
Ibi bigatuma 38 % bya abagore bakorana na ibigo bya imari , batanze ingwate ku butaka bwabo .
Abagore bakorana na ibigo bya imari na bo bikubye 2 mu myaka 4 , aho bavuye kuri 36 % muri 2012 bagera kuri 63 % muri 2016 .
Harabura iki ngo u Bufaransa bugire ambasaderi mu Rwanda ?
Imyaka ibaye ine u Bufaransa budafite ambasaderi ubuhagarariye i Kigali .
Uhaheruka ni Michel Flesch wagiye mu 2015 , kugeza ubu hakaba hataratangazwa umusimbura .
Imyaka ibaye ine u Bufaransa budafite ambasaderi ubuhagarariye i Kigali .
Uhaheruka ni Michel Flesch wagiye mu 2015 , kugeza ubu hakaba hataratangazwa umusimbura .
Kugeza ubu imirimo ya ambasade ya u Bufaransa i Kigali ikurikiranwa na Chargé da Affaires .
Flesch yagiye umubano wa ibihugu byombi utameze neza , ahanini hashingiwe ku mpamvu za politiki .
Mbere ya uko Ambasaderi Flesch agenda , Leta ya u Bufaransa yari yarahaye u Rwanda izina rishya rya uwo yifuza ko yayihagararira , Fred Constant , wari usanzwe ari Ambasaderi mu Birwa bya Antilles na Guyane .
Ntiyaje koherezwa mu Rwanda kuko hashize igihe kirenga umwaka rutaramwemeza ajyanwa muri Guinée Équatoriale .
Kuri uyu wa Mbere tariki 22 Nyakanga , Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Minisiteri ya Ububanyi na Amahanga , Ubutwererane na Ibikorwa bya Umuryango wa Afurika ya Iburasirazuba , Amb .
Nduhungirehe Olivier yakiriye mu biro bye Chargé da Affaires mushya wa u Bufaransa i Kigali , Jérémie Blin baganira ku guteza imbere umubano hagati ya ibihugu byombi .
Blin asimbuye Etienne de Souza wari umaze igihe akurikirana ibikorwa bya Ambasade ya u Bufaransa mu Rwanda .
IGIHE yagiranye ikiganiro na Amb Nduhungirehe , imubaza impamvu u Bufaransa bukomeje kohereza ba Chargé da Affaires , aho kuzana ambasaderi mushya .
Yagize ati " Igihe nikigera Abafaransa bazamushyiraho , natwe tukaba twiteguya kuzasuzuma ubwo busabe ariko ubu umubano umeze neza .
Bivuze ko ibyabaye mu bihe byashize atari byo bizaba ubu .
Umubano wa u Rwanda na u Bufaransa wagiye uba mubi nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , u Rwanda rushinja icyo gihugu uruhare mu gufasha Leta yakoze Jenoside , u Bufaransa nabwo bugashinja bamwe mu bayobozi bakuru ba u Rwanda guhanura indege yari itwaye Perezida Juvénal Habyarimana .
Umubano watangiye kuba mwiza mu 2017 ubwo Emmanuel Macron yatorerwaga kuyobora u Bufaransa , akazana impinduka mu bubanyi na amahanga .
Umwaka ushize , ubushinjacyaha bwa u Bufaransa bwahagaritse burundu iperereza ku ihanurwa rya indege ya Habyarimana nyuma yo kubura ibimenyetso ku bo bashinjaga kubigiramo uruhare .
Muri Mata uyu mwaka kandi Perezida Macron yashyizeho itsinda rya inzobere rishinzwe gucukumbura uruhare rwa u Bufaransa muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
IGIHE yabajije Nduhungirehe niba u Rwanda atari rwo rwaba rwanga kwemeza ba ambasaderi ba u Bufaransa , maze abihakana yivuye inyuma .
Yavuze ko nta muntu na umwe u Bufaransa bwigeze bwohereza vuba aha busaba ko u Rwanda rwamwemeza nka ambasaderi ngo rumwange .
Ati " Oya ntawe twigeze twanga rwose .
Ibyo ntabwo ari byo ntawe twigeze twanga .
Ntawe bigeze bohereza .
Na Perezida Macron yarabivuze umwaka ushize ko ubu turimo duteza imbere umubano kugira ngo ugaruke mu nzira nziza , ko igihe nikigera bazohereza ambasaderi .
Yakomeje agira ati " Ambasaderi ni u Bufaransa bumushyiraho si u Rwanda rumushyiraho .
U Bufaransa igihe cyose buzamushyiraho tuziga kuri ubwo busabe .
Umubano ushingiye kuri za ambasade hagati ya u Rwanda na u Bufaransa utangirira mu 1962 u Rwanda rukibona ubwigenge .
Mu kwezi gushize Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Ikigega Mpuzamahanga cya Abafaransa gishinzwe Iterambere ( Agence Française de Developpément , AFD ) , yaje mu Rwanda yizeza gukomeza gufatanya mu bikorwa bya iterambere .
Umuyobozi wa icyo kigo yahaherukaga mu 1992 .
Guhera mu 1962 , u Bufaransa bumaze kohereza mu Rwanda ba ambasaderi 16 , kuva kuri Jean - Marc Barbey wabimburiye abandi kugeza kuri Michel Flesh wagiye mu 2015 .
Amatora ya abakuru ba ibihugu yitezwe mu bihugu bya Afurika muri 2020
Politiki ni kimwe mu bivugwaho cyane ku isi , guhera umwaka utangiye kugeza urangiye .
Abakuru ba ibihugu ni bamwe mu bagena imirongo migari yayo ku buryo uwo mwanya uba urebwa na abatari bake , hagakoreshwa inzira zose zaba imbi na inziza ngo bicare kuri iyo ntebe icurirwamo ibitekerezo biyobora ibihugu bitandukanye .
Politiki ni kimwe mu bivugwaho cyane ku isi , guhera umwaka utangiye kugeza urangiye .
Abakuru ba ibihugu ni bamwe mu bagena imirongo migari yayo ku buryo uwo mwanya uba urebwa na abatari bake , hagakoreshwa inzira zose zaba imbi na inziza ngo bicare kuri iyo ntebe icurirwamo ibitekerezo biyobora ibihugu bitandukanye .
Uyu mwaka muri Afurika hateganyijwe amatora mu bihugu bitandukanye , azasiga bamwe mbahagurutse muri izo ntebe nkuru mu bihugu byabo , bagaha umwanya abandi bafite ibyerecyezo bishya bijyanye na ibyo abaturage bifuza .
Muri rusange , ibihugu 22 bya Afurika nibyo bifite amatora muri uyu mwaka ariko icyenda muri byo nibyo bizabamo amatora ya abakuru ba ibihugu .
IGIHE yakusanyije ibya ingenzi ukwiriye kumenya kuri ayo matora ategerejwe na benshi .
Mu iki gihugu hateganyijwe amatora ya Umukuru wa igihugu , tariki 22 Gashyantare .
Mu kwezi kwa cumi , ishyaka ritavuga rumwe na ubutegetsi ryavuze ko Jean Piere Fabre ari we mukandida waryo uzaba ahanganye na Perezida uriho Faure Gnassingbé .
Nta gutungurana kwitezwe kuko amahirwe agihabwa Faure umaze ku butegetsi imyaka 15 .
Amatora ateganyijwe muri iki gihugu ni aya Umukuru wa igihugu , Inteko rusange na ay Abadepite .
Aya matora ateganyijwe tariki 20 Gicurasi uyu mwaka .
Perezida Nkurunziza Pierre yatangaje ko ataziyamamariza indi manda .
Aya matora yitezwe kuzandika amateka muri iki gihugu nyuma ya imvururu zadutse guhera mu 2015 ubwo Nkurunziza yiyamarizaga manda ya gatatu itaravuzweho rumwe .
Andi matora ateganyijwe tariki 4 Ukwakira 2020 , ni aya Umukuru wa igihugu .
Perezia John Pombe Magufuli wayoboye Tanzania kuva mu mwaka 2015 yitezwe kuyobora indi manda .
Nubwo anengwa ibirimo kubangamira ubwisanzure , ashimwa na abaturage kuba yarabashije guhashya ruswa no kwirukana abayobozi badakora inshingano zabo .
Côte da Ivoire
Amatora ya Umukuru wa igihugu ataganyijwe tariki 31 Ukwakira uyu mwaka .
Perezida wa iki gihugu , Alassane Ouattara , wari waratangaje ko atazongera kwiyamamariza indi manda hejuru ya ebyiri amaze kuyobora , yavuze ko azagaragara muri ayo matora .
Burkina Faso Hateganyijwe amatora ya Umukuru wa igihugu na Inteko Ishinga Amategeko mu Ugushyingo 2020 .
Uwahoze ari Minisitiri wa intebe muri iki gihugu , Kadré Désiré Ouédraogo yamaze gutangaza ko aziyamamariza umwanya wa Umukuru wa igihugu akazaba ahanganye na Perezida uriho Roch Marc Christian Kaboré .
Ghana Amatora ateganyijwe muri iki gihugu ya Umukuru wa igihugu azaba tariki 7 Ukuboza 2020 .
Ishyaka ritavuga rumwe na Ubutegetsi , National Democratic Congress ryamaze gutangaza ko uwahoze ari Umukuru wa iki gihugu , John Mahama ari we uzaba arihagarariye ahanganye na Perezida uriho , Nana Akufo - Addo .
Muri iki gihugu hateganyijwe amatora ya Umukuru wa igihugu na Inteko Ishinga Amategeko tariki 27 Ukuboza ndetse na amatora ya abandi bayobozi batandukanye ateganyijwe mu Ukwakira .
Amatora ya Umukuru wa igihugu ateganyijwe tariki 27 Ukuboza .
Umuvugizi wa ishyaka " " " " Kwa Na Kwa " " " " rya uwahoze ari Perezida wa iki gihugu Francois Bozizé , yatangaje ko aziyamamariza kuyobora iki gihugu .
Hateganyijwe amatora ya Umukuru wa igihu mu Ukuboza .
Ishyaka ritavuga rumwe na ubutegetsi , Seychelles National Party ryamaze gutanga Ramkalawan nka umukandida ku mwanya wa Perezida aho azaba ahanganye na Perezida Danny Faure aziyamamariza indi manda .
Baherereye he ?
Ibirari bya abari bagize Guverinoma ya mbere nyuma ya Jenoside
Ku wa Kabiri tariki 19 Nyakanga 1994 nibwo hagiyeho Guverinoma ya Ubumwe .
Imyaka 25 irashize !
Ku wa Kabiri tariki 19 Nyakanga 1994 nibwo hagiyeho Guverinoma ya Ubumwe .
Imyaka 25 irashize !
Ni Guverinoma yagiyeho nyuma ya iminsi ibiri gusa ingabo zari iza FPR Inkotanyi zimaze kubohora imijyi ya Ruhengeri na Gisenyi , zinahagarika Jenoside yari imaze guhitana Abatutsi basaga miliyoni imwe .
Nubwo intambara ya amasasu yasaga na irangiye , umutima ntiwari hamwe kuko abanyapolitiki benshi na ibikomerezwa bya Leta ishinjwa gutegura no gukora Jenoside , bari hakurya gato muri Zaire bisuganya ngo bagaruke ku butegetsi bari bamaze kwirukanwaho .
Tariki 17 Nyakanga nyuma yo kubohoza ibice byose bya igihugu , FPR Inkotanyi yasohoye itangazo riteguza Guverinoma ya inzibacyuho yari igiye kujyaho , rinashimangira ko muri iyo Guverinoma hatazabonekamo abo mu mashyaka ya MRND , CDR na andi yagize uruhare muri Jenoside .
Guverinoma ya Ubumwe yari igizwe na abaminisitiri 17 ariko tariki 19 harahiye 14 , abandi bongerwamo tariki 20 Nyakanga .
Mu ijambo Paul Kagame yavuze kuri uwo munsi wo gushyiraho Guverinoma nshya , yavuze ko akazi kakiri kose bityo ko bisaba Guverinoma nshya gukoresha ingufu .
Yagize ati " Turebye aho tuva na aho tugana , ndabona ko nta na umwe wari ukwiye kuvuga ko twasoje inshingano zacu , ngo ajyeho yicare hasi atekereze ko ibibazo byose byarangiye .
Ni igihe cyo guhaguruka tugakorera hamwe , nka uko twabikoze mu bihe byashize bigatuma tugera aho tugeze uyu munsi , tugashyiraho guverinoma dufitiye icyizere ko izayobora igihugu ikakigeza mu nzira ya iterambere .
Guverinoma yo ku wa 19 Nyakanga , imyanya umunani yahawe FPR Inkotanyi , itatu ihabwa ishyaka MDR , itatu ihabwa PL , PSD ihabwa imyanya ibiri naho umwe uhabwa PDC .
Abari bagize Guverinoma ya mbere ya Ubumwe
Perezida : Pasteur Bizimungu
Pasteur Bizimungu ni we wahise agirwa Perezida wa inzibacyuho .
Uyu mugabo uvuka muri Gisenyi , yari umunyamuryango wa FPR Inkotanyi wigeze no kuyobora ikigo cya Electrogaz cyahoze gishinzwe ingufu ku butegetsi bwa Perezida Juvenal Habyarimana .
Bizimungu ubu ufite imyaka 69 yabaye Perezida kugeza kuwa 23 Werurwe 2000 ubwo yeguraga ku mwanya wa Perezida .
Bizimungu yaje gushinga ishyaka PDR Ubuyanja ritemewe na amategeko , mu 2002 aza gutabwa muri yombi ashinjwa kurema umutwe utemewe no kunyereza umutungo wa Leta , umwaka wakurikiyeho akatirwa gufungwa imyaka 15 .
Mu 2006 Bizimungu yandikiye ibaruwa Perezida Kagame asaba imbabazi , azihabwa mu 2007 ahita arekurwa .
Ubu aba mu Rwanda mu bikorwa bye bwite .
2 : Visi Perezida & Minisitiri wa Ingabo : Paul Kagame
Muri Guverinoma ya Ubumwe , Minisitiri wa Ingabo yagizwe Général - Major Paul Kagame anaba Visi Perezida .
Paul Kagame yagumye kuri uwo mwanya kugeza muri Werurwe 2000 ubwo yatorerwaga gusimbura Bizimungu ku mwanya wa Perezida .
Ni inshingano yakoze neza ndetse aza gutorerwa izindi manda , kugeza uyu munsi .
Minisitiri wa Intebe : Faustin Twagiramungu
Guverinoma ya mbere yagiyeho nyuma ya Jenoside yari iyobowe na Faustin Twagiramungu nka Minisitiri wa Intebe .
Twagiramungu wa ishyaka MDR ni umwe mu banyepolitiki bari barahanganye na ingoma ya Habyarimana , bashyigikiye imigambi ya ubumwe na ubwiyunge mu banyarwanda .
Uyu mugabo uvuka mu yahoze ari perefegitura ya Cyangugu , yaje kwegura tariki 28 Kanama 1995 , ahita afata iya ubuhungiro agana mu Bubuligi ari naho akiba .
Asigaye agaragara mu bikorwa birwanya Leta ya u Rwanda ndetse aherutse kwifatanya na Ihuriro P5 rya amashyaka aba hanze ya u Rwanda , atavuga rumwe na Guverinoma ya u Rwanda .
Minisitiri wa Intebe wungirije & Minisitiri wa umurimo : Alexis Kanyarengwe
Kanyarengwe Alexis wo mu Muryango FPR Inkotanyi ni we wahawe umwanya wa Minisitiri wa umurimo akaba na Minisitiri wa Intebe wungirije .
Uyu mugabo ukomoka mu yahoze ari Ruhengeri ( Amajyaruguru ) , ni umwe mu bahoze ari ibikomerezwa ku ngoma ya Habyarimana dore ko ari umwe mu basirikare 11 bafatanyije na Habyarimana guhirika ubutegetsi bwa Grégoire Kayibanda kuwa 5 Nyakanga 1973 .
Kanyarengwe wafatwaga nka nimero ya kabiri ku butegetsi bwa Habyarimana , baje gushwana mu 1980 ashinjwa gushaka kumuhirika , nyuma aza guhunga igihugu ari nabwo yifatanyaga na FPR mu rugamba rwo kubohora igihugu .
Kanyarengwe wabaye umuyobozi wa Umuryango FPR Inkotanyi kugeza mu 1998 , yaje kuvanwa muri Guverinoma mu 1997 .
Alexis Kanyarengwe yitabye Imana tariki 13 Ugushyingo 2006 azize uburwayi , ashyingurwa mu irimbi rya Remera mu mujyi wa Kigali .
Minisitiri wa ububanyi na amahanga : Jean Marie Ndagijimana
Nka igihugu cyari kimaze kuva muri Jenoside , ibihugu byinshi bigifata nka ikitariho , ntabwo byashobokaga kwisubiza ikuzo hatabayeho kugira Minisiteri ya ububanyi na amahanga kandi ikora cyane .
Ndagijimana wari mu ishyaka MDR ni we wahawe uwo mwanya atamazeho kabiri .
Uyu mugabo uvuka mu yahoze ari Cyangugu yamaze amezi ane kuri uwo mwanya , aza guhungira mu Bufaransa atwaye amafaranga yari yahawe ngo ajye gufunguza za ambasade .
Perezida Paul Kagame aherutse kubikomozaho ati " Minisitiri wa ububanyi na amahanga wa mbere wagiyeho icyo gihe yagambanye na abandi bayobozi muri Guverinoma nka Minisitiri wa Intebe icyo gihe , ahabwa amafaranga mu ntoki , ibihumbi amagana bya amadolari , ngo ajye mu mahanga asubukure ibikorwa bya za ambasade cyangwa afunguze inshya .
Uyu mugabo ntabwo yagarutse !
Kandi yari amaze amezi angahe mu kazi , iyo yari guverinoma ya mbere ya inzibacyuho .
Minisitiri wa Umutekano : Seth Sendashonga
Guverinoma ya inzibacyuho yashyizwe kuwa 19 Nyakanga 1994 , ntiyasize na umwanya wa Minisitiri wa Umutekano .
Uwo mwanya wahawe Seth Sendashonga wakomokaga mu yahoze ari Perefegitura ya Kibuye , wari impunzi muri Kenya ku butegetsi bwa Perezida Habyarimana .
Sendashonga wari umunyamuryango wa FPR Inkotanyi , yavuye muri Guverinoma mu 1995 ahita ajya mu buhungiro muri Kenya .
Aho niho yaje kurasirwa tariki 16 Gicurasi 1998 .
Perezida Paul Kagame aherutse kuvuga ko Sendashonga nyuma yo guhunga igihugu yakoranye na abashakaga guhungabanya umutekano ku buryo yari yatangiye kurenga umurongo .
Minisitiri wa Ubutabera : Alphonse Marie Nkubito
Minisiteri ya ubutabera yahawe umunya - Cyangugu , Alphonse Marie Nkubito wari impirimbanyi ya uburenganzira bwa muntu .
Nkubito yayoboye iyo Minisiteri kugeza mu 1995 .
Yaje kwitaba Imana kuwa 13 Gashyantare 1996 azize uburwayi .
Minisitiri wa Uburezi : Pierre - Célestin RWIGEMA
Pierre - Célestin Rwigema uvuka i Gitarama mu Ntara ya Amajyepfo ubu , ni we wagizwe Minisitiri wa mbere wa Uburezi bwa amashuri abanza na ayisumbuye nyuma ya Jenoside .
Rwigema wari mu ishyaka MDR , yaje kuva kuri uwo mwanya aba Minisitiri wa Intebe asimbuye Faustin Twagiramungu .
Umwanya wa Minisitiri wa Intebe yawuvuyeho muri Werurwe 2000 , aza guhungira muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Yagarutse mu gihugu mu mwaka wa 2011 , aza no gutorerwa kuba umudepite uhagarariye u Rwanda mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Umuryango wa Afurika ya Iburasirazuba ( EALA ) ari nawo akiriho kugeza ubu .
Minisitiri wa Amashuri Makuru na ubushakashatsi : Dr Joseph Nsengimana
Dr Nsengimana ni we wagizwe Minisitiri wa amashuri makuru na ubushakashatsi .
Uyu mugabo wavukiye i Busogo muri Musanze yashyizwe kuri uyu mwanya kubera ko yari asanzwe ari inzobere mu bijyanye na uburezi , dore ko yabaye umwarimu muri Kaminuza zirimo iya u Rwanda na iya Lubumbashi .
Nyuma yahawe indi myanya ikomeye irimo kuba minisitiri wa abakozi ba Leta na umurimo , Minisitiri wa ubutaka , gutuza abantu no kurengera ibidukikije ndetse aba umujyanama wihariye wa Perezida Paul Kagame .
Guhera mu 2006 yagiye mu kazi ko kuba ambasaderi , agasoza mu 2014 ubwo yari ahagarariye u Rwanda muri Ethiopia no mu Muryango wa Afurika Yunze Ubumwe .
Ubu Nsengimana aba mu Rwanda aho akorera imirimo itandukanye .
Minisitiri wa Imari : Marc Rugenera
Ibigega na isanduku bya igihugu muri Guverinoma ya mbere byaragijwe Marc Rugenera , umunya - Gitarama wo mu ishyaka PSD .
Uwo mwanya Rugenera yawuvuyeho mu 1997 aba Minisitiri wa Ubucuruzi nyuma aba Minisitiri wa ubukerarugendo .
Ubu Rugenera yashinze ndetse ayobora ikigo cya ubwishingizi cya Radiant .
Minisitiri wa Inganda : Prosper Higiro
Minisitiri wa inganda wa mbere nyuma ya Jenoside yabaye Prosper Higiro , umurwanashyaka wa PL ukomoka mu yahoze ari Kibungo .
Uyu mugabo wa imyaka 58 , nyuma yo kuva muri Guverinoma yabaye umusenateri ndetse na umwe mu bakandida biyamamaje ku mwanya wa Perezida wa Repubulika mu matora yo mu 2010 .
Higiro aherutse kugirwa ambasaderi muri Canada .
Uyu yabaye umuyobozi mu nzego zitandukanye zirimo kuba Umunyamabanga Mukuru wa Ihuriro rya Inteko zishinga Amategeko za Umuryango uhuza ibihugu byo mu Karere ka Ibiyaga Bigari ( FP - ICGRL ) .
Minisitiri wa Ubuzima : Dr Joseph Karemera
Karemera wahoze ari impunzi muri Uganda , ni umunyarwanda ukomoka mu yahoze ari Perefegitura ya Byumba , wabaye Minisitiri wa mbere wa ubuzima wa u Rwanda rwa nyuma ya Jenoside .
Uwo mwanya yawuvuyeho agirwa Minisitiri wa Uburezi .
Ntakivugwa cyane ariko ni umwe mu bagitanga ibitekerezo bihamye mu muryango wa politiki akomokamo ari wo FPR Inkotanyi .
Minisitiri ushinzwe itumanaho no gutwara abantu na ibintu : Immaculée Gahima Kayumba
Gahima wo mu muryango FPR Inkotanyi , ni umunya - Butare wabaye mu buhungiro mu gihugu cya u Burundi mbere ya Jenoside .
Nubwo atakivugwa cyane , Madamu Gahima wanabaye umusenateri ubu ari mu Rwanda aho akorera imirimo itandukanye .
Minisitiri wa imibereho myiza : Mugabo Pie
Mugabo Pie yabaye Minisitiri wa imibereho myiza ya abaturage muri Guverinoma ya mbere ya ubumwe , ari umuyoboke wa ishyaka PL .
Uyu mugabo wa inzobere mu mategeko yanabaye umucamanza na Perezida wa Urukiko rukuru .
Aba mu Rwanda aho atanga serivisi zitandukanye zijyanye na iby amategeko .
Minisitiri ushinzwe impunzi : Dr Jacques Bihozagara
Nka igihugu cyari kivuye muri Jenoside na intambara yo kubohora igihugu , hari abaturage basaga miliyoni ebyiri bahunze kandi bakenewe mu kongera kubaka igihugu .
Byari ngombwa gushyiraho Minisiteri ishinzwe gucyura impunzi , cyane ko ubuhunzi bwari mu bibazo byatumye FPR Inkotanyi ishingwa .
Dr Bihozagara yitabye Imana muri Werurwe 2016 , agwa muri Gereza ya Mpimba mu Burundi aho yari amaze umwaka afungiwe kubera impamvu za politiki .
Minisitiri wa Umuryango na Iterambere rya umugore : Inyumba Aloysia
Inyumba wakomokaga mu muryango FPR Inkotanyi ni we wagizwe Minisitiri ushinzwe iterambere rya umuryango na umugore .
Nka uwaturukaga mu muryango FPR Inkotanyi , Inyumba yatangije urugamba rwo gutinyura no gushishikariza abagore kumva ko bashoboye , nyuma ya uko bari bamaze no kugira uruhare mu rugamba rwo kubohora igihugu .
Yitabye Imana tariki 6 Ukuboza 2012 azize uburwayi .
Minisitiri wa Urubyiruko na amashyirahamwe : Patrick Mazimhaka
Uyu mugabo wabaye umuyobozi wungirije wa FPR Inkotanyi mbere gato ya urugamba rwo guhagarika Jenoside , ni we wahawe kuyobora urubyiruko muri Guverinoma ya mbere yabayeho nyuma ya Jenoside .
Muri 2003 yatorewe kuba umuyobozi wungirije muri Komisiyo ya Akanama ka Afurika yunze Ubumwe .
Yitabye Imana ku wa 25 Mutarama 2018 azize uburwayi .
Minisitiri wa ingufu na imirimo rusange : Charles Ntakirutinka
Charles Ntakirutinka yabaye Minisitiri wa ingufu na imirimo rusange nka umunyamuryango wa ishyaka PSD .
Ntakirutinka uvuka ku Gikongoro , mu 2001 afatanyije na Pasteur Bizimungu wahoze ari Perezida bashinze ishyaka PDR Ubuyanja ritari ryemewe na amategeko .
Yatawe muri yombi mu gihe kimwe na Bizimungu mu 2002 , ahamywa ibyaha birimo gukangurira abaturage kwigumura no kurema umutwe wa abagizi ba nabi .
Yakatiwe igifungo cya imyaka icumi , ayirangiza mu 2012 .
Ubu yasubiye mu buzima busanzwe ariko ntakigaragara mu bikorwa bya Politiki .
Minisitiri wa ubukerarugendo na ibidukikije : Nayinzira Jean - Népomuscène
Nayinzira yabaye Minisitiri wa Ibidukikije na ubukerarugendo muri guverinoma yaguye ya inzibacyuho yatangajwe ku wa 19 Nyakanga 1994 , yari iyobowe na Faustin Twagiramungu .
Yaje kuba umudepite ariko mu 2002 aza kwegura mu nteko ishinga Amategeko ashinjwa imyitwarire idahwitse .
Nayinzira yagarutse mu ruhando rwa politiki ahatanira kuba Perezida wa Repubulika nka umukandida wigenga , mu matora ya Perezida yo mu 2003 .
Uyu mugabo wavukiye mu yahoze ari Perefegitura ya Gisenyi ku wa 10 Werurwe 1943 , yitabye Imana kuwa 13 Kanama 2014 .
Minisitiri wa Ubuhinzi , Ubworozi na Amashyamba : Dr Iyamuremye Augustin
Iyamuremye wo mu ishyaka PSD ni we wabaye Minisitiri Minisitiri wa Ubuhinzi , Ubworozi na amashyamba muri Guverinoma ya mbere ya Ubumwe , icyakora we yashyizweho tariki 18 Kanama 1994 hashize ukwezi abandi bari mu mirimo .
Yabaye Minisitiri wa Ububanyi na Amahanga kuva mu 1999 kugeza muri 2000 .
Yanabaye kandi Minisitiri wa Itangazamakuru .
Iyamuremye ni we wayoboye Komisiyo yashinzwe kwiga ku ngingo za Itegeko Nshinga ryavuguruwe mu 2015 .
Kuri ubu Iyamuremye ni umuyobozi wa Urwego rwa Igihugu Ngishwanama rwa Inararibonye .
Minisitiri wa Igenamigambi , Birara Jean - Berchmas
Birara yagizwe Minisitiri tariki 2 Nzeri 1994 nyuma ya amezi asaga abiri Guverinoma nshya igiyeho .
Ni umunyapoliti uvuka mu yahoze ari Perefegitura ya Gisenyi .
Yirukanywe muri Guverinoma mu Ukwakira 1997 .
Ubu ari mu kiruhuko cya izabukuru , aba mu Mujyi wa Kigali .
Minisitiri wa Itangazamakuru : Nkuliyingoma Jean Baptiste
Nkuliyingoma yagizwe Minisitiri ahagarariye ishyaka MDR .
Akomoka mu yahoze ari Perefegitura ya Byumba .
Yavuye muri Guverinoma muri Kanama 1995 ubwo Twagiramungu wari Minisitiri wa Intebe yeguraga , bombi bafata iya ubuhungiro .
Urebye urutonde rwa abaminisitiri ba Guverinoma ya mbere yagiyeho nyuma ya Jenoside , nta na umwe ukiri muri Guverinoma .
Bake baracyari mu mirimo ya leta , abandi bari mu kiruhuko cya izabukuru kubera imyaka bagezeho ; bahunze igihugu kubera amakosa bakoze abandi bakomeje imirimo mu rwego rwa abikorera .
RDC : Umudepite yasubije Muzito wasabye ko u Rwanda rwomekwa kuri Congo ngo ibone amahoro
Umudepite akaba na Umuyobozi wa ishyaka Envol muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , Delly Sesanga , yamaganye igitekerezo cya umunyapolitiki Adolphe Muzito uherutse gusaba ko igihugu cye gitera u Rwanda rukomekwa kuri RDC kugira ngo amahoro aboneke mu Burasirazuba .
Umudepite akaba na Umuyobozi wa ishyaka Envol muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , Delly Sesanga , yamaganye igitekerezo cya umunyapolitiki Adolphe Muzito uherutse gusaba ko igihugu cye gitera u Rwanda rukomekwa kuri RDC kugira ngo amahoro aboneke mu Burasirazuba .
Amagambo ya Muzito uvugira ihuriro rya amashyaka atavuga rumwe na Leta , Lamuka , ku ikubitiro yamaganiwe kure na bamwe mu bayobozi bakomeye muri iryo huriro barimo Moise Katumbi na Jean Pierre Bemba .
Kuri uyu wa Gatandatu ubwo yari yahuye na abarwanashyaka ba ishaka rye bifurizanya umwaka mushya , Delly Sesanga , yabajijwe niba na we abona amahoro mu Burasirazuba bwa Congo azaturuka mu gutera u Rwanda bakarwiyomekaho .
Umuyobozi wa Envol akaba na Umudepite mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Congo , Sesanga yamaganye amagambo ya Muzito , avuga ko amahoro ya Congo azaturuka imbere muri Congo .
Yagize ati " Intambara sicyo gisubizo .
Iyi ntambara ahubwo yakarwanywe hagamijwe kuzana ubumwe imbere mu gihugu , gukuraho imikorere mibi ya ubuyobozi , ruswa , ikimenyane byazangereje leta bikanagira ingaruka ku nzego za umutekano .
Sesanga yavuze ko igisirikare cya Congo kitabuze imbaraga zo gutsinda intambara ziri mu Burasirazuba nka uko bamwe babikega , ahubwo ngo ni imikorere mibi .
Ati " Abanye - Congo bazi kurwana , barabyerakanye mu Ntambara ya Mbere na iya Kabiri za isi yose .
Yavuze ko imbaraga nyinshi zikwiriye gushyirwa mu kurwanya ibibazo byugarije igihugu biri imbere kurusha kwitwaza ibyo hanze , nka uko ikinyamakuru Politico cyabitangaje .
Mbere yo kuba umudepite , Sesanga yakoze mu myanya itandukanye muri Congo harimo no kuba Minisitiri wa igenamigambi .
Musenyeri wa Kinshasa , Fridolin Ambongo , na we aherutse kuvuga ko ibihugu bituranye na Congo birimo u Rwanda bifite umugambi wo gucamo ibice igihugu cye bikakiyomekaho .
Ni amagambo yamaganiwe kure haba muri Leta ya Congo ndetse na abandi bakurikiranira politiki ya akarere hafi .
Minisitiri wa Ububanyi na Amahanga , Dr Vincent Biruta , aherutse kuvuga ko imvugo za abanyapolitiki bamwe bo muri RDC ku Rwanda zibabaje kuko ahanini na ibyo bavuga ari ibintu biba bidafite inshingiro .
Ati " Ni ibintu bibabaje , wakwiteguye ko ibyo bavuga biba bifite icyo bafite gifatika ariko nta gihari .
Ntabwo ari ubwa mbere bene ibi bibazo bibaho , hashize igihe hari abanyapolitiki bo muri RDC bumva ko kugira ngo abaturage babo babemere ari uko bavuga nabi u Rwanda .
Dr Biruta yavuze ko nta mugambi uhari wo komeka ibice bya Congo ku Rwanda kandi nta na uzigera ubaho .
U Rwanda na RDC bifitanye umubano mwiza cyane cyane nyuma ya aho Félix Tshisekedi atorewe kuyobora icyo gihugu , akavuga ko arajwe ishinga no kubana neza na ibihugu bya ibituranyi .
Minisitiri Mateke wa Uganda yahishuye ko atemeranya na amasezerano na u Rwanda na umugambi mushya barufiteho
Mu gihe hashize iminsi mike hatekerezwa ko umubano wa u Rwanda na Uganda waba utangiye kugana mu cyerekezo kizima nyuma ya irekurwa rya abanyarwanda icyenda bari bafungiweyo binyuranyije na amategeko , ibintu byabaye nka ibisubira i Rudubi ubwo Umunyamabanga wa Leta Ushinzwe ubutwererane na akarere , Philemon Mateke , yavugaga uburyo atemera amasezerano yasinywe hagati ya Uganda na u Rwanda .
Mu gihe hashize iminsi mike hatekerezwa ko umubano wa u Rwanda na Uganda waba utangiye kugana mu cyerekezo kizima nyuma ya irekurwa rya abanyarwanda icyenda bari bafungiweyo binyuranyije na amategeko , ibintu byabaye nka ibisubira i Rudubi ubwo Umunyamabanga wa Leta Ushinzwe ubutwererane na akarere , Philemon Mateke , yavugaga uburyo atemera amasezerano yasinywe hagati ya Uganda na u Rwanda .
Ni amasezerano yasinyiwe i Luanda muri Angola ku wa 21 Kanama 2019 , agamije gushakira umuti ibibazo u Rwanda rwashinjaga icyo gihugu birimo gufunga abaturage barwo binyuranyije na amategeko no kubakorera iyicarubozo , gushyigikira imitwe igamije kuruhungabanyiriza umutekano no kubangamira ubucuruzi bwarwo .
Mu butumwa yanditse kuri Twitter kuri uyu wa Kane , Mateke yahishuye ko kuva kera na kare atemeraga amasezerano basinyanye na u Rwanda agamije guhosha umwuka mubi uri hagati ya ibihugu byombi , mu gihe ari umwe mu bagombaga kuba bakurikirana uko ashyirwa mu bikorwa .
Yagize ati " Naburiye bagenzi banjye ko nta cyiza kiva mu gusinyana amasezerano na ikibi .
Kugarura amahoro ntibyakunze kuri Chamberlain mu 1938 , ntabwo natwe bizashoboka .
Turekuye abanyabyaha babo , batwituye kurasa abaturage bacu nka imbwa !
Ni igihe cyo gusubiza kuri iyi myitwarire ya ubushotoranyi .
I warned colleagues that nothing good comes from signing a pact with the devil .
Appeasement didna t work for Chamberlain in 1938 , and it wona t work for us .
We release their criminals , and they repay by shooting our citizens like dogs !
Time to respond to this condescending behavior
— Philemon Mateke , PhD ( @ PhilemonMateke ) January 23 , 2020
Aha mu 1938 yashakaga kuvuga ku byabaye muri uwo mwaka hakorwaga inama za inkurikirane hagati ya ibihugu bya u Bwongereza , u Bufaransa , na u Butaliyani , bikemerera u Budage bwari buyobowe na Adolf Hitler kwiyomekaho ibice bimwe bya Czechoslovakia , mu buryo bwo kwirinda intambara .
Hitler yasabaga igice cya Sudetenland , Neville Chamberlain wari Minisitiri wa Intebe wa u Bwongereza afata iya mbere aza guhura na uwayoboraga u Bufaransa , Eduard Daladier na Benito Mussolini wayoboraga u Butaliyani , bahurira i Munich na Hitler , bemeranya ko agace ka Sudetenland komekwa ka u Budage , bataha bahamya ko habonetse amahoro .
Nyuma ya amezi atanu Hitler yarenze ku byemeranyijweho agaba igitero kuri Czechoslovakia yose arayifata .
Nubwo Mateke atatoboye ngo avuge izina rya igihugu , ibyo Mateke yavuze bihura neza na ibibazo birimo kuba hagati ya u Rwanda na Uganda .
Naho ibya abantu barashwe yavugaga bihuye na uko kuri uyu wa Gatatu u Rwanda rwashyikirije Uganda umurambo wa umuturage wayo , Ndagijimana Theogene , warashwe na inzego za umutekano za u Rwanda zamufatiye mu bikorwa bya magendu ashaka no kwinjiza ibiyobyabwenge mu gihugu , zamuhagarika akagerageza kuzirwanya .
Amagambo ya Mateke anahura na ay umudepite Ruth Nankabirwa , kuri uyu wa Gatatu wabwiye bagenzi be mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ko Guverinoma ya Uganda ikwiye gukemura bwangu ikibazo ifitanye na u Rwanda , ariko asa na uca amarenga ku buryo bwakoreshwa .
Yagize ati " Mureke duhe amahirwe asesuye Guverinoma ya Uganda , amahirwe yo kurangiza urugendo rwo guharanira ko dusubirana umubano mwiza nka uwo twahoranye , kuko ntabwo ushobora kwicara hano ngo utange amabwiriza ngo umupaka ufungurwe , ngo utekereze ko ayo mabwiriza azafungura umupaka .
Perezida wa Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Uganda , Rebecca Kadaga , yahise amubwira ko yizeye ko atarimo kuvuga ko bagomba guceceka ngo barindire umwanzuro wa Guverinoma na igihe hari umuntu wabo urashwe .
Nankabirwa yakomeje ati " Ntabwo wakemura ikibazo gihari uyu munsi hatabayeho kubura ubundi buzima .
Gusa imvugo ya Mateke yamaganywe na umudepite wa Uganda mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Umuryango ya Umuryango wa Afurika ya Uburasirazuba , Mukasa Mbidde , wavuze ati " namaganye aya magambo ya Minisitiri niba koko iyi ariyo konti yawe ya ukuri , ndabona igitekerezo cyawe nka ikidashinga , cyuje ubucucu , nta shingiro , ntigikwiye kandi cyuzuye amateshwa .
Komeza ubibe inyigisho zawe , ariko twe Abanya - Uganda turi maso " " " " .
I shudder at such a comment from a whole minister if this is your true handle .
I find your opinion devoid of reason , idiotic , preposterous , ludicrous , farcical and complete balderdash .
Pontificate , but we Ugandans are watchful .
— Hon Mukasa F Mbidde ( @ Mbidde ) January 23 , 2020
Mateke yashimangiye urwango rwe ku Rwanda
Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Minisiteri ya Ububanyi na Amahanga ya u Rwanda , Amb Olivier Nduhungirehe , yasubije Mateke ko ibikorwa bye ari ibya ubushobotoranyi kurushaho , ku buryo yagakwiye guceceka .
Ati " Umuntu wafatiwe mu cyuho arimo gutegura ibitero bya iterabwoba byishe abantu 14 bigakomeretsa abandi 16 mu gihugu cya abaturanyi , akwiye guceceka akareka abadipolomate ba nyabo bagakora akazi kabo .
Someone who was caught red - handed , while organising a deadly terror attack that killed 14 people and wounded 16 others in a neighbouring country , should have the decency to remain silent and allow real diplomats to do their job .

Olivier J .
Nduhungirehe ( @ onduhungirehe ) January 23 , 2020
Mu biganiro biheruka guhuza intumwa za u Rwanda na Uganda mu Ukuboza 2019 , u Rwanda rwagaragaje uburyo Mateke yari inyuma ya abarwanyi bagabye igitero i Musanze ahazwi nko mu Kinigi kigahitana abaturage 14 .
Ubwo bari ku ngingo zijyanye na uko Uganda ifasha imitwe yitwaje intwaro , Nduhungirehe yatanze urugero rwa igitero cyabaye mu ijoro rishyira ku itariki ya Kane Ukwakira aho abarwanyi ba umutwe wa RUD Urunana bateye mu Kinigi .
Mu iperereza ryakozwe , hari ibikoresho byafashwe birimo na telefoni zigendanwa na ubuhamya bwatanzwe na abafashwe , byagaragaje uruhare rwa Uganda muri iki gitero .
Nduhungirehe ati " Ibyo byose bigaragaza ko uwari uyoboye icyo gitero ari uwitwa Philemon Mateke akaba Umunyamabanga wa leta ya Uganda ushinzwe ubutwererane bwa akarere .
Byagaragajwe na za telefoni na ubuhamya bwatanzwe na abafashwe .
" Hari na uwitwa Nshimiye wiyita Governor ushinzwe ibikorwa byihariye muri RUD Urunana , atuye hariya mu Karere ka Kisoro na umuryango we , byagaragaye ko akunda kujya muri Kivu ya Amajyaruguru ahitwa Benza gutegura ibitero kandi ko ariwe wakoranaga bya hafi na Philemon Mateke .
Urwo ni urugero rumwe natanze ariko hari na izindi nyinshi twatanze zigaragaza ko bagikomeza guha urubuga abaturwanya .
Si ubwa mbere Mateke avuzwe mu bikorwa bigamije guhungabanya umutekano wa u Rwanda , kuko byavuzwe ko mu Ukuboza 2018 yakoranyaga inama yahuje FDLR na RNC i Kampala , ngo bategure igikorwa gihuriweho cya gisirikare ku Rwanda nka uko La Forge Bazeye na Theophile Abega bari bahagarariye FDLR muri iyo nama babivuze nyuma yo gufatirwa ku mupaka wa Bunagana basubiye mu birindiro muri RDC .
Dusubize amaso inyuma
Ubushotoranyi bwa Uganda ku Rwanda si ubwa vuba , ndetse mu myaka yashize havuyemo ugukozanyaho kwabereye muri Repubulika ya Demokarasi ya Congo , byavuyemo intambara ya Kisangani yarangiye RPA itsinze ingabo za Uganda , ibintu byababaje Uganda ku rwego rukomeye .
Gutsindirwa i Kisangani byatumye abaturage ba Uganda na Inteko Ishinga Amategeko bashyira igitutu ku bushobozi bwa Museveni no ku hazaza he .
Muri kwa gusuzugura u Rwanda , abadepite barakariye Museveni ariko baguma no kwikoma Guverinoma ya u Rwanda , nka uko raporo ya International Crisis Group yo mu 2000 ibigaragaza .
Icyo gihe Museveni yabonye ko uburyo bwo gucubya abaturage be ari ukwibasira RPA mu magambo atyaye .
Mu ijambo ryo ku wa 30 Kanama 1999 , Museveni yabaye nka uwikura mu bibazo abyegeka ku bandi .
Ati " Icyo nabasobanurira ni uko abavandimwe bacu muri RPA batabashije gukura ngo bamenye uko ibintu bimwe na bimwe bikorwa .
Bumva ko kunyura iya bugufi hano na hariya bizabageza ku ntego yabo .
Ikindi maze iminsi numva ni uko RPA yashatse kwigarurira Congo ariko ko turimo kubakoma imbere .
" Ku ruhande rwacu dushishikajwe no kongerera ubushobozi abanye - Congo ariko bigaragara ko Abanyarwanda batabyishimiye .
Ariko nubwo twaba tubangamiye imigambi bafite muri Congo , ni gute bumva ko batugabaho ibitero ngo birangirire aho ?
Ni ukureba hafi cyane .
Igisirikare cya Uganda nticyigeze cyakira inshuro cyakubiswe na Abanyarwanda , aho bumvaga ko ishema na icyubahiro byabo byahungabanyijwe , ibitangazamakuru byanzika ko UPDF yatsinzwe ndetse abasirikare bayo barenga 200 bagapfa .
Raporo ya ICG ivuga ko hahise hatangira inama za ibanga i Kampala zikitabirwa na abasirikare bakiri mu mirimo na abasezerewe , ngo " bashakishe uburyo bwo kwihimura ku cyo bafataga nka ubugambanyi bwa abari bafatanyije na u Rwanda .
Hari aho yagize iti " Abasirikare bakuru mu Ngabo za Uganda bavuga ko umubano na u Rwanda utazongera na rimwe kuba nka uko wahoze nyuma ya ibyabereye i Kisangani .
Nyuma ya imyaka myinshi , Uganda ikomeje gushotora u Rwanda aho yakunze gufunga abaturage barwo ibashinja ubutasi , ibintu itigeze igaragariza ibimenyetso ishingiraho , ndetse nta na abagejejwe mu rukiko ngo ibyaha bibahame , ariko bagiye bakorerwa iyicarubozo rikomeye , bamwe bakarekurwa baragizwe intere , bamwe bibaviramo ubumuga abandi babira ubuzima .
Inkuru wasoma : Uruhare rwa Minisitiri Mateke wa Uganda mu gitero cyagabwe mu Kinigi
Raporo yo mu 2000 : Uko impuguke zasesenguye ishwanyagurika rya umubano wa u Rwanda na Uganda
Museveni yiyemeje gushyira iherezo ku bibazo biri hagati ya Uganda na u Rwanda ; Yaba koko akomeje ?
Imvugo ya Museveni yo gushyira iherezo ku bibazo biri mu mubano na u Rwanda niyo yasorejeho umwaka wa 2019 , gusa usesenguye neza wagira amakenga na ugushidikanya .
Imvugo ya Museveni yo gushyira iherezo ku bibazo biri mu mubano na u Rwanda niyo yasorejeho umwaka wa 2019 , gusa usesenguye neza wagira amakenga na ugushidikanya .
Ni inshuro ya kabiri abanyarwanda bashobora kuba bagira amakenga na icyizere gike ku kuba Uganda yakemura ibibazo imaze igihe itera mu mubano wayo na u Rwanda .
Ubwa mbere hari ubwo hasinywaga amasezerano ya Luanda , ubwa kabiri byashingirwa ku magambo ya Museveni asoza umwaka wa 2019 .
Mu butumwa yashyize ku rukuta rwe rwa Twitter mbere ya uko twinjira mu mwaka mushya wa 2020 , Museveni yavuze ko yakiriye intumwa ye Ambasaderi Adonia Ayebare uherutse mu Rwanda afite ubutumwa bugenewe Perezida Kagame ku mubano wa ibihugu byombi .
Museveni yavuze ko Ayebare na Perezida Kagame bagiranye ibiganiro byiza ndetse ko mu gihe cya vuba , hagiye gufatwa imyanzuro ishyira iherezo ku bwumvikane buke bumaze igihe kinini mu mubano wa ibihugu byombi .
Ati " Vuba aha , impande zombi zigiye gufata imyanzuro ihamye mu guhosha umwuka mubi .
Ndabizeza ko Uganda izakora ibyo isabwa mu gushyira mu buryo umubano mwiza wa ibihugu byombi .
Ndashimira Perezida Kagame , abavandimwe bacu ba abanyarwanda na abaturage ba Uganda .
Ambasaderi Adonia Ayebare wakiriwe muri Village Urugwiro ku mugoroba wo ku Cyumweru tariki ya 29 Ukuboza 2019 .
Asanzwe ari Intumwa ihoraho ya Uganda mu Muryango wa Abibumbye i New York .
Ubutumwa bwanyujijwe ku rukuta rwa Twitter rwa Ibiro bya Umukuru wa Igihugu bwavugaga ko ubutumwa Ambasaderi Ayebare yari afite , " butanga icyizere " " " " mu gukemura ibibazo bimaze igihe mu mubano wa ibihugu byombi .
Mu kiganiro yagiranye na RBA kuri uyu wa Kabiri , Perezida Kagame yavuze ko iyo ntumwa yari i Kigali mu bikorwa bimaze igihe bigamije gushaka umuti wa ibibazo , ariko ko nyuma ya ibiganiro ikiba ari ingenzi ari ishyirwa mu bikorwa rya imyanzuro yabyo .
Ati " Kuvuga rero ngo haje intumwa icyizere cyabonetse , ntabwo nibwira ko ari uko nabivuga , njye navuga ko iyo ari indi ntambwe ikomeje guterwa muri ubwo buryo bwo gushakisha icyatuma ikibazo icyo aricyo cyose cyaba gihari gishobora gukemuka kandi nyine ibyo biva mu bantu mu kuvugana , kuganira .
Ubutumwa bwa Museveni ku kibazo cya Uganda na u Rwanda biragoye ko umuntu yabwizera 100 % , ngo yishyiremo ko hari ikigiye gukorwa kuko mu gihe yabwandikaga , ibimenyetso bigaragaza ibihabanye na ibyo yavugaga .
Mbere na mbere ubwo hasinywaga amasezerano ya amahoro ya Luanda , abanyarwanda baketse ko ikibazo gikemutse , ko nta na umwe uzongera guhohoterwa ari muri Uganda ndetse ko na abafungiyeyo bagiye kurekurwa .
Gusa siko byagenze , kuko byakomeje nka uko byari bisanzwe , abafungwa bagafungwa , abakorerwa iyicarubozo rigakomeza bakajya bajugunywa ku mipaka bagizwe intere .
Ni nako Uganda kandi yakomeje umubano wayo na imitwe igamije guhungabanya umutekano wa u Rwanda irimo RNC na FDLR ndetse irinangira ubwo yasabaga kubahiriza amasezerano Museveni yasinywe .
Ibi nibyo byatumye intumwa za u Rwanda na Uganda zinanirwa kumvikana mu biganiro biheruka kubera i Kampala .
Mu gihe Museveni yandikaga ko umuti ugiye kuboneka , ku rundi ruhande ikinyamakuru Red Pepper cyari kimaze gutangaza inkuru ivuga ko abanyarwanda 200 bagamije ibikorwa bya iterabwoba binjiye muri Uganda mu mugambi wo guhungabanya iki gihugu mu bihe bya iminsi mikuru .
Muri iyo nkuru havugwamo ko bamwe muri abo bakora ibikorwa bya iterabwoba batawe muri yombi na Urwego rushinzwe Umutekano imbere mu gihugu , ISO .
Red Pepper isanzwe iterwa inkunga na umuvandimwe wa Museveni , Salim Saleh ni kimwe mu binyamakuru byakunze gusiga u Rwanda icyasha no guha rugari abarwanya ubutegetsi bwarwo .
Umwe mu bo cyanditse ko ari abanyarwanda bagamije ibikorwa bya iterabwoba kuri Uganda ni uwitwa Abdul Razak Subwanone , umunyarwanda uba muri Uganda aho acuruza ibyuma bya imodoka akura i Dubai .
We na undi munyarwanda witwa Edward Nsenga ucuruza telefoni bafashwe na ISO mu mukwabu watwawemo abagera kuri 200 .
Ikigaragaza umugambi wa Uganda udahinduka ni uko aba banyarwanda bakuwe mu bandi na mbere ya uko bagezwa imbere ya ubutabera ngo biregure , ubu bivugwa ko bafunzwe mu buryo bunyuranyije na amategeko na ISO mu nzu zayo za ibanga ahitwa Kyengera , bashinjwa kuba intasi ziturutse mu gihugu cya igituranyi .
Perezida Kagame mu kiganiro yagiranye na Televiziyo ya u Rwanda , yavuze ko bitumvikana uburyo abanyarwanda bafatirwa muri Uganda bitwa intasi kuko bamwe muri bo batanafite ubwo bushobozi ahubwo baba bashaka imibereho kimwe na abandi .
Ati " Ibyo kugera ahantu igihugu gihiga abanyagihugu ba abaturanyi kuri ubwo buryo ntabwo byasobanuka .
Abandi bakavuga ngo abo baba bagiyeyo , baba bagiye gutata , gutata iki kirimo abana , kirimo abagore , abagabo , kirimo abantu batazi kwandika no gusoma , abantu bari aho bashakisha uko biberaho nka uko abanya - Uganda benshi bari hano .
Perezida Kagame yavuze ko u Rwanda rutigeze rukora nka umuturanyi warwo ngo rutangire ruhige abaturage ba Uganda .
Ibimenyetso byagiye bijya hanze nyuma ya ibyo abayobozi ba Uganda bakunze kuvuga ku mubano na u Rwanda , bigaragaza ko abantu bakwiye kwishima mu rugero , ntibizere ko ikibazo cyakemutse ahubwo bagategereza bibaye .
Ni uko ubutumwa bwa Museveni bwakwakirwa .
Nta cyahindutse ku muburo wahawe Abanyarwanda ku kujya muri Uganda – Min .
