Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Minisiteri ya Ububanyi na Amahanga , Amb .
Nduhungirehe Olivier , yanyomoje amakuru yakwirakwijwe ko u Rwanda rwafunguriye amarembo abaturage barwo bashaka kujye muri Uganda , ashimangira ko nta cyahindutse ku muburo rwabahaye ku kaga bashobora kugirira muri icyo gihugu .
Ibi Nduhungirehe yabitangaje kuri uyu wa 3 Mutarama 2020 yifashishije Twitter , avuguruza inkuru yatangajwe na ikinyamakuru Chimp Reports cyo muri Uganda cyanditse ko U Rwanda rworoheje uburyo bwo kunyura ku mupaka bajya muri Uganda .
Ati " Iki ni ikindi gihuha cya @ Gilespies na ikinyamakuru cye [ sinshobora no kubibara byose ] .
Umuburo u Rwanda rwahaye abaturage barwo bifuza kujya muri Uganda ntiwahindutse .
Nta kintu cyigeze gihinduka guhera muri Gashyantare 2019 .
Ayo makuru Chimp reports yayatangaje ivuga ko yaganiriye na abantu batandukanye bagiye bambuka bakajya muri Uganda , babanje " gutanga impamvu zumvikana .
Muri Gashyantare 2019 nibwo u Rwanda rwafashe umwanzuro wo gusaba abanyarwanda kutajya muri Uganda kubera umutekano wabo , nyuma ya uko bigaragaye ko abajyayo na ababayo bashimutwa , bafungwa ndetse bagakorerwa iyicarubozo bazira ubusa .
Icyo kinyamakuru gitangaje ibi nyuma ya uko Perezida Museveni , ubwo yasozaga umwaka ushize wa 2019 , yavuze ko igihugu cye cyiteguye gukora ibyo gisabwa mu gushyira iherezo ku bibazo biri mu mubano wa Uganda na u Rwanda , ariko abasesenguzi bakomeza kugira amakenga na ugushidikanya .
Museveni kandi yavuze ko yakiriye intumwa ye Ambasaderi Adonia Ayebare , wakiriwe muri Village Urugwiro ku mugoroba wo ku Cyumweru tariki ya 29 Ukuboza 2019 afite ubutumwa bugenewe Perezida Kagame ku mubano wa ibihugu byombi .
Museveni yavuze ko Ayebare na Perezida Kagame bagiranye ibiganiro byiza ndetse ko mu gihe cya vuba , hagiye gufatwa imyanzuro ishyira iherezo ku bwumvikane buke bumaze igihe kinini mu mubano wa ibihugu byombi .
Ati " Vuba aha , impande zombi zigiye gufata imyanzuro ihamye mu guhosha umwuka mubi .
Ndabizeza ko Uganda izakora ibyo isabwa mu gushyira mu buryo umubano mwiza wa ibihugu byombi .
Ndashimira Perezida Kagame , abavandimwe bacu ba abanyarwanda na abaturage ba Uganda .
Ku wa 31 Ukuboza Perezida Kagame yavuze ko iyo ntumwa yari i Kigali mu bikorwa bimaze igihe bigamije gushaka umuti wa ibibazo , ariko ko nyuma ya ibiganiro ikiba ari ingenzi ari ishyirwa mu bikorwa rya imyanzuro yabyo .
Ati " Kuvuga rero ngo haje intumwa icyizere cyabonetse , ntabwo nibwira ko ari uko nabivuga , njye navuga ko iyo ari indi ntambwe ikomeje guterwa muri ubwo buryo bwo gushakisha icyatuma ikibazo icyo aricyo cyose cyaba gihari gishobora gukemuka kandi nyine ibyo biva mu bantu , mu kuvugana , kuganira .
Ubwo hasinywaga amasezerano ya amahoro ya Luanda mu mwaka ushize , abanyarwanda baketse ko ikibazo gikemutse , ko nta na umwe uzongera guhohoterwa ari muri Uganda ndetse ko na abafungiyeyo bagiye kurekurwa .
Gusa siko byagenze , kuko byakomeje nka uko byari bisanzwe , abafungwa bagafungwa , abakorerwa iyicarubozo rigakomeza bakajya bajugunywa ku mipaka bagizwe intere .
Uganda kandi ntiyahagaritse umubano wayo na imitwe igamije guhungabanya umutekano wa u Rwanda irimo RNC na FDLR ndetse irinangira ubwo yasabwaga kubahiriza amasezerano Museveni yasinye .
Ibi nibyo byatumye intumwa za u Rwanda na Uganda zinanirwa kumvikana mu biganiro biheruka kubera i Kampala .
Kelly akurikiranyweho gukoresha uburaya umwana wa umukobwa
Ubushinjacyaha bwo muri Leta ya Minnesota bukurikiranye umuhanzi R Kelly ku byaha byo gukoresha ibikorwa bya uburaya umukobwa utarageza imyaka ya ubukure .
Ubushinjacyaha bwo muri Leta ya Minnesota bukurikiranye umuhanzi R Kelly ku byaha byo gukoresha ibikorwa bya uburaya umukobwa utarageza imyaka ya ubukure .
Umuvugizi wa ubushinjacyaha mu Karere ka Hennepin , Mike Freeman niwe watangaje ibyaha bishinjwa Robert Sylvester Kelly wa imyaka 50 .
Freeman yavuze ko ibyo R .
Kelly ashinjwa byabaye muri Nyakanga 2001 nyuma ya aho umwana wa umukobwa wari ufite imyaka 17 yamusabye ko yamusigira isinya ya urwibutso [ autograph ] .
Kelly ngo yasinyiye uyu mwana anamuha nomero ze za telefone .
Ubwo yamuhamagaraga yamusabye kumusanga kuri hoteli yari arimo , yakirwa na umugabo yaketse ko bari uwo mu itsinda rye .
Iki kirego kivuga ko R .
Kelly ubwo yahuraga na uyu mwana baganiriye umwanya muto , ubundi amwishyura $ 200 kugira ngo amubyinire .
Bemeranyije kuri ayo mafaranga , maze amukuramo imyenda nyuma nawe akuramo iye , agenda amukorakora uko yamubyiniraga .
Umubano wabo warakomeje R .
Kelly amuha itike yo kujya mu nyanya ya icyubahiro mu gitaramo cyari kigenewe abarengeje imyaka 18 , yinjirayo atishyuye cyangwa ngo yerekane na indangamuntu ye .
Uyu mukobwa yagannye inzego za ubutabera muri Mutarama uyu mwaka , ubwo ibindi birego byari bikomeje kwisuka kuri R .
Umuvugizi wa ubushinjacyaha , Mike Freeman yavuze ko bibabaje kuba R Kelly yarakoresheje ubwamamare bwe mu kwangiza abana ba abakobwa .
Ntabwo haramenyekana igihe R Kelly azagerezwa imbere ya urukiko rwo muri Leta ya Minnesota kuko hari izindi nkiko nazo zimukurikirana .
Umwe mu bunganira R Kelly yahakanye ibyaha ashinjwa avuga ko ari abashaka gukomeza kurunda ibyaha ku mukiriya wabo .
Yashidikanyije niba koko baranahuye nubwo mu bivugwa ngo atumva icyaha cya ubusambanyi kirimo .
Ikirego cyo muri Leta ya Minnesota kije nyuma ya ibindi byinshi uyu muhanzi yagiye ashinjwa muri Leta zitandukanye , aho akurikiranyweho ibyaha bijyanye no gusambanya abana bataruzuza imyaka ya ubukure .
Ubushinjacyaha bwa Leta za Illinois na New York bwamushinjije gushaka abagore ajyana mu buraya , kwishyura abantu kugira ngo bamuhishire no gutanga amafaranga kugira ngo asubizwe amashusho yamugaragazaga asambana na abana batarageza ku myaka ya ubukure .
Muri Gashyantare yahakanye ibyaha 10 yashinjwaga na ubushinjacyaha bwo muri Leta ya Illinois arafungwa aza kurekurwa atanze ingwate ya ibihumbi $ 100 .
Kuri ubu R .
Kelly azitaba urukiko rwo muri Chicago tariki 4 Nzeri aho azaburana ku byaha byo gufata amashusho ari gusambana na abakobwa bane bari bataruzuza imyaka ya ubukure mu 1998 .
Abagore na abakobwa bihariye 95 % bya Abanyarwanda bahuye na icuruzwa rya abantu
Ubushakashatsi bushya bwagaragaje ko icuruzwa rya abantu ari ikibazo gihangayikishije u Rwanda na Isi muri rusange , ndetse ko bukorerwa umubare munini wa urubyiruko rwiganjemo abakobwa kurusha abahungu .
Ubushakashatsi bushya bwagaragaje ko icuruzwa rya abantu ari ikibazo gihangayikishije u Rwanda na Isi muri rusange , ndetse ko bukorerwa umubare munini wa urubyiruko rwiganjemo abakobwa kurusha abahungu .
Ubushakashatsi ku kibazo cya icuruzwa rya abantu mu Rwanda bwamuritswe kuri uyu wa 19 Nyakanga 2019 , bwakozwe n Umuryango Never Again Rwanda hagati ya 2017 na 2018 .
Imibare yatanzwe na Urwego rwa abinjira na abasohoka yagaragaje ko mu Rwanda ahanini abacuruzwa bahanyuzwa bajyanwe mu bindi bihugu , kuko abahakurwa ari bo bake .
Mu bantu 515 bacurujwe higanjemo Abarundi , bagera kuri 323 bingana na 62 .
Harimo kandi Abanye - Congo 77 ( 15 % ) , Abanyarwanda 70 ( 13 .
6 % ) na abantu 45 ( 8 .
7 ) bo mu bindi bihugu .
Urebeye ku gitsina , abagore na abakobwa bari 400 ( 77 .
67 % ) naho aba igitsina gabo ari 115 ( 22 .
Ku ruhanda rwa u Rwanda , ubu bushakashatsi bwerekana ko mu bacurujwe , 95 .
24 % ari aba igitsina gore , 87 .
01 % ni urubyiruko naho 18 .
8 % bari munsi ya imyaka 18 .
Ubushakashatsi bwerekanye ko inzira Abanyarwanda banyuzwamo bajyanwa gucuruzwa ari izegereye imipaka nko mu Turere twa Rusizi , Burera , Nyagatare , Rubavu , Gicumbi na Kirehe .
Ibihugu bakunze kujya gucururizwamo harimo Arabie Saoudite ( 38 .
55 % ) , Uganda ( 37 .
35 % na Kenya ( 7 .
23 % ) , Mozambique , Tanzania , Malawi , Afurika ya Epfo , Zambia , Malaysia , Omar , Qatar , Kuwait Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Abarabu na ahandi .
Abakoze ubushakashatsi basobanuye ko abajya gucuruzwa akenshi babeshywa ko bagiye guhabwa akazi keza , kwiga na ibindi , bagezwayo ntibabibone cyangwa bagashorwa mu bikorwa bya urukozasoni na ibindi bigira ingaruka ku buzima bwabo .
Zimwe mu mpamvu zituma ubucuruzi bwa abantu bwiyongera harimo imibereho mibi , ubukene , ubushomeri mu rubyiruko , igitutu cya umuryango , ababeshywa ko bagiye kurihirwa amashuri na ibindi .
Umuyobozi wa Never Again , Dr Nkurunziza Ryarasa Joseph , yavuze ko hakenewe ubuvugizi kugira ngo abanyarwanda bamenye uko icuruzwa rya abantu rikorwa , ingaruka rigira na uko baryirinda .
Ati " Icyo dusaba ni ukugira ngo habeho ihanahana rya amakuru cyane cyane mu kigo gishinzwe abinjira na abasohoka , Urwego rwa Ubugenzacyaha , Polisi na urw Ubutabera , kuko kugira ngo iki kibazo gikemuke ni uko abantu baba bafite amakuru yuzuye .
Yasabye ko hakwiye no kujyaho ikigo gifasha mu isanamitima ku bantu bahungabanyirijwe mu icuruzwa rya abantu , abateshejwe ishuri bagafashwa kurisubiramo .
Umuyobozi wa Ishami rishinzwe ubutabera mpuzamahanga muri Minisiteri ya Ubutabera , Umurungi Providence , yavuze ko icuruzwa rya abantu atari ikibazo cya u Rwanda gusa ahubwo cyugarije Isi yose .
Ati " Ibivuye muri ubu bushakashatsi bizadufasha gushyira muri gahunda no guteganye icyakorwa mu rwego rwo kurwanya icuruzwa rya abantu .
Umurungi yavuze ko imiryango ariyo ifite uruhare rukomeye kuko bigaragara ko abajya gucuruzwa bajyanwa na abo bafitanye isano .
Ishyirahamwe mpuzamahanga ryita ku murimo ( ILO ) riheruka kugaragaza ko abantu barenga miliyoni 24 .
9 barimo abagabo , abagore na abana bashowe mu bucuruzi bwa abantu mu 2017 .
Umuzimu wasaritse abarwanya u Rwanda uzorohera Twagiramungu na Rusesabagina bihuje ?
Umunyapolitiki utavuga rumwe na Leta ya u Rwanda , Faustin Twagiramungu , yihuje ku mugaragaro na Ihuriro MRCD , riyobowe na Paul Rusesabagina , mu bufatanye bwiswe ubwo guhuza imbaraga mu kurwanya ubutegetsi bwa u Rwanda , hakoreshejwe inzira zose .
Umunyapolitiki utavuga rumwe na Leta ya u Rwanda , Faustin Twagiramungu , yihuje ku mugaragaro na Ihuriro MRCD , riyobowe na Paul Rusesabagina , mu bufatanye bwiswe ubwo guhuza imbaraga mu kurwanya ubutegetsi bwa u Rwanda , hakoreshejwe inzira zose .
Amasezerano hagati ya ishyaka RDI Rwanda Rwiza , rya Twagiramungu na MRCD , igizwe na RRM ya Nsabimana Callixte Sankara , ufungiwe mu Rwanda , PDR Ihumure na CNRD Ubwiyunge ya Gen .
Irategeka Wilson wiyomoye kuri FDLR , yasinywe kuri uyu wa Kabiri i Bruxelles mu Bubiligi .
MRCD niyo Nsabimana Sankara , yari abereye umuvugizi na Visi Perezida wa kabiri .
Ifite ishami rya gisirikare ryitwa FLN , ikaba ari umutwe wa iterabwoba wagabye ibitero mu Majyepfo ya u Rwanda , bigahitana abaturage icyenda , 19 bagakomereka ndetse na imitungo myinshi igasahurwa indi ikangizwa .
Uwari umuvugizi wa uyu mutwe Nsabimana yumvikanye ku maradiyo ya BBC na VOA , na imbuga nka YouTube yigamba ibyo bitero , avuga ko ari ibya FLN iyobowe na Habimana Hamada .
Umusesenguzi mu bya politiki ya ibiyaga bigari , akaba impuguke mu itangazamakuru , Albert Rudatsimburwa , avuga ko kuba Twagiramungu yahisemo kwihuza ku mugaragaro na umutwe wa iterabwoba , MRCD , bisobanura ko atakiri muri politiki gusa ahubwo yinjiye no mu iterabwoba .
Avuga ko Twagiramungu yifuza guhirika ubuyobozi bwa u Rwanda ariko akaba yarabuze uko abigenza , bityo akaba yihuje na abandi babimazemo iminsi , ariko ku bwe iri huriro ntacyo ryageraho .
Ati " Ni amagambo gusa , ni ukuvugira kuri radiyo hirya no hino ariko ntacyo bivuze , nta na ikintu gifatika gihari " " " " .
Inenge kuri Rusesabagina na Twagiramungu
Rudatsimburwa avuga ko aba bagabo bose bafite inenge izingiye ku bushobozi buke butuma ubufatanye bwabo ntacyo bwageraho .
Mbere ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , Paul Rusesabagina yari umuntu usanzwe , yavukiye i Murama ya Gitarama ku wa 15 Kamena 1954 , ariko nyuma yagiye gutura i Bruxelles mu Bubiligi na Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Uburyo abantu bamuzi bwahinduwe cyane na filimi Hotel Rwanda yamukinweho nka uwarokoye abantu 1268 muri Hôtel des Mille Collines , abayobejwe nayo batangira kumuhundagazaho ibihembo kugeza kuri Presidential Medal Award of Freedom , yahawe na Perezida George W .
Bush wa Amerika mu Ugushyingo 2005 .
Rudatsimburwa agaruka ku mateka ya Rusesabagina akavuga ko atari umunyapolitiki , ahubwo yari umuntu wakoreraga hôtel akaza kugirwa igitangaza na filimi bityo agatangira kwibaza ko uwo muntu uri muri filime ari we kandi atari we .
Ati " Ni ukwisumbukuruza gusa kandi nta bushobozi afite uretse ko yabonye abantu bamwumva kuko bibaza ko ari wawundi wo muri filime ariko mu banyarwanda nta kintu avuze , ntacyo bamuziho uretse ibyo ahwihwisa mu maradiyo gusa na ahandi " " " " .
Akomereza kuri Twagiramungu , akavuga ko we yabaye umunyapolitiki kuva kera ariko ubu akaba ari umunyapolitiki wasigajwe inyuma na amateka , kuko uko u Rwanda rwateye imbere ntacyo bimubwiye akiri mu bya kera yari yaramenyereye ku ngoma zindi .
Mu nteruro imwe Rudatsimburwa ati " Nta hantu bishobora kubageza kuko nta ruhare bafite no ku banyarwanda " " " " .
Umuzimu wasaritse abarwanya u Rwanda bazawukira ?
Si ubwa mbere abatavuga rumwe na ubutegetsi bwa u Rwanda , bifatanyije bagashyiraho amahuriro ngo bahuze imbaraga bagere ku mugambi wabo ariko bikarangira bishwanyutse ntacyo bigezeho .
Ingero ni nyinshi cyane .
Ntawe utazi uko RNC ya Kayumba Nyamwasa yashwanyutse .
Uguterana amagambo hagati ya Dr Théogène Rudasingwa na Kayumba Nyamwasa , bari bahuriye muri RNC , mbere ya uko bacikamo ibice , byatumye na abo bizezaga ibitangaza bacika intege .
Aha niho havutsemo amashyaka atemewe mu Rwanda arimo na RRM ya Nsabimana , nayo yacitsemo ibice mbere ya ifatwa rye kubera ubwumvikane buke , gusuzugurana no kutemera uburyo abayobozi bishyira mu myanya .
Hari kandi na amatiku hagati ya abasivili na abahoze mu gisirikare .
RRM igizwe na abantu ahanini bavuye mu Rwanda bahunze ibyaha bakoze cyangwa andi makosa .
Twagiramungu ubwe nawe yashinze ihuriro rya amashyaka atavuga rumwe na Leta ya u Rwanda ( CPC ) , ryari rigizwe na FDLR , UDR , RDI , CNR , na PS Imberakuri , igice cya gatatu .
Abarigize baje kunaniranwa nawe bamushinja igitugu .
Muri rusange iyo ugiye kwitegereza umuzimu wasaritse aya mashyaka , ni ugupingana no kuryana , buri wese arwanira kuba ku isonga no guhabwa ibyubahiro bya umukuru wa ishyaka cyangwa uzayobora igihugu igihe bageze ku butegetsi .
Rudatsimburwa yongeraho izindi mpamvu abashinga aya mahuriro ntacyo bageraho ari uko ikibagenza ari inyungu zabo bwite , kwitwaza iturufu ya amoko na intege nke basanganywe .
Ati " Ubundi mu mvugo zabo usanga nka Rusesabagina afite akantu ko kuzana ibya amoko , RNC usanga ikibazo bafite ari umuyobozi mukuru .
Ni uguhuza gusa ariko ubona ko bafite intege ziri hasi cyane , bakibaza ko guhuza imbaraga byatuma bazamura urwego rwa imbaraga zabo ariko akenshi ubona ko kuba ari abantu bifitiye gahunda zabo bwite , birangira akenshi bashwanye kuko hari aho batazahuza " " " " .
Rudatsimburwa akomeza agira ati " Ntibafite ingengabitekerezo ifatika yatuma babona na imfashanyo , birangirira aho .
Mu bya ukuri ( Twagiramungu ) , aba ashaka kwihuza na abandi kuko nta bushobozi na buke afite , niwe wenyine wibaza ko izina gusa rikurura ariko hashize imyaka 25 uriya muntu ntabwo azwi , ntawe yakurura , nta na benewabo yakurura .
Avuga ko FPR Inkotanyi yashobotse bitewe no guhuza mu bitekerezo byari bifitiye akamaro abanyarwanda bose yaba abari impunzi na abandi bari mu gihugu babaho mu buzima bwa ingoma ya Habyarimana .
Ati " Niyo mpamvu FPR yakuruye abantu na ubushobozi bwa abo bantu .
Ikindi harimo na abantu bafite ubunararibonye bwa uko niba byanze muri politiki hari uko babikora bakurikije ubushobozi bwo gushoza intambara .
Abandi ntabyo bafite , akenshi banafashwa na abantu bashaka kugirira u Rwanda nabi ariko nabo kubera aho u Rwanda rugeze nta ngaruka yindi bifite uretse gukerereza iterambere ryabo " " " " .
U Budage ntibwakwicarana na abahoze ari aba - Nazi
Twagiramungu na abandi bafatanyije kurwanya ubutegetsi bwa u Rwanda , ntibasiba kumvikana bavuga ko bazagaruka mu Rwanda habaye ibiganiro .
Rudatsimburwa asanga ntaho ibi biganiro byahera kuko u Rwanda rudaheza kandi ruhora rushishikariza impunzi na abari mu mahanga gutaha , bityo na abo bashaka ibiganiro bakwiye gutaha niba hari icyo bahindura ku cyerekezo cya u Rwanda , bakagikora .
Icyakora avuga ko harimo na abantu kuganira na bo byagereranywa no kuvuga uti u Budage bwa iki gihe bukwiye kwicarana na abahoze ari aba - Nazi cya gihe cya Hitler kuko abuzukuru babo babisabye .
Abo Twagiramungu yifatanyije nabo harimo abashyiriweho impapuro mpuzamahanga zibata muri yombi , Rudatsimburwa avuga ko nta kabuza uyu musaza agomba gufatwa nka umuterabwoba kuko kuba yifatanyije nabo bivuze ko yemera ibyo bakora .
Kugeza ubu ikibazwa ni ikidasanzwe ubufatanye bwa MRCD na RDI Rwanda Rwiza buzanye ku buryo bidatinze abantu batazumva iri huriro ryatewe na umuzimu wasaritse abarwanya u Rwanda , nabo bagacikamo ibice .
Bigenda bite iyo umudepite ageze mu Nteko ntatange ibitekerezo ?
Iyo havuzwe Umudepite nta kindi cyumvikana mu matwi ya benshi , uretse uwo umuturage aba yaritoreye ngo amuhagararire mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko atanga ibitekerezo bya impinduka zikenewe , ni nayo mpamvu babita intumwa za rubanda .
Iyo havuzwe Umudepite nta kindi cyumvikana mu matwi ya benshi , uretse uwo umuturage aba yaritoreye ngo amuhagararire mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko atanga ibitekerezo bya impinduka zikenewe , ni nayo mpamvu babita intumwa za rubanda .
Mu nshingano za intumwa za rubanda harimo gutora amategeko abareye abaturage , kugenzura ibikorwa bya guverinoma , kwemeza abayobozi runaka , hari na ibihugu baba bafite inshingano zo gutora abakuru ba igihugu .
Nubwo baba baratowe na abaturage ngo babahagararire , mu bihugu bimwe birimo na u Rwanda , usanga hari abaturage bavuga ko baheruka babatora ntibazongere kubaca iryera cyangwa bagatora amategeko atabanogeye .
Tariki 19 Nzeri 2018 ubwo yakiraga indahiro za Abadepite , Perezida Paul Kagame , yavuze ko bagomba kujya begera abaturage , bakabikora nka uko babigenza iyo babashakamo amajwi .
Ati " Igihe mwese mwamaze mwiyamamaza hirya no hino mu gihugu , mwabonanye na Abanyarwanda , uko mwabagezeho mubashakaho amajwi ariko bizakomeza kubageraho mubasanga , mufatanya gukemura ibibazo bafite .
Mu nteko habamo imirimo myinshi irimo kwiga imishinga ya amategeko , kuyisuzuma , kuyitangaho ibitekerezo na ibindi .
Akenshi abaturage bamenya ubushobozi bwa umudepite batoye bitewe na uburyo abavuganira , ibitekerezo atanga ku ngingo zitandukanye zizanwa mu Nteko , kubasura na ibindi .
Hari ibihugu umudepite ugeze mu nteko ntiyongere kumvikana ku ngingo zibangamiye abaturage agaragazwa , byaba na ngombwa akaba yahagarikwa .
Nko mu 2018 muri Kenya , ikinyamakuru The Standard cyasohoye urutonde rwa abadepite batajya bavuga mu Nteko .
Havugwaga ko hari Abadepite bicara mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko , ntibabe batekereza umushinga wafasha abaturage ahubwo icyo bakora , bikaba gusa gushyigikira imishinga yavuzwe na abandi .
Iki kibazo cyazamuwe na bamwe mu badepite muri iki gihugu , batangiye bijujuta bavuga ko hari bagenzi babo bahitagamo kwisohokera , mu gihe abandi babaga bageze ku ngingo zikomeye zo gutorerwamo amategeko .
Depite Justin Bedan Njoka Muturi yabwiye abanyamakuru ati " Ntabwo nishimye kuko hari abadepite bagenzi bacu usanga birirwa bavuga ko bishimira ibyo bagezeho mu nteko , mu gihe mu bya ukuri ntacyo bigeze bakora .
Yavuze ko hari bamwe usanga batagaragara mu gihe barimo gushaka gushyiraho itegeko runaka , nyamara nyuma ryajya gutorwa ugasanga batangiye kwijujuta kandi batarigeze bagaragara mbere ngo baritangeho ibitekerezo .
Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Kenya yavuze ko 70 % bya abayigize wasangaga nta jambo bafata ngo batange ibitekerezo , bamwe muri bakaba baravugaga ko babiterwa na uko babaga bakiri bashya mu nshingano .
Mu Rwanda bihagaze gute ?
Kugeza ubu Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya u Rwanda igizwe na Imitwe ibiri , Umutwe wa Abadepite na Sena .
Kuva tariki 19 Nzeri 2018 umutwe wa abadepite wabonye abadepite bashya 80 bari muri manda izageza mu 2023 , naho kuva mu Ukwakira 2019 hatowe abasenateri , kugeza ubu bose hamwe ni 26 .
Nubwo bitoroshye kumenya imikorere ya buri mudepite , iyo uganiriye na bamwe muri aba bakubwira ko nubwo hari bamwe batavuga , ngo ni uburenganzira bwabo cyane ko nta tegeko rihari ribategeka kuvuga .
Depite , Dr Frank Habineza , usanzwe ari na Umuyobozi wa Ishyaka Riharanira Demokarasi no kurengera ibidukikije ( DGPR ) , yabwiye IGIHE ati " Abadepite bose bafite uburenganzira bungana imbere ya amategeko , nta mudepite kandi ubuzwa kugira igitekerezo atanga , buri wese afite uburenganzira bwa iminota ingana , burya umuntu kutavuga ni umutimanama we .
Dr Habineza avuga ko ubwabo nka abadepite badashobora kwicara ngo banenge umudepite runaka utajya utanga ibitekerezo , keretse wenda bikorewe mu mutwe wa politike aturukamo .
Ati " Ibyo byakorwa na amashyaka kuko buri shyaka rigira umuhwituzi .
Nka ubu twe nubwo turi babiri mu nteko ariko dufite umuhwituzi ari we njye , ubu mfite uburenganzira bwo gukurikirana umudepite wo mu ishyaka ryanjye iyo nta gitekerezo atanga cyangwa ntacyo avuga , ndamubaza nti ese wowe ko mbona utavuga wabaye iki ?
na ahandi ubwo ni uko babikora .
Dr Habineza avuga ko ku giti cye intego yajyanye mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko , ni uko buri gihe aba yiteguye kugira icyo yavuga gifasha umuturage .
Ati " Nta tegeko ryacaho ntarivuzeho kandi na mugenzi wanjye uba muri PAC agomba kureba uko amafaranga akoreshwa neza .
Kuva mu 2008 , Depite Nyirahirwa Veneranda ari mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya u Rwanda .
Yabwiye IGIHE ko abantu bashobora kwibeshya ko hari abadepite batavuga kandi iyo bari muri komisiyo batanga ibitekerezo .
Ati " Burya hari ibintu abantu batazi , mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko akazi gakorwa mu byiciro bitandukanye , hari imirimo ikorerwa muri komisiyo abadepite bakajya impaka ku mategeko , nyuma akazashyikirizwa inteko rusange , aha ni naho abaturage bose baba babyumva kuri radiyo .
" Hari abantu benshi usanga bazi ko dutangira akazi saa cyenda mu gihe harimo inteko rusange ariko siko biri .
Tuba twatangiriye muri komisiyo saa tatu ikageza saa sita , nyuma saa cyenda tukajya mu nteko rusange .
Nyirahirwa yavuze ko muri ayo matsinda , hari abantu usanga batanga ibitekerezo , ntibabitange mu nteko rusange .
Ati " Hari abadepite usanga bavuga cyane mu mirimo ya komisiyo , mu nteko rusange burya hageramo ibyasuzumiwe muri za komisiyo ugasanga mu nteko rusange ntavuze , ariko hari na abandi bavuga hose .
Icyakora , yemeza ko hashobora kuba na utatanga ibitekerezo aho hombi kuko iyo bageze mu nteko , nta muntu babwira ngo azagende avuge cyane .
Ati " Nta muntu uza kuguha amabwiriza ngo vuga , wanamara rwose imyaka itanu utavuze kandi nta wazabikubaza .
Depite , Sheikh Harerimana Musa Fazil , Visi Perezida ushinzwe Imari na Abakozi mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya u Rwanda umutwe wa abadepite , yabwiye IGIHE ko kugeza ubu nta tegeko rihana umudepite utatanze ibitekerezo , bityo ko utabikoze nta tegeko aba yishe .
Agira ati " Nta cyaha gihari iyo utavuze kuko inteko ikorera mu mategeko , iyaba hari itegeko rivuga ngo niba utavuze umwaka wose bigenda gutya , icyo gihe twaryubahiriza ariko noneho ubwo nta tegeko rihari , ubwo nabyo biremewe , ikitabujijwe na amategeko kiba cyemewe .
Yavuze ko gahunda nyinshi mu nteko zibera muri za komisiyo , ku buryo hari abadepite benshi baba baratanze ibitekerezo , byagera mu nteko rusange akumva nta mpamvu yo kongera kuvuga .
Sheikh Harerimana yavuze ko bari kwiga ku buryo na ibiganiro byabeye muri za Komisiyo byajya bica kuri radiyo kugira ngo abaturage babashe gukurikirana ibikorwa bya Inteko na imikorere ya abadepite batoye .
Ati " Twamaze kuganira na ubuyobozi bwa RBA ngo turebe ukuntu na impaka zabereye muri Komisiyo , rimwe na rimwe zajya zinyura kuri radiyo Rwanda Inteko , ibyo turimo kubiganira bizadutwara amafaranga kandi ntaraboneka ariko niwo murongo dushaka kuzakoreramo .
Muri Uganda mu 2016 hasohotse urutonde rwa abadepite batajya bagaragara mu batanga ibitekerezo ku ngingo zireba abaturage , nyamara ari bo bahagarariye .
Mu badepite 427 bagize Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Uganda , 82 ngo nta jambo na rimwe bari bakavuze , 51 bari baravuze ijambo rimwe .
Mu 2011 , mu Bwongereza ibinyamakuru byasohoye urutonde rwa abadepite ba abanebwe .
Icyo gihe bashingiraga ku mubare wa inama abadepite bakoranaga na abaturage bo mu duce bahagarariye .
Baje gusanga Depite Sir Stuart Bell , yari amaze imyaka 14 mu Nteko , nta na rimwe arajya kugirana ibiganiro na abaturage bamutoye ngo yumve ibibazo byabo .
Sir Stuart Bell yaje kwitaba Imana mu 2012 afite imyaka 74 .
Baringa ku cyiswe " balkanisation " ya u Rwanda kuri RDC
Ijambo " balkanisation " rimaze kuba intero na inyikirizo mu mvugo ya abatavuga rumwe na ubutegetsi muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , kuva Perezida Félix Tshisekedi yatorerwa kuyobora iki gihugu .
Ijambo " balkanisation " rimaze kuba intero na inyikirizo mu mvugo ya abatavuga rumwe na ubutegetsi muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , kuva Perezida Félix Tshisekedi yatorerwa kuyobora iki gihugu .
Aba batifuza ko amahoro agaruka muri RDC , bakomeje guhimba ikinyoma ko u Rwanda rushaka kwigarura Uburasirazuba bwayo , bagamije kubiba urwango ku Banyarwanda na Abanye - Congo bavuga Ikinyarwanda .
Ibivugwa bisa no kureba filimi mbarankuru ya intambara zabaye mu kinyejana cya 20 mu Burayi bwa Amajyepfo , mu gace kiswe les Balkans , ubu kigizwe na ibihugu nka Bulgarie , Croatie , u Bugiriki , Roumanie , Slovénie , Albanie , Bosnie - Herzégovine , Kosovo , Macédoine ya Amajyaruguru , Monténégro , Serbie na Turquie ; byari byarigaruriwe na Ubwami bwa Abami bwa Ottoman , bukabiremamo uduhugu twinshi .
Igitandukanye muri uyu mwaka wa 2020 , ni uko ibi bivugirwa mu mihanda ya Kinshasa , aho ababiyoboye badakomoka muri Hongrie cyangwa Turikiya , bahora baririmba bati " balkanisation ntikabe kuri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
Mu Karere ka Ibiyaga Bigari , ijambo balkanisation ryatangiye kuhumvikana mu mpera ya imyaka ya 1990 , ubwo u Rwanda na Uganda byateraga icyahoze cyitwa Zaïre .
Abazayirwa bari bafite ubwoba ko abaturanyi babo babiri bagiye kwisubiza ibice bahoranye mbere ya uko Abanyaburayi bigabagabanya Afurika , ariko ntibyigeze biba .
Iyi mitekerereze yongeye kumvikana nyuma ya aho Joseph Kabila agiriye ku butegetsi mu 2001 .
Abamurwanya bavugaga ko afite inkomoko mu Rwanda kandi akaba afite uruhare mu mugambi mpuzamahanga wo gucamo ibice RDC , ibice byayo bya Uburasirazuba bikize ku mabuye ya agaciro bikomekwa ku Rwanda .
Kujya ku butegetsi kwa Félix Tshisekedi bigaragara ko ntacyo byahinduye .
Ubu iyo ntero na inyikirizo biri kuzamurwa na Ihuriro rya Amashyaka atavuga rumwe na Ubutegetsi ya Lamuka ririmo na Martin Fayulu watsinzwe mu matora ya umukuru wa igihugu aheruka .
Ibyavuye mu matora yari ahanganiyemo na Félix Tshisekedi byagaragaje ko yabaye uwa kabiri ariko Inama nkuru ya Kiliziya Gatolika muri RDC yo yavuze ko ariwe watsinze .
Yaba Lamuka na Kiliziya ntibigeze bemera ko Fayulu yatsinzwe .
Kubiba urwango
Ku ruhande rwe nka Perezida watowe , Félix Tshisekedi , yahisemo kuzahura umubano wa igihugu cye na u Rwanda , mbere yo kohereza umubare wa ingabo za Congo mu Burasirazuba bwa igihugu ngo zijye kurwanya imitwe yitwaje intwaro yahagize akarima kayo .
Ubu Ingabo za Congo ( FARDC ) zimaze kwigarurira ibice byinshi byari byarayogojwe na iyo mitwe ; ku buryo na iyo gahunda yo kwigarurira ibice bya RDC iyo iza kuba ihari , icyizere cyayo ubu kiri kubarirwa ku busa .
Abarwanya ubutegetsi mu RDC bahisemo kubiba urwango ku Banyarwanda na Abanye - Congo bavuga Ikinyarwanda kugira ngo bace intege umubano mwiza uri kubagarirwa hagati ya u Rwanda na RDC .
Ariko na ubundi abatavuga rumwe na ubutegetsi nta nyungu bafite mu kuba amahoro yagaruka muri RDC .
Mu myaka 25 ishize , ikibazo cya umutekano muke mu Burasirazuba bwa RDC cyafashije abari abami ba intambara kwigwizaho imitungo no kwinjira mu bikorwa bya politiki cyangwa igisirikare .
Urugero rwa hafi ni umutwe wa ADF - Nalu ukomoka muri Uganda , wigize nka ba kavukire , ukaba uterwa inkunga na uwahoze ari umunyapolitiki ku butegetsi bwa Kabila , Mbusa Nyamwisi , ubu wituriye muri Uganda .
Uyu Mbusa Nyamwisi yanahoze ari mu ihuriro Lamuka , nyuma aza kwitandukanya naryo .
Mu gihe RDC iri kugerageza kwivana mu ntambara imaze imyaka irenga 20 , cyane cyane hashingiwe ku mibanire myiza na abaturanyi bo mu Burasirazuba , abarwanya ubutegetsi bakomeje kubiba urwango ku Banyarwanda , ariko si na Abanyarwanda , ahubwo ni abo bita ko bakomoka mu bwoko bwa Abatutsi na Abanye - Congo bavuga Ikinyarwanda mu rwego rwo guca intege umubano mwiza hagati ya u Rwanda na RDC .
Igitangaje ni uko imvugo ya " balkanisation " ari ikirego kidafite ishingiro .
Mu gihe Umuhuzabikorwa wa Ihuriro rya abatavuga rumwe na Ubutegetsi , Lamuka , wanahoze ari Minisitiri wa Intebe , Adolphe Muzito , yagaragaje mu buryo bweruye ko ashaka gutera u Rwanda byanashoboka bakarwomeka kuri RDC ; uyu ni na we ushinja u Rwanda kugambirira kwigarurira ibice bya igihugu cye .
Nubwo bashinje Joseph Kabila gufatanya na u Rwanda muri uwo mugambi akiri ku butegetsi , ubu bakaba bageze kuri Félix Tshisekedi , ubwabo bigeze gukorana na u Rwanda mu bihe byatambutse .
Ibi bigaragaza ikinyoma gikomeye kandi cyumvikana .
Byongeye kandi muri gahunda ya ubuhahirane busesuye mu Muryango wa Afurika Yunze Ubumwe na ubusabe bwa RDC bwo kwinjira mu Muryango wa Afurika ya Uburasirazuba ( EAC ) , bigaragara ko kwigarurira ubutaka bwa ikindi gihugu byaba ari amafuti .
Aho gutanga ibisubizo bya ibibazo nyabyo Abanye - Congo bafite ubu nka ubushomeri , kutagira inganda zihagije no kwangiza ibikorwa remezo , kwangirika kwa ibikorwaremezo na ibindi bishobora gusunikira urubyiruko rudafite akazi kwishora mu byaha cyangwa kwinjira mu mitwe yitwaje intwaro , [ … ] abatavuga rumwe na ubutegetsi muri RD Congo bahisemo gushyushya imitwe ya abaturage babo bakoresheje
imitekerereze ishaje .
Gukoma mu nkokora u Rwanda cyangwa ikindi gihugu cyo mu Karere ntibyongera umusaruro ; ntibirema imirimo kandi ntibinazana ubukungu .
Abavuga " balkanisation " ntibigeze bakandagiza ikirenge ku mupaka uhuza u Rwanda na RDC , umwe mu inyurwaho na benshi ku Isi ; ntibigeze byibura banumva ubuhamya bwa abagore bahakorera ubucuruzi , bahambukira inshuro nyinshi ku munsi bashaka imibereho .
Ubukungu nyabwo bwa RDC ni abaturage bayo .
Muri Afurika yose , umutungo kamere ubyarira inyungu ibigo mpuzamahanga biwubyaza umusaruro na abayobozi bamwe na bamwe bahabwa utuvungukira na icyizere cyo kubarindira ubutegetsi bwabo .
Ku ngoma ya Félix Tshisekedi , RDC ifite amahirwe yo guhinduka igihugu kirimo amahoro kandi gitera imbere ; ariko kugira ngo ibyo bigerweho birasaba ko bigirwamo uruhare na impande zitandukanye zigize ubukungu nyabwo bwa RDC .
Gushaka kwihorera ku Rwanda barugira umwanzi bahuriyeho ni igitekerezo gifutamye cyabafasha kwihuza ariko ntibirambe .
Iyi nkuru yanyuze mu kinyamakuru Jeuneafrique , ni ibitekerezo bwite bya umwanditsi Gatete Nyiringabo , umunyamategeko akaba na inzobere mu burenganzira bwa muntu .
Minisitiri Mbabazi yatangije imurikabitabo rya 2020 , akomoza ku nyungu ziri mu bwanditsi
Minisitiri ya Urubyiruko na Umuco , Rosemary Mbabazi , yatangije imurikabitabo rya Igihugu mu buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga rizakorerwa ku mbuga za internet , asaba Abanyarwanda kugira umuco wo gusoma no kwandika kuko ariwo nkingi ikomeye ya iterambere rya igihugu .
Minisitiri ya Urubyiruko na Umuco , Rosemary Mbabazi , yatangije imurikabitabo rya Igihugu mu buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga rizakorerwa ku mbuga za internet , asaba Abanyarwanda kugira umuco wo gusoma no kwandika kuko ariwo nkingi ikomeye ya iterambere rya igihugu .
Iri murikabitabo ryateguwe na Minisiteri ya Urubyiruko na Umuco ndetse na Ikigo cya Igihugu gishinzwe Ishyinguranyandiko na Serivisi za Inkoranyabitabo , RALSA .
Muri uyu mwaka rifite insanganyamatsiko igira iti " Twandike ibitabo , bimenywe , bigurishwe mu Isi ya ikoranabuhanga " " " " .
Minisitiri Mbabazi yagize ati " Gusoma no kwandika ni inkingi ikomeye ya iterambere rya igihugu cyacu , niyo mpamvu leta ya u Rwanda ishyira imbaraga mu gukundisha abanyarwanda uwo muco , hategurwa ibikorwa bitandukanye harimo ubukangurambaga bwo gusoma no kumurika ibitabo .
" Igikorwa cyo kumurika ibitabo ni igikorwa ngarukamwaka guhera mu 2017 kandi uko gikozwe hari intambwe iterwa mu ruganda rwa ibitabo , aho usanga abitabira kumurika bagenda biyongera .
Yavuze ko ibitabo byandikwa bikwiriye kuba bijyanye na igihe kandi bifite ireme ku buryo bigira icyo byungura ababisoma .
Yavuze ko iri murikabitabo ari irya abanyarwanda bose , ko bakwiye kuryitabira kugira ngo umuco wo gusoma no kwandika bawugire uwabo .
Yagize ati " Igitabo ntigisanza kandi na ubumenyi ntibusaza , ni uburyo bwiza bwo kugeza ubumenyi ku bariho na abazaza tubagezaho ubumenyi na ibitekeerzo byubaka .
Iri murikabitabo rya igihugu 2020 riri mu buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga rizakorwa kuva tariki 15 Kamena kugeza tariki 15 Kanama uyu mwaka .
Iri murikabitabo rya Igihugu mu buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga rizakorerwa ku mbuga za Internet zitandukanye .
Ushobora kurigeraho unyuza aha .
Imurikabitabo ni igikorwa ngarukamwaka gitoza umuco wo gusoma no kwandika bya umwihariko mu bana .
Dutembere kuri Stade ya mbere yubatswe mu Rwanda yakiniweho na Umwami Rudahigwa
Stade ya Rwinkwavu ni yo yubatswe bwa mbere mu Rwanda , iherereye mu Murenge wa Rwinkwavu mu Karere ka Kayonza , yubatswe iruhande rwa umuhanda .
Hirya yayo gato hahoze hacukurwa amabuye ya agaciro ndetse amateka yerekana ko ari ho hambere yacukuwe mu Rwanda na Ababiligi .
Stade ya Rwinkwavu ni yo yubatswe bwa mbere mu Rwanda , iherereye mu Murenge wa Rwinkwavu mu Karere ka Kayonza , yubatswe iruhande rwa umuhanda .
Hirya yayo gato hahoze hacukurwa amabuye ya agaciro ndetse amateka yerekana ko ari ho hambere yacukuwe mu Rwanda na Ababiligi .
Ni stade abenshi bitirira Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa [ Charles Leon Pierre ] watwaye u Rwanda kuva mu 1931 kugeza 1959 , bivugwa ko yakundaga kureba aho bakinira umupira wa amaguru cyane ko nawe yajyaga acishamo akawukina .
Umunyamakuru wa IGIHE yatembereye kuri iyi stade aganira na abakuru barimo Musafiri Kabemba watangiranye na ubucukuzi bwa amabuye ya agaciro mu Rwanda , uyu kandi yari ahari ubwo iyi stade yatangiraga kubakwa .
Kabemba Musafiri ufite imyaka 102 yabwiye IGIHE ko igitekerezo cyo kubaka iyi stade cyagizwe na umuzungu wa umubiligi nyuma yaho benshi mu basore bakoreshwaga mu bucukuzi bwa amabuye ya agaciro i Rwinkwavu , mu masaha ya ikigoroba basoje akazi batagiraga ikindi kintu kibahuriza hamwe .
Amateka agaragaza ko ubucukuzi bwa amabuye ya agaciro mu Rwanda bwatangiye mu 1930 - 1931 ubwo gasegereti yavumburwaga mu birombe bya Rwinkwavu na Rutongo .
Ababiligi ngo bazanye abakongomani 300 barimo na Musafiri kugira ngo bafatanye na abandi basore ba abanyarwanda kuyacukura .
Uko Stade ya Rwinkwavu yubatswe
Kabemba Musafiri avuga ko iyi stade ijya kubakwa yari ahari ariko ko atibuka neza umwaka , gusa ngo byaturutse ku muzungu wa umubiligi wari umuyobozi mukuru wa abacukura amabuye ya agaciro ndetse akanaba inshuti ya Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa .
Uyu muzungu yazanye umukino wa umupira wa amaguru nka uburyo buzajya bufasha abacukuzi ba amabuye ya agaciro kwidagadura mu gihe bavuye muri iyo mirimo .
Ati " [ Stade ] yayishinze hafi mu 1940 , yashinzwe na umuzungu wa umubiligi wakundaga gukina umupira wa amaguru , Umwami Rudahigwa yarahazaga cyane nawe akishimira kubona uwo mukino , bigera aho bayishyiraho igipangu kiyizengurutse hose , twayikiniragaho nimugoroba no kucyumweru , ni nabwo Umwami yakundaga kuhaza .
" Yari stade nziza cyane ifite igipangu , hari ikipe ya abacukura amabuye ya agaciro hakaba na ikipe ya abazungu , hari na andi makipe yadusuraga ku cyumweru aturutse ahandi hantu hose bacukuraga amabuye , amakipe yacu yose yabaga afite abajyanama .
Uko abakinnyi bahembwaga
Kabemba Musafiri yavuze ko abakinnyi batahabwaga amafaranga ahubwo bahabwaga inka zabaga zatanzwe na Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa .
Ati " Abakinnyi beza bahabwaga inka hamwe na abatsinze ibitego , babanzaga kubatekera neza bakahaba ibiryo byinshi birimo inyama ubundi bakajya mu kibuga bamara gutsinda nanone bakababagira inka , undi witwaye neza nawe akagabirwa inka akayitahana " " " " .
Umwami Rudahigwa yacishagamo agakina umupira
Kabemba Musafiri yavuze ko Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa yari umwe mu bakundaga gukina no kureba uko bakina umupira wa amaguru , ngo rimwe na rimwe nawe yajyaga acishamo akawukina nubwo bitari cyane .
Ati " Hari ubwo yazaga inaha akizihirwa nawe agakina , yajyaga mu ikipe ya abacukuraga amabuye hamwe na abandi batware , abazungu ba ababiligi nabo bakajya mu ikipe yabo ubundi bagakina gusa ntabwo byabagaho kenshi .
Kabemba yavuze ko guhera mu 1960 kuzamura imipira yaberaga kuri iki kibuga yatangiye kugabanyuka ndetse abaturage batangira gusenya urupangu bakitwarira amabuye kugira ngo bayubakishe .
Abaturage barifuza ko iyi Stade yavugururwa
Bamwe mu baturage bo mu Murenge wa Rwinkwavu bavuze ko bifuza kubona iyi stade yavuguruwe ikajya iberaho imikino ikomeye , abandi basabye ko hashyirwa ibimenyetso byerekana ko ariyo stade yubatswe bwa mbere mu Rwanda .
Bankundiye Alphonsine yagize ati " Turifuza ko hashyirwa ikimenyetso cyerekana ko ari yo stade ya mbere yubatswe mu Rwanda , binabaye byiza bayivugurura natwe tukajya tuharebera imipira ikomeye .
Buregeya Emmanuel we yagize ati " Leta ikwiriye kubungabunga iyi stade na inzu ziri hano zubatswe icyo gihe zabagamo abazungu ba ababiligi , byose bikwiriye kwitabwaho ku buryo bishyirwa mu mateka ya igihugu cyacu .
Umuyobozi wa Ikigo cya Igihugu cya ingoro ndangamurage za u Rwanda , Amb Robert Masozera , yabwiye IGIHE ko bari kubarura ahantu hatandukanye hirya no hino mu gihugu hari ibyiza nyaburanga ku buryo nyuma hazakurikiraho kubibyaza umusaruro .
Ati " Rwinkwavu hari mu hantu twitayeho kimwe na ahandi hirya no hino mu gihugu , tumaze kubona ahantu harenga 600 mu Rwanda hose kandi ntiturarangiza gukora urutonde , aho tumaze gukorera ubushakashatsi no kwandika ni 145 , iriya stade ntabwo irazamo turacyareba niba akarere kabyifuza kuko tugendera ku byifuzo bya Akarere .
Yavuze ko nyuma yo kuhabarura aribwo hazakurikira icyiciro cyo gushaka uburyo hakwitabwaho hakavugururwa hakabyazwa umusaruro .
Kugeza ubu kuri iyi stade hakinirwaho ikipe ikina mu cyiciro cya kabiri ya Akagera , ariko hakunda no kubera inama zihuriza hamwe abaturage benshi .
RDC : Leta irashaka kugura inzu ya Papa Wemba ikagirwa inzu ndangamuco
Guverinoma ya Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo yatangaje ko iri kwiga uburyo yagura inzu yahoze ari iya umuhanzi wa icyamamare Jules Shungu Wembadio uzwi nka Papa Wemba , igahindurwa inzu ndangamuco .
Guverinoma ya Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo yatangaje ko iri kwiga uburyo yagura inzu yahoze ari iya umuhanzi wa icyamamare Jules Shungu Wembadio uzwi nka Papa Wemba , igahindurwa inzu ndangamuco .
Byatangajwe mu byemezo bya inama ya abaminisitiri yateranye kuri uyu wa Gatanu iyobowe na Perezida Félix Tshisekedi .
Papa Wemba yapfuye tariki 24 Mata 2016 ubwo yari ku rubyiniro mu iserukiramuco Femua , Festival des Musiques Urbaines da Anoumabo ryaberaga muri Côte da Ivoire .
Mu nama ya abaminisitiri , Perezida Félix Tshisekedi yasabye Minisiteri ya umuco na ubugeni kureba niba Leta yagura inzu yahoze ari iya Papa Wemba , ikagirwa inzu ndangamuco izaba irimo na studio itunganya umuziki .
Itangazo rigira riti " Umukuru wa Igihugu nyuma yo kubona ko uwo muhanzi wa icyamamare , yamenyekanishije cyane umuziki wa Congo , yasabye Guverinoma kugurira Leta inzu ye yashyizwe ku isoko , igasanwa ku buryo bubereye inzu ndangamuco .
Papa Wemba yapfuye amaze imyaka 50 akora umuziki .
Yafatwaga nka umwami wa injyana ya Rumba muri Repubilika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
