Sinzatesha agaciro uwakansubije , igitabo kivuga amateka ya Abanyarwandakazi na uburyo basubiranye ijambo
Umwanditsi Hategekimana Richard , Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Urugaga rwa Abanditsi mu Rwanda agiye kumurika igitabo gishya yise Sinzatesha Agaciro Uwakansubije kijya mu mizi amateka ya abagore mu Rwanda .
Umwanditsi Hategekimana Richard , Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Urugaga rwa Abanditsi mu Rwanda agiye kumurika igitabo gishya yise Sinzatesha Agaciro Uwakansubije kijya mu mizi amateka ya abagore mu Rwanda .
Gikubiyemo amateka ya abagore mu Rwanda rwa mbere ya ubukoloni , guteshwa agaciro mu bukoloni na nyuma ya aho ndetse na uburyo bongeye gusubizwa agaciro nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Iki gitabo cya amapaji asaga 250 kizamurikwa ku mugaragaro kuwa Gatanu tariki 15 Ugushyingo 2019 muri Kigali Convention Centre .
Hetegekimana usanzwe yandika ibitabo bitandukanye , yavuze ko iki gitabo kigaragaza neza uburyo mbere ya umwaduko wa abazungu abanyarwandakazi bagiraga ijambo mu miyoborere na ubuzima bwa igihugu , bikavaho mu gihe cya ubukooloni , muri Repubulika ya mbere na iya kabiri , bakongera kwisanga mu buzima bwa igihugu ubwo Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yahagarikwaga na Ingabo za FPR Inkotanyi zari
ziyobowe na Perezida Paul Kagame .
Muri iki gitabo atangamo ingero za uburyo abagore bagize uruhare mu rugamba rwo kubohora igihugu na umusanzu bakomeje gutanga nyuma ya Jenoside ngo u Rwanda rwongere kuba igihugu cyubashywe .
Aganira na IGIHE , Hategekimana yavuze ko yanditse icyo gitabo , kugira ngo yibutse abagore ko ubwisanzure na ijambo bafite hari aho byaturutse , bityo ko bakwiriye kurinda icyo gihango bafitanye na Perezida Paul Kagame .
Ati " Mbere ya ubukoloni , Abanyarwandakazi bari bafite agaciro , bagagaragara mu buzima bwa igihugu ariko kuva mu bukoloni kugeza mu 1994 agaciro kabo barakambuwe .
Imiyoborere myiza ya Perezda Paul Kagame na umuryango FPR Inkotanyi yasubije agaciro Abanyarwandakazi , bafata iya mbere mu kugirana igihango na Perezida wa Repubulika , biyemeza ko agaciro yabahaye batazigera bakamutesha .
Yakomeje agira ati " Ni igitabo kigaragaza amateka ya umugore , kikamwereka aho ari , aho ava na aho yerekeza kikanamwibutsa igihango afitanye na Perezida wa Repubulika Paul Kagame .
Muri iki gitabo , ijambo rya ibanze ryasinywe na Madamu Ingabire Marie Immaculée uyobora Umuryango Transparency International Rwanda .
Hategekimana avuga ko yabikoze kugira ngo igitabo cye koko kigire umwihariko no kugaragaza uruhare rwa abagore mu iterambere .
Igitabo Sinzatesha Agaciro Uwakansubije kibaye icya gatatu cya Hategekimana Richard , cyabanzirijwe na ibirimo " Intwari Mpinduramatwara Paul Kagame " " " " na ikindi cyitwa " Urubyiruko dufitanye igihango " " " " .
Amafoto mpangano ya abami batwaye u Rwanda imyaka 870 na abagabekazi babo
Hashize imyaka 929 ( 1091 - 2020 ) u Rwanda rubaye igihugu gihamye gituwe na bene Kanyarwanda .
Amateka ya igihugu cyacu muri iki kinyagihumbi gishize ni maremare bitavugwa , dore ko rwayobowe na abami 28 bafatanyije na abagabekazi 27 kuva mu 1091 kugera mu 1961 mu gihe cya akaga kiswe revolisiyo , ubwo ingoma ya cyami yasimburwaga na Repubulika .
Hashize imyaka 929 ( 1091 - 2020 ) u Rwanda rubaye igihugu gihamye gituwe na bene Kanyarwanda .
Amateka ya igihugu cyacu muri iki kinyagihumbi gishize ni maremare bitavugwa , dore ko rwayobowe na abami 28 bafatanyije na abagabekazi 27 kuva mu 1091 kugera mu 1961 mu gihe cya akaga kiswe revolisiyo , ubwo ingoma ya cyami yasimburwaga na Repubulika .
Hifashishijwe ibisigo bya Abasizi bisingiza Abami na ingoma zabo ndetse na Abacurabwenge bari abarinzi ba amateka na intekerezo za igihugu , hiyongereyeho na Abiru bari abanyamabanga na abagaragu ba ingoma , hakusanyijwe amateka ya u Rwanda kuva mu ntango yarwo ubwo Gihanga I Ngomijana yashyiragaho imfatiro za igihugu kugera ubwo Ingoma cya cyami yasimburwaga na Repubulika .
Mu bakoreye mu ngata Gihanga I Ngomijana harimo ubuvivi bwe Ndoba watwaye u Rwanda ahasaga mu wa 1213 kugera 1246 arangwa na ibitekerezo bihanitse mu bumenyi mu bya ibidukikije , inyamaswa na urusobe rwa ibinyabuzima .
Muri make Ndoba yari afite ubuhanga karemano muri siyansi , dore ko ari nawe dukesha ibirangamuryango nko kuba Abasinga barangwa na Sakabaka , Abashambo bakarangwa na Intare , Abenengwe bakarangwa na Ingwe mu gihe Abega barangwa na Ibikeri , byose ni we tubikesha .
Hari kandi na Ruganzu Bwimba watwaye u Rwanda kuva mu 1312 kugera mu 1345 wabaye imbimbuzi mu ndwanyi zaranze amateka ya u Rwanda mu guhirimbanira ubuhangange bwa igihugu .
Niwe wagabye igitero cya mbere atera Gisaka yashakaga gusibanganya u Rwanda we arayitanga arayitera .
Ni we dukesha kurwanira ishyaka igihugu , cyane cyane mu guhangana na abagomera umurage wa Gihanga wa igihugu gisangiwe .
Nta na uwarenza ingohe Cyilima Rugwe , watwaye u Rwanda kuva mu 1345 kugera mu 1378 , umutekerereza wa ubutabera bwunga mu mateka ya u Rwanda .
Ni we washyizeho Inkiko za Umuryango , iza Abunzi na iza Gacaca agena na uko ibihano bizajya bitangwa ku bagomye .
Yashakaga ko u Rwanda ruba igihugu kizira icyaha , abyubakira ku guhana igihango nka uburyo bwo gukumira icyaha kitaraba .
Nta na uwakwibagirwa Ruganzu II Ndoli , watwaye u Rwanda kuva mu 1510 kugera mu 1543 wari indwanyi karundura , wadukanye amatwara yo guhangana na amahanga adakunda u Rwanda akayagusha ruhabo , akarwagura kurusha abandi bami bose dore ko yarwometseho ibihugu icyenda .
Hari inzobere kandi muri dipolomasi Mutara Semugeshi , watwaye u Rwanda mu 1543 kugera mu 1576 , ni we mwami dukesha politiki ya mbere ya ububanyi na amahanga , yubatse kandi imiyoborere ihamye mu kwegereza ubuyobozi abaturage aho yashyizeho inzego zisaga 75 nka Intebe ya Abasizi , Abatware ba Ubutaka , Abatware ba Inyambo , Intebe ya Abahaditsi ( abavuzi ba amatungo - vétérinaire ) , Intebe ya Abahoryo (
Agronome ) , Intebe ya Abamotsi ( abari bashinzwe itangazamakuru rya ibwami ) na izindi .
Ni we washyizeho uburyo bwa imisimburanire ya Abami ku ngoma bijyanye na inshingano zabo nka aho Umwami Mutara yabaga ashinzwe kwagura ubworozi bwa inka yakurikirwaga na Kigeli wari umwami wa intambara , Mibambwe wari ushinzwe uburumbuke , Yuhi wari umwami usigasira amahoro bityo bityo .
Ntitwakwibagirwa na abandi nka Cyilima Rujugira ( 1675 – 1708 ) , wadukanye intero ya u Rwanda rutera rudaterwa , Yuhi Gahindiro ( 1746 - 1802 ) wazanye gahunda za ubugiraneza nka Girinka na Kigeli Rwabugili ( 1859 - 1895 ) wacecekesheje ibihugu byashakaga kwiyomora ku Rwanda .
Mu mateka ya Isi na ibihangange byayibayemo nka Abami ba u Rwanda , benshi baburiwe irengero , amasura yabo aribagirana kuko nta buryo bwariho bwo gufata amafoto no kuyashyingura ariko ibikorwa byabo bikaba bikibukwa kuko basize imusozi amavugwa ya ibikorwa bihanitse .
Umushakashatsi ku mateka ya u Rwanda , Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , yahereye aho maze akusanya ibitekerezo bya ubuzima bwaranze aba bakurambere , yifashisha abahanga mu gushushanya bahanga amafoto ya abami ba u Rwanda , cyane umwami wa mbere wafotowe yari Kigeli Rwabugili mu 1894 , abandi bamubanjirije ntawe uzi neza uko basaga .
Aya mafoto mpangano ya Abami ba u Rwanda na Abagabekazi babo , yakozwe na umunyabugeni Mugisha Paul wize ku Nyundo , yashyizwe hanze bwa mbere mu gitabo " Intwari za Imbanza , zubatse u Rwanda rugahamya igitinyiro " " " " cyasohotse muri Gicurasi 2018 .
Uko ubumenyi na ikoranabuhanga bigenda bikwira ku Isi yose rero , abahanga bagiye bitabaza inyurabwenge maze bakazimbura amasura ya abo bantu babayeho mu myaka ibihumbi kugira ngo bajye bayifashisha mu kubavuga ibigwi no kubagiraho icyitegererezo , ariko batari za baringa cyangwa umuntu udashobora kubonwa .
Ni muri urwo rwego hariho amafoto ya Yesu , Mariya , Yozefu , intumwa za Yesu 12 , Musa wavanye Abayisiraheli mu Misiri na abandi .
Nsanzabera avuga ko " Abo bagize ibikorwa bakora ku Isi na ubu bikiri intangarirwa , kandi amafoto yabo mpangano akaba yaramamaye mu buryo buhanitse ndetse ntashidikanyweho ko aribo koko .
Nka abakoze ishusho ya Yezu , icyo bakoze ni ukureba ku bikorwa bye , amateka yamuranze na imyitwarire ye ku Isi , barema amafoto mpangano ye kugira ngo buri wese ajye abasha kumubona mu buryo bugenekereje .
Mu gushushanya amafoto mpangano agenekereje ya abami ba u Rwanda , hagendewe ku bushakashatsi bushingiye ku bikorwa byabaranze , uruhererekane - mvugo rwa ibyabaye ku ngoma zabo , imishyingiranire ya umuryango wa abami ba u Rwanda na indi miryango migari ya Abanyarwanda , igenantekerezo ( Philosophie ) na imyitwarire yaranze Abami ba u Rwanda ndetse na ikigero cya imyaka ya ubukure mu iyimikwa ryabo .
Nsanzabera ati " Ese niba umwami runaka yarakoze ibikorwa bikomeye mu kubaka u Rwanda , aho ntiyasaga atya ?
Iyo ni imwe mu ngingo yitaweho cyane mu kugenekereza amafoto ya abami ba u Rwanda .
Kuko kenshi imirimo ya umuntu isa na isura ye , ikanahamya umutima wamuranze mu bihe byose .
Aya mafoto mpangano yanashingiye ku kigero cya ubukure cya abami na abagabekazi .
Hari aho atandukanye mu kigero cya ubukure bitewe na uko hari abagiye bimikwa bafite imyaka ibiri , abari abasore ba ibihame , abahawe ingoma bakiri ingimbi na abayihawe bakuze cyane .
Ni nako byagenze ku Bagabekazi kuko hari abagiye bapfakara bakiri bato , umwami agatanga , bakiri ibirongore , abandi ugasanga bari bakiri abagore ba amariza na ibindi .
Intego ya Nsanzabera ni uko ababyifuza bakoresha amafoto mpangano mu nyandiko na filime zirebana na amateka ya u Rwanda mu kwerekana amashusho ya abami na abagabekazi .
Aya mafoto ni uburiza bwa andi yaranze u Rwanda mu bihe bitandukanye , azasohoka mu bindi bitabo .
Umusozi wa Kigali wasabirwagaho kugira Umutima wa u Rwanda
Abanyarwanda ba kera bahoranye umuhango mwiza wo gusaba Imana kugira Umutima wa u Rwanda .
Bakawusabira ku musozi wa Kigali bafataga nka igicumbi cya Umutima wa u Rwanda .
Ese Abanyarwanda ba ubu bawusabira he ?
Cyangwa se ntawo bagikeneye ?
None se iyo Imbuto Foundation igarutse ku bidindiza " Ndi Umunyarwanda " " " " , aho si ibyo iba ishaka kumenya ?
Reka twumve icyo Abacukumbuzi ba ireme rya Umuco na Amateka bya u Rwanda babivugaho mu bushakashatsi bwabo .
Abanyarwanda ba kera bahoranye umuhango mwiza wo gusaba Imana kugira Umutima wa u Rwanda .
Bakawusabira ku musozi wa Kigali bafataga nka igicumbi cya Umutima wa u Rwanda .
Ese Abanyarwanda ba ubu bawusabira he ?
Cyangwa se ntawo bagikeneye ?
None se iyo Imbuto Foundation igarutse ku bidindiza " Ndi Umunyarwanda " " " " , aho si ibyo iba ishaka kumenya ?
Reka twumve icyo Abacukumbuzi ba ireme rya Umuco na Amateka bya u Rwanda babivugaho mu bushakashatsi bwabo .
Umusozi wa Kigali na Igenamigambi rya ingoma inye ( Ubu twagereranya na Vision 2020 cyangwa 2050 ) .
Kumenya icyerekezo cya u Rwanda mu myaka ijana ni byo bitwereka neza icyo ubusugire na ubwigenge bya u Rwanda gakondo byari bisobanuye , bityo na none tukabasha no gusobanukirwa neza na icyari ku mutima ( Philosophie ) wa abakurambere baremye u Rwanda bakarwubaka , bakarurwanira ndetse benshi bakanarupfira .
Aha tugiye kubona ko ubusugire na imibereho myiza ya Abanyawanda ku ngoma eshatu bwategurwaga na Abami bitwa Mutara na Cyilima mbereho nk imyaka ijana .
Nka uko musanzwe mubizi , mu mazina ya Abami atanu yasimburanaga mu bihe bine yakurikiranaga atya : Mutara , Kigeli , Mibambwe , Yuhi na Cyilima .
Aha biragaragara neza ko hagati ya Mutara na Cyilima hacagamo Ingoma eshatu mbere ya uko Cyilima atangiza ikindi cyiciro cya Abami .
Inshingano za abami Kigeli na Mibambwe zabaga ari ukwagura u Rwanda kuko ku ngoma eshatu zabaga zarabanje Inka na Abantu byabaga byaragwiriye bityo hakaba haragombaga kuboneka uruhumekero habayeho kwagura ubutaka bwa igihugu .
Yuhi yari ashinzwe imihango ya i Bwami cyane cyane Umuriro waho utarazimaga ukaba wararangaga ubusugire bwa igihugu .
Aha murumva ko Yuhi yari ashinzwe gutunganya ibijyanye na ubusugire bwa igihugu na ibijyanye na imiyoborere myiza kimwe na Iyobokamana kugira ngo abandi bami bane babone urufatiro rukomeye bazubakiraho .
Ubwo hari aho bitaniye cyane na ibikorwa ubu mu igenamigambi rirerire ?
Yaba Yuhi , Kigeli na Mibambwe uko ari batatu babanzirizwaga kandi bagaherukwa na Mutara cyangwa na Cyilima .
Musenyeri Kagame yaragaragaje ko mu Rwanda Ingoma eshatu zamaraga imyaka 100 kuko buri yose yari imyaka yegereye 33 .
Mbese ni ukuvugako kuva Mutara cyangwa Cyilima batanze kugera hongera kwima undi Mutara cyangwa undi Cyilima ; muri rusange habaga hashize imyaka 100 .
Umuhango wo kwaka Umutima wa Ingoma
Mutara na Cyilima bari Abami ba Inka kandi bagombaga kugira umuhango ukomeye wo mu Bwiru bakoraga ujyanye na icyerekezo cya u Rwanda mu ngoma eshatu zigiye gukurikiraho .
Niwo mu Bwiru bita " Inzira ya Ishora " " " " .
Hari umuhango baheragaho wo kuvugurura Ingoma za ibwami nka Kalinga , Cyimumugizi , Kiragutse na Mpatsibihugu .
Barebaga niba mu myaka hafi ijana ishize nta kibazo izo ngoma zagize kugira ngo bibaye ngombwa babe basisazura cyangwa se ngo bazisimbuze izindi .
Iyo basangaga izo ngoma zikiri nzima cyangwa bagasanga zigomba gusimbuzwa ; byanze bikunze bagombaga kuziha icyo bitaga " kuziha imitima mishya " " " " .
Iyo mihango yo kubonera Ingoma za ingabe imitima , imwe bayikoreraga ahitwa i Karama ku murwa wa Kigali hariya ku musozi wa Mont Kigali aho bavuga ko mu mirwa yose ya Abami umurwa wa Kigali ari wo wari Imfura ya imirwa yose ya Abami .
Aho i Karama bahajyaga baje kuhatora imitima ya Ingoma za ingabe arizo Cyiragutse , Cyimumugizi , Mpatsibihugu na Kalinga .
Mu gihe ingoma Kalinga yari Ingabe ya ubwami bwa u Rwanda , ziriya zindi uko ari eshatu zo bigaragara ko zari ingabe za buri mwami muri bariya Bami batatu bari hagati ya Mutara na Cyilima .
Bishoboka ko Cyiragutse ari ingabe ya Mibambwe maze Mpatsibihugu ikaba iya Kigeli bitewe na uko bose bari bashinzwe kwagura u Rwanda nka uko amazina ya izo ngoma abigaragaza .
Cyimumugizi ikaba ingabe ya Yuhi kuko ariwe wari ushinzwe imihango ya ubwami bwa u Rwanda nka uko na none izina ryayo ribigaragaza .
Ibi rero ubona bimeze nka bya bindi bya Umwami Salomo wo muri Bibiliya igihe yajyaga gutambira ku musozi wa Gabaon nka uko tubisoma mu 2 Abami 3 : 1 - 14 .
Ubwo Salomo yariho atamba Imana yaramubonekeye imubwira kuyisaba icyo ashaka maze Salomo ayisaba ubwenge kugira ngo agire ubushishozi bwo kuyobora ishyanga rya Israel .
Uriya muhango wa Salomo wo gusaba Imana ubwenge ( Umutima ) bari ku musozi muremure nka uwa Kigali urasa cyane na ibyo Abiru ba i Rwanda bakoraga bafatanije na Umwami nka uko tugiye kubibona .
Iyo rero Abiru na abandi banyamihango bageraga ku murwa wa Kigali babaga bazanye : Umutsobe wa isugi , Umukobwa wa isugi na Umwenenyabirungu wa isugi , bakazana amata , inzoga na imbuto bagatereka aho .
Hanyuma rero bendaga ya mata na za nzoga bagakozamo icyuhagiro icyarimwe bakuhagira igiti cya umurama ( ngo gitere uburame ) babaga bazanye maze Umutsobe mukuru agapfukama agasenga avuga aya magambo :
Gahorane Imana Kigali .
Tuje kwenda imitima ya ingoma Ngo Umwami mu Rwanda agire umutima Ingoma mu Rwanda zigire umutima Abagabo mu Rwanda bagire umutima Abagore mu Rwanda bagire umutima Inka mu Rwanda zigire umutima U Rwanda rwose rugire umutima .
Aha murabona ko niba Ingoma ya Ingabe ya u Rwanda ari yo Kalinga iyo ibonye Umutima ugereranya Ubwenge na Ubushishozi , Umwami wayimye nawe aba abonye umutima .
Na none Ingoma za Abami ari zo Cyimumugizi , Kiragutse na Mpatsibihugu iyo zibonye umutima , ni ubutegetsi bwa imyaka ijana bwa Abami Kigeli , Mibambwe na Yuhi burangwa na umutima .
Uwo mutima rero ni wo ugera mu baturage no mu nka .
Ibyo birangira ari u Rwanda rwose rubonye umutima kugira ngo rubone kuba umurame .
Ibyo bimeze nka uko Umwami Salomo yasabye ubwenge Imana ikamushima ikamubwira ko izamuha na ibyo atasabye nko kurama , ubukire , amahoro no kunesha abanzi bitewe na uko yahisemo neza .
Ibyo Imana yamusezeranyije byose bimeze nka ibyo Abanyarwanda bizeraga kubona bamaze kubona Umutima wa Ingoma .
Dore uko uduce twa ubwiru dukurikira tubivuga :
Uri umurame umwami abe umurame Ingoma mu Rwanda zibe umurame Abagabo ba i Rwanda babe umurame Abagore ba iRwanda babe umurame Inka mu Rwanda zibe umurame U Rwanda rwose rube umurame
Nyuma rero yo kubona umutima no kubona uburame ; ibyo ntabwo byari bihagije kuko u Rwanda rwose rwagombaga kuzira ubusembwa , kuvogerwa no guhumana ari byo bishushanywa na ba bantu ba amasugi bazanye .
Ubusanzwe umuntu wa isugi ni umuntu ugifite ababyeyi bombi cyangwa umukobwa utarasambanyijwe .
Muri ya masengesho ya Umutsobe mukuru yakomezaga agira ati :
Aya ni amasugi umwami abe isugi Ingoma i Rwanda zibe amasugi Abagabo i Rwanda babe amasugi Abagore mu Rwanda babe amasugi Inka i Rwanda zibe amasugi U Rwanda rwose ruhorane amasugi
Usibye imihango yo mu bwiru yo gusabira u Rwanda rwose umutima , uburame na ubusugire , mu magambo amwe na ayo tubonye hejuru , na none icyerekezo cyari ukugira ubuhoro ( amahoro ) mu Rwanda rwa Umwami .
Umwami wa i Rwanda agira ubuhoro Ingoma za i Rwanda zigira ubuhoro , Abagabo ba i Rwanda bagira ubuhoro Abagore ba i Rwanda bagira ubuhoro Inka za i Rwanda zigira ubuhoro U Rwanda rwose rugira ubuhoro
Nyuma ya ibyo byose u Rwanda rukagira uburumbuke bwa amata , ubuki na inturire .
Ibyo nabyo babivugaga mu mugambo ahwanye na ayo hejuru bati
Nga aya amata na ubuki Kugira ngo Umwami agire amata na ubuki Ingoma mu Rwanda zigire amata nubuki Abagabo bagire amata na ubuki Abagore bagire amata na ubuki Inka mu Rwanda zigire amata na ubuki .
Nyuma ya ibi , hazaga amasengesho yo gucyamura ( gukebura ) amahanga yose adatura umwami wa u Rwanda .
Dore amagambo bavugaga muri ubwo Bwiru :
Twacyamura u Burundi ku ngoma Twacyamura u Bushubi ku ngoma Twacyamura u Bunyabungo ku ngoma Amahanga yose adatura umwami wa u Rwanda Twayacyamura
Ibi twabigereranya na diporomasi ya ubu iba igamije gutuma amahanga yandi ayoboka ibya igihugu cyawe .
Amahame remezo ya u Rwanda gakondo
Iyi mihango yakorwaga na Abami bitwa Mutara na Cyilima hari ibintu idusobanurira neza bigatuma tumenya Ihame - ngengabitekerezo ryubatse u Rwanda rikaruha Indangagaciro .
Ihame - ngengabitekerezo ni ryo soko ya ibikorwa na imyitwarire bya umuntu cyangwa bya ikigo biturukamo .
Ni yo mpamvu nta muntu , nta kigo , nta shyaka nta na ishyanga byabaho bidafite Ihame - ngenga - bitekerezo ababigize bagenderaho .
Ku gihugu Ihame - ngengabitekerezo ni ryo rigena kandi rikagenga Indangagaciro na Kirazira bya igihugu !
None abakurambere baturaze u Rwanda barwubatse babikuye ku rihe hame - ngengabitekerezo ukurikije ibyo tumaze kubona ?
Ihame - ngengabitekerezo rya mbere ryagenaga kandi rikagenga ibyo mu Rwanda byose ; ni iritumenyesha icyo u " Rwanda rwose " " " " ari cyo : " u Rwanda rwose " " " " ntabwo ari ubutaka bwose bwa aho twita mu Rwanda gusa ; ahubwo ni ahantu hari : Ingoma - Umwami - Abagabo - Abagore - Inka .
Ibi rero ni nabyo byerekana ibyo twabonye bya Ibanga rya Umwami na Ingoma , na Ibanga rya Inka na Ingabo .
Aha icya mbere kigomba kumvikana mu Ihame ngenga - bitekerezo rya abahanze u Rwanda , ni uko ahantu hose ku isi hari kuba haboneka Umwami wimye Ingoma - ngabe yahawe umutima , hakaboneka Abagabo na Abagore ndetse na Inka , habashaga kuboneka u " Rwanda rwose .
" " " " Kimwe na uko ibyo byose uwari kubivana ku butaka bwa u Rwanda haba hatakaje kuba " u Rwanda rwose .
Impamvu ni ko ikihagira u Rwanda rwose ari izi ndangagaciro za Abanyarwanda zihari tuzi ko izo ndangagaciro zari zubakiye ku Mana , Inka na Ingoma .
Nka uko Umwami yabaga ahatswe na Ingoma maze Ingabo ( Abaturage ) nazo zikaba zihatswe na Umwami ; ni nako u Rwanda rwose rwabaga ruhatswe na Imana bitewe na uko Ingoma yimye u Rwanda ari Imana yayihaye umutima .
Nka uko Inka ihaka isabwa kubyara icyo ihatse ; ni nako Imana ihatse u Rwanda na yo isabwa guhora irubyara ( irugoboka ) .
Burya mu Kinyarwanda ijambo " gusenga " " " " risobanuye gukesha byose uguhatse !
Ni yo mpamvu usanga na isengesho gakondo ryo gusabira u Rwanda na ryo ari ibyo ryabaga ryerekejeho .
Nimwongere murebe amagambo arigize :
Seka seka gasani ka i Rwanda Rusekere rugubwe neza Rusenderezemo amahoro na amahe Rutsindire ubukenya na ubugingo buke Rutsindire ubusame na ubusharire Rutsindire icyago na icyagane Rutsindire nyamunsi na intumwa yayo Rutsindire umwanzi wo mu kirambi Na umurozi uvuka ishyanga Garika ibiganza utugabire Rugaba , Rugabo , Rwagisha Maze twishyuke mu Rwanda umu .
Ihame - ngengabitekerezo rya abahanze u Rwanda ni ukugira Ishyanga aho Umwami yima Ingoma - ngabe yahawe umutima ( ubushishozi ) na Imana , maze ingoma ( reigns ) zikagira umutima ( ubushishozi ) bigatuma Ingabo za Umwami ( Abagabo na Abagore ) nabo bagira umutima uzagera no ku nka na zo zikagira umutima ( wo gukamwa no konsa izazo ) .
Murabona neza ko uru ari uruhererekane rwa Umutima uva ku MANA ukagera mu Mwami unyuze mu NGOMA - NGABE maze ukarangiriza mu NKA unyuze mu ngabo ( Abagabo na Abagore ) .
Uru ruhererekane kandi ni rwo rwahoze rukoze " umutima wa u Rwanda rwose " " " " .
Byongeye kandi u Rwanda rwose iyo rwabaga rubonye umutima ; ni byo na none byateraga igihugu kugira uburame , ubusugire , ubuhoro na uburumbuke ndetse no kugarura amahanga adatura u Rwanda .
Ibi rero abakurambere bacu bakoraga kera ngo bahorane Umutima wa u Rwanda ( wa Ubunyarwanda ) na ubu mpamya ko bikenewe .
Kubura uwo umutima wa u Rwanda , wa ubunyarwanda ni byo byatumye abanyarwanda bishora mu mahano ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Ngo na Ruganzu Ndoli amaze kubohora u Rwanda amacakubiri yatumye rugirwa ingaruzwamuheto imyaka irenga icumi , yatangiye yigisha umutima wa u Rwanda .
Arwanya ba mutima - nda , mutima - rwana , mutima - muke , agakunda cyane mitimi - igwanye ( ihuje ) .
Ese ubu abo ba mutima - nda sibo batumye u Rwanda rutabohoka burundu ?
Imana tugira ni uko " imiyaga isubiza inyuma indege itwaye abanyarwanda itayibuza kugera iyo ijya " " " " nka uko Nyakubahwa Perezida wa Repubulika aherutse kubyibutsa Abanyarwanda bo mu Rwanda rutugendamo !
Naho ibidindiza Ndi Umunyarwanda byo ubanza dukwiye kubirebera mu mizi yabyo mikuru twitabaje amahame - remezo yagengaga ishyaka rya u Rwanda na Abanyarwanda .
Ibitekerezo bya Gérard Nyirimanzi na Nyirishema Célestin , Abacukumbuzi ba Ireme rya Umuco na Amateka bya u Rwanda .
Babikuye mu Ubwiru , Inzira ya Ishora , vers 279 - 310 .
Hagiye kuba amarushanwa ya igisoro , umwe mu mikino nyarwanda imaze igihe
Mu rwego rwo guteza imbere imikino gakondo na umuco nyarwanda , hagiye kuba amarushanwa yo gukina igisoro agamije kumenyekanisha no gukundisha abanyarwanda uwo mukino .
Mu rwego rwo guteza imbere imikino gakondo na umuco nyarwanda , hagiye kuba amarushanwa yo gukina igisoro agamije kumenyekanisha no gukundisha abanyarwanda uwo mukino .
Igisoro ni umwe mu mikino gakondo yatangiye kumenyekana mu Rwanda mu mwaka wa 1510 ku ngoma ya Umwami Ruganzu II Ndoli .
Ni umukino ukinanwa ubuhanga bwinshi hifashishijwe insoro ( zimeze nka utubumbe duto ) bagenda betereka mu twobo twabugenewe .
Ni umukino amateka agaragaza ko na Ruganzu Ndoli yawukinnye kuko hirya no hino mu gihugu hari ibimenyetso byamwitiriwe nko ku bitare bya Mpushi muri Kamonyi ahari igisoro , ikibumbiro , amajanja ya imbwa ze na intebe yicaragaho .
Umuyobozi wa sosiyete Umutsakura yateguye ayo marushanwa , Nshimyumuremyi Justin yabwiye IGIHE ko amarushanwa yatangiye mu Ukwakira uyu mwaka , umukino wa nyuma ukazaba kuwa Gatanu tariki 22 Ugushyingo muri Olympique Hotel ku Kimironko .
Ababugu ( abakina igisoro ) babiri nibo bazaba bahatanira umwanya wa mbere .
Nshimyumuremyi yavuze ko igisoro ari umwe mu mikino ya umwihariko wa abanyarwanda , nyamara udahabwa agaciro kuko ufatwa nka usuzuguritse .
Ati " impamvu yo gukora aya marushanwa ni ukuwusigasira .
Usanga indi mikino yarahawe agaciro ariko igisoro basa nka aho bagisize inyuma kandi ari umwihariko wacu abanyarwanda .
Aya marushanwa ni uburyo bwo kugira ngo igisoro cyongere kimenyekane , cyongere gikinwe ndetse mu bihe bizaza nkuko abakina Football ibagirira umumaro na abakina igisoro boye kujya bitwa inkorabusa cyangwa se abanebwe .
Yongeyeho ko " Hambere igisoro cyari gifatiye abanyarwanda runini .
Bagikoreshaga mu mibare .
Kubera ko bari bataragira irindi terambere rihambaye , iyo bakinaga barabaraga bati ndazana butatu nkurase burindwi , nongere nzane bune murase 12 [ … ] kumenya iyo mibare rero bigaragaza ubuhanga bari bafite .
Uretse kumenyekanisha uwo mukino , Nshimyumuremyi yavuze ko bashaka no kugikundisha abakiri bato kugira ngo bazagisigasire .
Kwinjira muri uyu mukino wa nyuma bizaba ari ubuntu .
Uzaba uwa mbere azahembwa ibihumbi 75 Frw , uwa kabiri ahembwe ibihumbi 50 naho uwa gatatu ahembwe ibihumbi 30 Frw .
Biteganyijwe ko hazanakorwa ibindi bikorwa bya umuco birimo indirimbo gakondo , imivugo na ibisigo , ibyivugo na ibindi .
Abategura aya marushanwa bavuze ko icyifuzo ari uko aya marushanwa yajya ategurwa nibura gatatu mu mwaka ubushobozi buramutse bubonetse .
Padiri Amerika agiye kumurika igitabo gitanga umucyo ku mpaka za urudaca zishingiye kuri Bibiliya
Padiri Amerika Victor , uyobora Paruwasi ya Nyabinyenga muri Diyosezi Gatolika ya Kabgayi agiye kumurika igitabo yise Nzi uwo Nemeye gishishikariza abakiristu mu madini yose kumenya imvano ya ibyo bemera aho kuba imbata za idini .
Padiri Amerika Victor , uyobora Paruwasi ya Nyabinyenga muri Diyosezi Gatolika ya Kabgayi agiye kumurika igitabo yise Nzi uwo Nemeye gishishikariza abakiristu mu madini yose kumenya imvano ya ibyo bemera aho kuba imbata za idini .
Muri iki gitabo , Padiri Amerika yashyizemo ibice bitandukanye bishingiye ku bushakashatsi na Bibiliya , bigaragaza ukuri kwa imyererere abantu bajya bibazaho .
Avugamo inzira ikwiriye abanyamadini kuri ubu basa na abarajwe ishinga no kurwana intambara zishingiye ku myemerere , ugasanga barwanira abayoboke kurusha uko bwaranira kwigisha ukuri kwa ijambo rya Imana .
Agaruka no ku bibazo bigaragara mu muryango ariko bitavugwaho rumwe , nka ibijyanye no kwihorera , gusenda abagore , kuboneza urubyaro na ibindi .
Mu kiganiro yagiranye na IGIHE , Padiri Amerika yavuze ko yagize igitekerezo cyo kwandika iki gitabo nyuma yo kwegerwa na bamwe mu bakiristu ayoboye akumva ibibazo bakunze kumubaza bigaragaza ko hari ibyo badasobanukiwe .
Yabihereye kandi mu gace paruwasi ayobora iherereyemo kabonekamo amadini menshi ariko ugasanga ashishikajwe no gushaka abayoboke asebya andi aho kwigisha ukuri kwa ijambo rya Imana kuboneka muri Bibiliya .
Ati " Muri iki gihe abantu benshi baremera , dufite amadini atandukanye dusengeramo ugasanga umuntu yabaye uwa idini kuruta kuba uwa ukuri , agatsimbarara kuri bya bindi bemera ariko atanabisobanukiwe .
Yakomeje agira ati " Igitabo cyanjye ntabwo ari igitabo cya idini , ni igitabo nanditse nka umuntu uri mu buzima bwa iyobokamana ariko cyakwifashishwa na abantu bose .
Padiri Amerika nko ku kijyanye no kuboneza urubyaro , agaragaza ko hari abagendera ku mugambo aboneka muri Bibiliya avuga ngo " Mubyare mwororoke mungane na umusenyi wo ku Nyanja " " " " .
Yavuze ko nubwo Bibiliya ivuga ityo , Aburahamu ufatwa nka sekuruza wa abemera bose yabyaye abana umunani gusa mu gihe cye bishingiye ku bushobozi na inshingano yari afite .
Ibyo bijyanye na andi magambo yo muri Bibiliya , mu ibaruwa ya kabiri Pawulo intumwa yandikiye abanyakolenti , 12 : 14 handitse ngo " si abana bateganyiriza ababyeyi ahubwo ni ababyeyi bateganyiriza abana babo .
Padiri Amerika agaragaza ko iyo ngingo yereka umubyeyi ko kubyara ari uburenganzira na inshingano .
Ati " Byara uwo ushoboye kurera , utazaba interagahinda akurushye , arushye na igihugu .
Muri iki gitabo kandi umwanditsi agaruka ku buhanuzi bweze muri iki gihe cyane cyane ubujyanye na igihe isi izarangirira .
Yabwiye IGIHE ko ntawe ukwiriye guhanura ibya irangira rya isi atarayishyizeho , ko bikwiriye guharirwa Imana ari nayo yaremye .
Yifuza ko uzasoma iki gitabo asobanukirwa na imyemerere ye ndetse na itandukaniro na iy abandi ariko byose bikaba ibiganisha ku kubana neza na abandi aho gushwana .
Ati " Tureke kuba abantu ba idini , ntabwo idini ari ishyaka .
Ishyaka rya mbere ni ukurwanirira kubana neza na abandi , kugira ngo mugenzi wawe akugirireho umugisha nawe umugirireho umugisha .
Musenyeri wa Diyosezi ya Kabgayi , Smaragde Mbonyintege ni we wanditse ijambo rya ikaze rya iki gitabo .
Mbonyintege mu ijambo rya ikaze , yavuze ko iki gitabo kije gukemura impaka za urudaca ku myumvire ya Bibiliya mu matorerro atandukanye .
Ati " Impaka za urudaca ku myumvire ya Bibiliya duhuriyeho na andi matorero ndetse no ku Masakramentu bamwe mu banyamatorero bakunze kugoreka imyumvire , umwanditsi yabiboneye ibisubizo ku buryo bwumvikana .
Yongeyeho ati " Iki gitabo ndagishimira ko kitagamije kwinjira mu mpaka na abagoreka ibyo twigisha , ahubwo gufasha mbere na mbere abakristu bacu gusobanukirwa mu mpaka za ababarundaho ibisobanuro biyobya .
Iki gitabo kizamurikwa kuri uyu wa Gatanu i Kigali kuri Hotel St Famille , guhera saa kumi na igice za umugoroba .
Uruzinduko rwa amasaha arindwi Bush yakoreye mu Rwanda , rugasiga ishusho nshya ya umubano mu ishoramari
Ku wa kabiri tariki 19 Gashyantare 2008 , uwari Perezida wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika George W .
Bush yagiriye uruzinduko rwa amasaha arindwi mu Rwanda , rusiga ibihugu byombi bisinye amasezerano ya ishoramari na icyerekezo cya umubano mushya .
Ku wa kabiri tariki 19 Gashyantare 2008 , uwari Perezida wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika George W .
Bush yagiriye uruzinduko rwa amasaha arindwi mu Rwanda , rusiga ibihugu byombi bisinye amasezerano ya ishoramari na icyerekezo cya umubano mushya .
Yaje mu Rwanda asoza uruzinduko rwa iminsi yari amaze muri Afurika mu bihugu birimo Bénin , Tanzania , Ghana na Liberia .
Bush yaje mu Rwanda ibibazo byasizwe na Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi bikiri byinshi , abapfakazi ba Jenoside , impfubyi , ibikorwa remezo bidahagije na gahunda za imibereho myiza ya abaturage bikiri hasi .
Icyakora yaje u Rwanda rutangiye kwigaragaza , aho 95 % bya abana bagejeje igihe cyo kujya kwiga mu mashuri abanza bajyagayo na hejuru ya 90 % ya abana bavuka bahabwa inkingo .
Yageze ku Kibuga Mpuzamahanga cya Indege cya Kigali mu gitondo , impande nyinshi za umujyi umutekano wakajijwe .
Bush yazanye na umufasha we Laura Bush , bahitira ku rwibutso rwa Jenoside rwa Kigali kunamira inzirakarengane zazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi no gusobanurirwa byimbitse itegurwa na ishyirwa mu bikorwa rya iyo Jenoside ikomeye yakozwe mu kinyejana cya 20 .
Amaze gusura urwibutso no gushyira indabyo ku mva ziruhukiyemo imibiri isaga ibihumbi 250 , Bush yavuze ko ibyabaye mu Rwanda bidakwiriye kugira ahandi biba .
Yagize ati " Aha ni ahantu hatitiza ibyiyumviro byawe .
Byanyibukije ko tudakwiriye gutuma ibintu nka ibi biba kandi ko abaturage ba u Rwanda bakeneye ubufasha ngo biyunge , batere imbere nyuma ya ibi bihe bya ubwicanyi .
Turasabira umugisha uva ku Mana abagifite ibikomere na abamaze igihe bakeneye ubufasha ndetse na abana ubuzima bwabo bwashegeshwe na ibihe banyuzemo .
Yongeyeho ati " Turashimira ubuyobozi kuba bwarashyizeho ahantu nka aha hibutsa abantu ko ikibi ntaho cyagiye mu Isi kandi ko kigomba kurwanywa .
Avuye ku rwibutso rwa Jenoside , Bush yakomereje muri Village Urugwiro kuganira na Perezida Kagame no gusinya amasezerano ya ishoramari hagati ya ibihugu byombi .
Mu 2007 , u Rwanda rwohereje muri Amerika ibicuruzwa bifite agaciro ka miliyoni 13 za amadolari ya Amerika , ruvanayo ibicuruzwa bifite agaciro ka miliyoni $ 16 .
Amasezerano amaze gusinywa , abakuru ba ibihugu byombi bagiranye ikiganiro na abanyamakuru , Perezida Kagame avuga ko ayo masezerano ari ubutumire ku bashoramari bo muri Amerika kuza mu Rwanda .
Ati " Ni ubutumire ku bashoramari kandi tubabwira ko nibaramuka baje hano ishoramari ryabo rizarindwa neza ku buryo bazabona umusaruro wa ibyo batanze .
Yongeye kubisubiramo nyuma ubwo batahaga Ibiro bishya bya Ambasade ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , avuga ko gutaha inyubako nshya za ambasade bikwiriye kuba nka rukuruzi ikururira abashoramari bo muri Amerika kuza gushora mu Rwanda .
Ibirori byakomereje ku Kacyiru ku Biro bishya bya Ambasade ya Amerika mu Rwanda , bishimira imyaka ibiri yari ishize byubakwa .
Ni ibiro Perezida Bush yitiriye Martin Luther King waharaniye ubwigenge bwa abirabura muri Amerika .
Muri ibyo birori byitabiriwe na abantu babarirwa mu magana , Michael Arieti wari Ambasaderi wa Amerika mu Rwanda yavuze ko uwo munsi ari uwa amateka mu mubano wa u Rwanda na Amerika .
Yatangiye yibutsa ko mu 2004 aribwo Leta ya u Rwanda yemeye kugurisha ikibanza ngo kigurwe na Amerika cyubakweho ambasade .
Yavuze ko imirimo yo kubaka iyo ambasade yakozwe na abakozi 750 , barimo abasaga 650 ba Abanyarwanda .
Bush wari umaze amasaha make mu Rwanda , yahawe umwanya avuga ko bitumvikana uburyo igihugu cyanyuze mu bibazo nka ibyo yari amaze kubona ku rwibutso , cyabashije kwiyubaka kikaba gitanga icyizere .
Yavuze ko ejo heza ha u Rwanda hashoboka cyane ashingiye ku muhate na urukundo yabonanye Perezida Kagame .
Ati " Ntabwo byumvikana uburyo icyizere cyagaruka nyuma yo guca mu bihe nka biriya .
Abanyamerika turi kumwe namwe mu rugamba rwo guharanira ejo heza .
Nishimira kuganira na abayobozi bakomeye bita ku baturage babo .
Nkunda umuhate na urukundo ari nabyo Perezida wanyu afite .
Yita bikomeye ku bibazo bya abaturage be .
Yavuze ko kuba hatashywe inyubako nshya za ambasade , ari umukoro ku Banyamerika wo gukomeza umutima wo gufasha no gushyigikira iterambere rya u Rwanda .
Ahagana saa cyenda , Bush na Laura bagiye muri Lycée de Kigali kuganira na abanyeshuri baho ibijyanye no kwirinda SIDA , ahava ahawe inkoni ya Kinyarwanda nka impano .
Ubwo yageraga ku kibuga cya indege atashye , yaganiriye gato na abasirikare bari baravuye mu butumwa bwa amahoro mu Ntara ya Darfur muri Sudani , dore ko igihugu cye cyari kimaze iminsi gitanga amahugurwa ku ngabo zigiye kujya mu butumwa bwa amahoro .
Bivugwa ko mu ruzinduko rwa Bush , we na Perezida Kagame baganiriye ku mutekano wo mu Karere cyane cyane muri Kenya aho imvururu zakurikiye amatora yo mu Ukuboza 2007 zari zimaze guhitana abantu basaga igihumbi .
No mu kiganiro na abanyamakuru , Bush yabikomojeho , avuga ko hatagizwe igikorwa ibiri kuba muri Kenya biganisha ku byabaye mu Rwanda mu 1994 .
Bush ni we Perezida wa Amerika uheruka gusura u Rwanda , akaba uwa kabiri nyuma ya Bill Clinton wahaje mu 1998 Jenoside imaze imyaka ine ihagaritswe .
Uruzinduko rwe rwongereye ishoramari na ubucuruzi hagati ya ibihugu byombi kuko mu 2018 , ibyo u Rwanda rwohereza muri Amerika byari bigeze kuri miliyoni $ 67 .
4 , bivuye kuri miliyoni $ 13 mu 2007 ibyo ruvanayo biba miliyoni 425 .
3 bivuye kuri miliyoni $ 16 mu 2007 .
Ibigwi na ibirindiro bya umwami Kigeli Rwabugili , mu gitero cya Imigogo ( Igice cya mbere )
Abatekereza ba amateka ya u Rwanda na abayatekererezwa , bakunze gutangarira ibikorwa bya umwami Kigeli Rwabugili , wazengereje amahanga , akayagusha ruhabo , kugeza ubwo ashaririwe no kumva izina " Rwanda " mu matwi yabo .
Abatekereza ba amateka ya u Rwanda na abayatekererezwa , bakunze gutangarira ibikorwa bya umwami Kigeli Rwabugili , wazengereje amahanga , akayagusha ruhabo , kugeza ubwo ashaririwe no kumva izina " Rwanda " mu matwi yabo .
Muri iki gice cya uruhererekane rwa inkuru twise " Ibigwi na ibirindiro " Aho tuzajya tubakusanyiriza amateka ya ibihangange byabaye mu rwa Gasabo bifite ibikorwa bikomeye , tugiye kubavunguriraho gato ku bigwi na ibirindiro bya umwami Kigeli Rwabugili , dore ko utabikuyeho akamanyu nibura gato gato , utashobora kubiva imuzi ngo ubigere imuzingo .
Nka uko tubikesha igitabo " Intwari za imbanza , zubatse u Rwanda rugahaya igitinyiro " cyanditswe na Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , inzobere ku Muco , ubusizi na amateka , tugiye kubatekerereza bimwe mu bigwi na ibirindiro bya umwami Kigeli Rwabugili , aho tubimburiye ku bigwi bye mu gitero cya imigogo , na na ubu kikirahirwa na amahanga , bya umwihariko abakigabweho
ba Abanyankore ba Abahinda .
Mu gitero cyiswe icya Imigogo Rwabugili yagabye muri Nkore , cyabaye mu gihe Abanyaburayi bari batangiye gusesekara muri Afurika ya Iburasirazuba ngo bayikoronize , icyo gihe agace ka igihugu cya Uganda Nkore yabarizwagamo kari karatangiye kugendagendwamo na Abongereza barimo kwiga inzira bazanyuramo batangira kuhakoroniza no kuhasakaza ibikorwa byabo .
Mu Rwanda ho bari bakihasunasuna byo kuhatinya kubera amateka yaho ya abayobozi na abaturage ba indwanyi .
Impano za mbere Abongereza bahaye Abanyankore ni imbunda na amasasu yo kwirwanaho bahashya umwanzi ubashotoye .
Zimwe mu mbunda Abanyankore bari bafite ni izo bitaga Makoba .
Izo mbunda babahaye zigera ku 300 nizo zabashutse batangira kwigerezaho ngo bagiye gutera u Rwanda rwabazengereje imyaka myinshi , dore ko hari ikindi gitero Rwabugili yari aherutse kubagabaho mu myaka ibiri yari ishize , ni ukuvuga mu wa 1892 .
Bitewe nuko ibice byo mu Burasirazuba bwa u Rwanda byari byaramaze kwigarurirwa burundu na u Rwanda , icyari kiraje ishinga Rwabugili , ni ibihugu byo mu Burengerazuba bwa u Rwanda byari bitarigarurirwa ibindi byigaruriwe na ababanjirije Rwabugili , byaratangiye kwigomeka .
Abanyankore bari batangiye kwiga uburyo bagaba ibitero bya ubushotoranyi ku Rwanda , bikaba na uburyo bwo kubihimuraho kuko bari barabumvishije mu gitero cyaherukaga .
Ubushotoranyi bwakozwe na Ntare IV Rugingiza rwa Migereka umwami wa Nkore watwaraga icyo gihe , aho yambutse umupaka aza kunyaga Inyambo za i Rwanda , agatwika ingoro ya Rwabugili yari i Rutaraka muri Nyagatare .
Icyo gihe Rwabugili yari yaragabye ibitero mu Burengerazuba bwa u Rwanda ku Ijwi ryari ryarigometse , arabimenya ko umwami wa Nkore Ntare Rugingiza rwa Migereka yamuteye akanyaga Inka ze zari Rutaraka muri Nyagatare .
Umugenga wazo Kinyamakara cya Ndezi ari na we wayoboraga ingoro ya Rwabugili yari i Rutaraka mu Ndorwa , yari mu ruzinduko , nuko banyaga inka za Rwabugili na umwe mu baja be barimo Nyiranziza muka Mpore ya Semandira .
Umutasi wabanje gutatira Ntare yari umuhungu we Muhanika wa Ntare .
Amakuru ya icyo gitero cya Abanyankore , Rwabugili yayabariwe n umuhima Bukomangando wabaciye mu rihumye akabonera akito kuri ibyo bitero ko kwihakirwa kuri Rwabugili , kuko yari amuziho ubuhangange na ubudatsindwa .
Rwabugili uburakari buramusaba yibaza uko ari bubigenze abifatira ingamba , kuko ntabwo yagombaga kugaruka igitero cyo ku Ijwi atagisoje .
Yaje gutegura igitero cyagabwe ku Banyankore muri Gashyantare umwaka wa 1894 , cyiswe " Igitero cya Imigogo " " " " kuko cyitabiriwe na Imitwe ibiri ya Ingabo za Abanyankore zitwa : " " " " Ingogo na imigogo " " " " .
Umwami Kigeli Rwabugili wari i Bunyabungo na Ingabo ze , yabanje kohereza yo Nyamuhenda wa Kajeje , na umutwe yari ayoboye witwaga " Ibisumizi " " " " .
Mu gushyika aho urugerero rwa Abanyankore rwari rukambitse i Kagitumba , Nyamuhenda wa Kajeje yasanze atari ukunyaga Inka gusa , ahubwo biteguye no kurwana .
Nyamuhenda na Ibisumizi , bakabona Abanyankore barimo bohereza mu kirere ibintu biturika byaka umuriro bikabayobera kuko batari bagasobanukirwa na imikorere ya imbunda zari zadutse vuba muri Afurika .
Bitewe nuko gusubira inyuma ku rugamba no kuruhunga bitari mu ndangagaciro za Abanyarwanda , biyemeje kururwana , nubwo babonaga harimo udushya twinshi turimo na imbunda zitari zimenyerewe muri aka karere .
Icyo gitero Abanyankore bagabye mu Rwanda , nicyo kiswe mu mateka ya u Rwanda na Nkore " Ehururu ya Rwanda " " " " .
Urugamba rwaremeye mu Kibande cya Ruhumba rwa Kiyojo .
Nyamuhenda na Ibisumizi yari ayoboye , Abanyankore bahabarasira kubamara kuko bo bari bakirwanisha imiheto na imyambi , abandi bafite imyuko iruka umuriro !
Nyamuhenda abonye ko Ingabo zigiye kumushirana , aravunura ahagarika urugamba ajya guhamagaza indi mitwe ya ingabo .
Nuko atanga ubutumwa ibukuru aho Rwabugili yari , amutangariza amacumu ya urugamba .
Rwabugili yazibiranyijwe na uburakari butagira ingano , bitewe na agasuzuguro kangana gutyo Abanyankore basuzuguye u Rwanda none bakaba bagiye no gutsindwa urugamba rwo kubarwanya , bitarigeze bibaho mu mateka ya abami ba u Rwanda .
Rwabugili yafashe imitwe ya Ingabo yose yari ku Ijwi na i Bunyabungo yageraga kuri 30 , ahamagaza na indi yari inyanyangiye ku ngerero zitandukanye hirya no hino mu gihugu yose igera kuri 50 , baravunura batera Nkore .
Bageze i Rutaraka ku ngoro ya Rwabugili , basanga harabaye amatongo , bahicara umwanya munini biga imigendekere ya urugamba bagiyemo .
Abanyankore babonye Ingabo za uruvunganzoka za Abanyarwanda , zitangiye kubanyanyagiramo , batangira gushya ubwoba , ariko birema agatima ku bwo kwiringira imbunda bari bafite kandi bibwiraga ko Abanyarwanda bari bataragera ku ikoranabuhanga nka iryo .
Abanyankore batangira kurasa mu kirere no gukanga kwinshi , ariko Abanyarwanda barimo kubiga no kwitegereza ibyo barimo .
Rwabugili akitegereza iyo myuko yohereza imiriro mu kirere , niko kubaza Nyamuhenda wa Kajeje , ati " Ko ndeba bariya Banyankore bohereza imiriro mu kirere , kandi nkaba mbona igera ku butaka yazimye , babicishije iki ?
Nyamuhenda wa Kajeje , amutekerereza uburyo bagiye bakabahagarara imbere bahanganye nka abagiye kurasana nka uko bisanzwe mu mirwanire ya gakondo , noneho batangira kubarasa mu mutwe no mu gituza abantu batangira kwikubita hasi na intwaro zabo , ari nako urushunzi rwa amaraso rwisuka ku butaka , bapfa umusubizo .
Mu gice gikurikira , tuzabaramburira imigendekere ya urwo rugamba rwongereye ibigwi bya Rwabugili na igitinyiro cya u Rwanda kirushaho kwiyongera … .
Nzaharanira kutaruta ubutumwa kuko buruta intumwa !
Isezerano rya Bamporiki nyuma yo kugirwa Minisitiri
Ku wa Mbere tariki 4 Ugushyingo 2019 nibwo Perezida wa Repubulika Paul Kagame yashyize mu murimo mishya bamwe mu bayobozi banyuranye .
Bamporiki Edouard yagizwe Umunyamabanga wa leta muri Minisiteri ya Urubyiruko na Umuco .
Ku wa Mbere tariki 4 Ugushyingo 2019 nibwo Perezida wa Repubulika Paul Kagame yashyize mu murimo mishya bamwe mu bayobozi banyuranye .
Bamporiki Edouard yagizwe Umunyamabanga wa leta muri Minisiteri ya Urubyiruko na Umuco .
Nyuma yo guhabwa uyu mwanya Bamporiki Edouard yashimiye Perezida Kagame amwizeza ko atazamutenguha ndetse azasohoza ubutumwa amutumye .
Abinyujije ku rukuta rwe rwa Twitter , Bamporiki yagize ati " Witaba kare ugatumwa kure , Watumwa na Umukuru ugashima ushingura ugana iyo utumwe .
Ubutumwa mumpaye Nyakubahwa Mutoza wa Ikirenga Paul Kagame nzabusohoza bwemye , nzaharanira kutaruta ubutumwa kuko buruta intumwa .
Nzaba Mudahusha ku ruhembe muntumye kurasaniraho .
U Rwanda nirweme .
Ubu butumwa buri mu Kinyarwanda cyiza , bwumvikanisha uburyo uyu mugabo wari usanzwe ari umukuru wa Itorero rya Igihugu yishimiye inshingano nshya yahawe .
Usibye kuzishimira , ikindi Bamporiki yavuzemo ni uko atazigera ashaka kuruta ubutumwa ahawe kuko buruta intumwa .
Aha akaba yumvikanishaga ko atazitwaza umwanya abonye ngo akomere kuruta inshingano ze .
Bamporiki yamenyekanye nka umukinnyi wa filime , ikinamico akaba na umwanditsi wa ibitabo , imivugo na ibisigo , azwi cyane mu ikinamico urunana aho akina yitwa Tadeyo cyangwa se Kideyo , aho akina ari se wa Budensiyana na Solina , inshuti ya Bushombe na Sitefano ba i Nyarurembo .
Yavutse tariki 24 Ukuboza 1983 , i Nyamasheke mu Ntara ya Iburengerazuba , ari naho yaje kwiga amashuri abanza ndetse na ayisumbuye , nyuma yiga amategeko mpuzamahanga muri Kaminuza yigenga ya Kigali ULK .
Yakuze akunda cyane kwandika imivugo , bituma yitabira amarushanwa atandukanye mu bigo bya amashuri .
Afite imyaka 11 gusa ya amavuko , yakoze umuvugo witwa " Iyo badatsembwa tuba dutwenga " " " " ari nawo watumye amenyekana nka umusizi akiri umwana .
Amaze kuba umusore yagiye abona umwanya wo kuvuga imivugo mu birori bitandukanye byo ku rwego rwa igihugu , nko ku munsi mukuru wa Intwari na indi minsi mikuru itandukanye .
Bamporiki wari usanzwe yumva ikinamico " Urunana " " " " akiri muto , akifuza kuba umwe mu bakinnyi bayo , mu 2003 yashakishije aho umushinga uyitegura ukorera , arahamenya maze agezeyo arabinginga ngo bareke ajye akinamo .
Aza kubyemererwa maze ahabwa umwanya yitwa Tadeyo .
Na ubwo abantu bagiye bumva Tadeyo akina ari umusaza ndetse ufite abana bakuru na abuzukuru , yari muto kuko icyo gihe yari afite imyaka 20 ya amavuko , bamwe mu bakinaga byumvikana ko ababereye umubyeyi baramurutaga .
Mu bindi bijyanye na ubuhanzi , Bamporiki yakunze kugaragara muri filime zitandukanye ndetse ahabwa ibikombe na ibihembo muri sinema , haba mu za abandi yagiye akinamo ndetse no mu zo yagiye yandika akanazikinamo .
Muri za abandi yagaragayemo harimo iyitwa Munyurangabo ya uwitwa Isaac Chung ukomoka muri Amerika , iyitwa Rwanda take two ya Pia nawe wo muri Amerika , na iyitwa Imitoma ya Kwezi John .
Mu mafilime yanditse ku giti cye akanakinamo harimo iyitwa Ukuri kuri he ndetse na Long Coat ( Ikote rirerire ) .
Mu 2006 yitabiriye Iserukiramuco rya amafilime rya Cannes mu Bufaransa , mu 2010 yitabira iryabereye i Rotterdam mu Buholandi , mu 2011 yitabira iryabereye muri Turikiya ryitwa " Crimes and punishment " " " " .
Mu 2008 yabonye igihembo yakuye i New York muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , akaba yarahembewe kwandika filime nziza ( Best Script ) abikesheje filime " Long Coat " " " " , yagaragayemo abahanzi ba Abanyarwanda nka Nirere Shanel , Mani Martin na umukinnyi Jimmy Gatete .
Mu 2011 yabonye igihembo cya umukinnyi mwiza ( Best Actor ) mu iserukiramuco rya Heart Land .
Nyuma ya ubuhanzi mu byiciro bitandukanye , Bamporiki mu 2013 yatorewe kuba intumwa ya rubanda , aba Umudepite mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya u Rwanda .
Ku itariki ya 30 Kanama 2017 , Bamporiki yahawe imirimo mishya agirwa Umuyobozi wa Itorero rya Igihugu .
Bamporiki ni umugabo wubatse , wambikanye impeta ya urudashira na Uwingabire Claudine tariki ya 18 Ukuboza 2010 .
Bamporiki yize amasomo atandukanye , arimo ajyanye na sinema yize i Burayi ahitwa Plague , aza no kwiga muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ibijyanye no kubaka amahoro no kurwanya amakimbirane .
Mu masomo asanzwe yize muri Kaminuza yigenga ya Kigali ULK aho yakuye impamyabumenyi ya icyiciro cya gatatu mu mategeko mpuzamahanga .
Ubutumwa bwa Bamporiki Edouard nyuma yo guhabwa umwanya mushya
Witaba kare ugatumwa kure , Watumwa na Umukuru ugashima ushingura ugana iyo utumwe .
Ubutumwa mumpaye Nyakubahwa Mutoza wa Ikirenga @ PaulKagame nzabusohoza bwemye , nzaharanira kutaruta ubutumwa kuko buruta intumwa .
Nzaba Mudahusha kuruhembe muntumye kurasaniraho .
URwanda nirweme .
— Bamporiki Edouard ( @ Bamporikie ) November 4 , 2019
Inkomoko gakondo ya ibicumbi bya imiryango migari ya Abanyarwanda ( Igice cya mbere )
Abantu benshi bakunze kwibaza ikibazo kijyanye na ibicumbi bikuru bya imiryango bakomokamo nka gakondo ya ubutaka bwatuweho na abakurambere mbere ya uko bororoka bagakwirakwira hirya no hino ku butaka bwa u Rwanda , ari nako babuhangaho ibihugu byaje kungwa bikabyara igihugu kimwe aricyo u Rwanda .
Abantu benshi bakunze kwibaza ikibazo kijyanye na ibicumbi bikuru bya imiryango bakomokamo nka gakondo ya ubutaka bwatuweho na abakurambere mbere ya uko bororoka bagakwirakwira hirya no hino ku butaka bwa u Rwanda , ari nako babuhangaho ibihugu byaje kungwa bikabyara igihugu kimwe aricyo u Rwanda .
Nka uko tubikesha igitabo " Iyororoka rya Abanyarwanda , Inkomoko ya imiryango migari " dukesha Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , inzobere mu muco , ubusizi na amateka ya u Rwanda , tugiye kubatekerere za gakondo nkuru za ibicumbi bikuru bya imiryango migari ya Abanyarwanda .
Abanyarwanda bibumbiye mu Bicumbi bikuru bya imiryango , imiryango migari ndetse na inzu za imiryango .
Ibicumbi bikuru bya imiryango , nibyo byabyaye imiryango migari , naho imiryango migari ibyara inzu za imiryango .
Muri aya mateka tukaba tugiye kwanzikira kuri gakondo za ibicumbi bikuru bya imiryango ya Abanyarwanda aribyo : Abasinga , Abazigaba na Abanyiginya .
Gakondo z igicumbi gikuru cya imiryango ya Abasinga
Abatekereza ba amateka ya u Rwanda , bagaragaza neza ko Abasinga batuye bwa mbere ku butaka bwa u Rwanda , bafite inkomoko ku Bahima babarizwa ku butaka bwa igihugu cya Uganda , aribo bakunze kwita " Abahima ba Abanyankole " " " " .
Mu iyaduka ryabo , baje bafite intego yo guhamya ubuhangange bwo gutura ku butaka bwari butwikiriwe na amashyamba ya kimeza , babuhangaho ibihugu , bituma bakura izina ryabo mu rurimi rwa igisekuruza cyabo rwa urunyankore , bakurijeho kwitwa " Abasinga " " " " aribyo mu Kinyarwanda bisobanuye : Abatsinze " .
Mu gutura kuri ubu butaka bwa u Rwanda , Abasinga binjiriye bwa mbere mu Majyaruguru ya u Rwanda bakomereza mu Burengerazuba bagana mu Majyepfo , bakurikiranye ubutohe bwa umwegega wa Ikiyaga cya Kivu na amashyamba ya Ibirunga na aya kimeza nka Gishwati , Nyungwe , Mukura na Cyamudongo .
Ayo mashyamba bayahereyeho bahiga , kugeza ubwo bayatutira , bayahangaho ibihugu .
Kubera ko ntawe bacuranwaga ngo abakome imbere kuri ubu butaka , barisanzuye baratura kugeza na ubwo basakaje ingoma zabo mu Rwanda rw u Burengerazuba , mu Rwanda rwa Amajyepfo no mu Rwanda rwo Hagati ndetse bambuka na Nyabarongo basatira u Rwanda rwa i Burasirazuba .
Gakondo yabo ari nayo gicumbi gikuru batuyemo , kuri ubu ni mu Mirenge ya : Kigeyo , Mushonyi , Musasa , Ruhango , Gihango , Kivumu na Boneza yo mu Karere ka Rutsiro na Umurenge wa Nyamyumba wo mu Karere ka Rubavu
Gakondo z igicumbi gikuru cya imiryango ya Abazigaba
Abatekereza ba amateka ya u Rwanda , bagaragaza neza ko Abazigaba batuye mu ba mbere kuri ubu butaka bwa u Rwanda bakurikiye bene wabo ba Abasinga , bafite ikomoko ku Bahima babarizwa ku butaka bwa igihugu cya Uganda , aribo bakunze kwita " Abahima ba Abanyankole " " " " .
Mu iyaduka ryabo , badukiriye igice cya i Burasirazuba bwa u Rwanda bogoze ibiyaga bigari bihabarizwa , aba ariho batema amashyamba ya Cyimeza barayakonda , barayatutira bayahangamo ibihugu bishyira kera .
Batuye ako gace babungira ubutohe gakomora ku ruzi rwa Akagera na ibiyaga bihaboneka nka Nasho , Hago , Ihema na ibindi .
Nuko batangira kwagura ibihugu byabo bagana mu Rwanda rwo hagati no mu Majyepfo ya Iburasirazuba .
Gakondo ya imbanza ya igicumbi gikuru cya imiryango ya Abazigaba ni mu mirenge ya : Mwili na Murundi yo mu Karere ka Kayonza , ukongeraho Umurenge wa Rwimbogo yo muri Gatsibo .
Gakondo z igicumbi gikuru cya imiryango ya Abanyiginya
Abatekereze ba amateka ya Igicumbi cya imiryango migari cya Abanyiginya , bavuga ko cyaba gikomoka mu Majyaruguru ya Iburasirazuba bwa Afurika mu gihugu cya Ethiopia .
Inkomoko yabo ikaba ari iyo mu muryango wa Abagala bakunze kwita na Abaromo , wari ukomeye muri icyo gihugu kandi wari nawo mugabwangoma mu myaka ya 300 nyuma ya Yezu Kirisitu .
Abanyiginya basesekaye mu Karere ka Afurika ya Iburasirazuba no mu Rwanda , ahasaga muwa 700 , ubwo bari mu iyimukayimuka nka abandi bose rya abatuye muri Afurika , bashaka ubwinyagamburiro bwa imiryango yabo na amatungo yabo .
Nyuma ya igihe kitari gito , bafashe urugendo rwo mu muhora uhuza Afurika ya Amajyaruguru ya Iburasirazuba na iy Amajyepfo , bagaca mu bihugu bya Somaliya , Kenya na Uganda , niko gusesekara kuri ubu butaka bwa u Rwanda .
Barasukiye mu Burasirazuba bwa u Rwanda mu Murenge wa Gatsibo wo mu Karere ka Gatsibo , basanga Abazigaba barahakabye barema ingoma ya u Rweya rwa u Mubali , yari ikomatanyije Imirenge ya Akarere ka Gatsibo , na imirenge imwe na imwe iri mu Majyaruguru ya Akarere ka Kayonza .
Abahasesekaye muri ibyo bihe , nibo bavuyemo Abasekuruza ba Imbanza ba Kazi wabyaye Gihanga cyahanze ingoma ya u Rwanda .
Mu gusesekara mu Rweya rwa Abazigaba , bahaserukanye , ibigwi na imihigo ya ibyo bazanye muri aka karere , nka uko babivuze mu izina ryabo ubwo Abazigaba babazaga izina ryabo .
Nka aho bakavuze irya igisekuruza cyabo cya Abagala cyangwa se Abaromo , badukana izina rishya ryibigwi na ibirindiro bya ahazaza habo , rya Abanyiginya rishatse kuvuga " Abantu barambye ku butunzi na ubupfura " " " " .
Nyuma ya imyaka isaga 300 , Abanyiginya bamaze mu busembere bacumbikiwe na Abazigaba , nibwo umucyo wa ubuhangange wabamurikiye bahanga igihugu cyabo kitwaga Gasabo , cyinjira mu ruhando rwa ibindi bihugu bigera kuri 24 byari bisanganyije ubu butaka bwa u Rwanda , baba babaye igihugu cya 25 , gihangwa na Gihanga Ngomijana , umukurambere wa Abangiyinya bahanze ingoma ya u Rwanda .
I Gasabo niho Abanyiginya na imiryango ibakomokaho baguriye ubutaka bwabo bahanga ibindi bihugu ku bisigara bya ubutaka Abasinga na Abazigaba bari baranennye .
Ibihugu byahanzwe na bene Gihanga , muri byo dusangamo Ndorwa ya Abashambo , Kibali ya Abega , u Bugara bwa Abacyaba na u Bugesera bwa Abahondogo .
Amateka ya impitabie ku gihugu cya u Rwanda , adutekerereza ko gakondo nkuru ya igicumbi gikuru cya Abanyiginya na imiryango migari ibakomokaho , ari mu Mirenge ya Nduba , Bumbogo , Rutunga , Gikomero , Ndera na Rusororo yo mu Karere ka Gasabo , ukongeraho na Umurenge wa Fumbwe wo mu Karere ka Rwamagana .
Nyuma yo kubagezaho Gakondo nkuru za ibicumbi bya imiryango ya Abanyarwanda , mu bice bikurikiraho , tuzabagezaho za Gakondo nkuru za imiryango migari ya Abanyarwanda , uko ari 24 .
Impanuro zikubiye mu gitabo " Amakosa 100 nticuza " " " " cya Rubaduka Frank
Rubaduka Frank yanditse igitabo kigaragaza amakosa yakoze mu buzima ariko aticuza .
Iki gitabo yacyise 100 mistakes i dona t regret cyangwa se mu rurimi rwa Ikinyarwanda Amakosa 100 nticuza .
Rubaduka Frank yanditse igitabo kigaragaza amakosa yakoze mu buzima ariko aticuza .
Iki gitabo yacyise 100 mistakes i dona t regret cyangwa se mu rurimi rwa Ikinyarwanda Amakosa 100 nticuza .
Uyu musore watangije irushanwa rya Miss Career Africa agiye gushyira hanze iki gitabo yageneye urubyiruko na undi wese ushaka gutsinda ubwoba agakurikira amahitamo ya umutima we .
Iki gitabo yacyanditse mu gihe cya imyaka ibiri .
Kizacururizwa ku rubuga rwa Amazon .
Uyu musore yahisemo gukurikira ibyo akunda nyuma ya uko atanze igitabo gisoza kaminuza kikangwa bitewe na uko yari yatinze , kuko hari hashize icyumweru abandi batanze ibyabo .
Gutinda gutanga igitabo gisoza kaminuza yabitewe na uko yari yahugiye ku bikorwa bya sosiyete ye .
Yahisemo guhagarika amasomo , ahubwo yita ku bikorwa bya sosiyete ye kuko ariho yari yerekeje umutima .
Umuryango we ntiwishimye iyo nzira kuko washakaga ko yiga akaminuza akajya gusaba akazi ahandi ku buryo wazajya umubona mu biro ari umuntu ukomeye .
Hashize igihe gito ahagaritse kwiga , yatsindiye inkunga ya amadorali ibihumbi 150 yahawe na Abanya - Australia .
Rubaduka witegura kwizihiza isabukuru ya imyaka 27 ya amavuko , yahise ashinga sosiyete eshanu mu bihe bitandukanye buri imwe ishamikiye ku yindi .
Yabwiye IGIHE ko yahisemo gutanga ubutumwa muri iki gitabo kubera ko abenshi bakunze guhisha inzira banyuzemo kandi zabera urugero rwiza benshi .
Ati " Abantu benshi iyo batangiye gutera imbere hari ukuntu bahisha amakosa na ibindi bintu bagiye bahura nabyo .
Ariko kuko njye nagiranye igihango na Imana ko ningira aho ngera nta mpamyabumenyi mfite nzabwira urubyiruko rugenzi rwanjye ko umuntu adakeneye impamyabumenyi na ibitangaza kugira ngo abe igitangaza mu Isi .
Yavuze ko byarangiye uwari umuterankunga we muri Kaminuza anyuzwe na intego ye amutera inkunga ya umushinga wa mbere yakoze hashize umwaka umwe abona undi muterankunga .
Iki gitabo acyitezeho guhindura imyumvire ya abandi na iy ababyeyi babuza abana babo gukurikira amahitamo yabo .
Aniteze ko umuntu wakuriye mu buzima bubi uzasoma iki gitabo azahita ahagarika kumva ko akeneye umuntu uvuga rikijyana kugira ngo agera ku cyo yiyemeje .
Rubaduka yavuze ko amaze imyaka itatu muri Kigali , kandi ko nta muntu ukomeye baziranye wamufashije gukurikira inzozi ze uretse kuba yarabyaje umusaruro amahirwe Leta yashyiriyeho urubyiruko .
Niwe watangije irushanwa rya Miss Career Africa rigamije kugaragaza imishinga ya abakobwa yahindura ubuzima bwa sosiyete .
Rubaduka Frank yavukiye muri Uganda , umuryango we utahuka mu Rwanda nyuma ya uko Ingabo zari iza RPA zihagaritse Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi muri Mata 1994 .
Village Urugwiro , inyubako ya amateka akomeye mu Rwanda
Village Urugwiro , ni inyubako yubashywe kuva icyubakwa kugeza na ubu .
Benshi tuyirebera kure kubera icyubahiro tuyigomba nka ibiro bicurirwamo icyerecyezo gitumye u Rwanda ruba ubukombe , ikaba isoko ya amahoro aduhesha ibikombe mu mahanga .
Village Urugwiro , ni inyubako yubashywe kuva icyubakwa kugeza na ubu .
Benshi tuyirebera kure kubera icyubahiro tuyigomba nka ibiro bicurirwamo icyerecyezo gitumye u Rwanda ruba ubukombe , ikaba isoko ya amahoro aduhesha ibikombe mu mahanga .
Ni inyubako ya amateka kuko abagera kuri 50 % bya Abanyarwanda bariho bavutse iriho , iganje ku Kacyiru , mu Karere ka Gasabo mu Mujyi wa Kigali aho imaze imyaka 44 .
Yubatswe mu 1975 na Umuryango wahuzaga Ibihugu bya Afurika cyane cyane ibyakolonijwe na u Bufaransa na ibikoresha Igifaransa , Organization Commune Africaine et Malgache ( OCAM ) .
Uwo muryango kuri ubu wazimye , u Rwanda rwawinjiyemo mu 1965 .
Mu 1975 , nibwo rwari kwakira inama yawo yagombaga kwitabirwa na abakuru ba ibihugu bagera kuri 15 .
Byari ihurizo rikomeye ku gihugu nka u Rwanda cyari gifite hoteli nke zitwa ko zikomeye nka Mille Collines na Diplomate zari zigezweho icyo gihe ariko zifite ubushobozi bwo kwakira abashyitsi baringaniye .
Muri icyo gihe u Rwanda rwiteguraga kwakira inama , inyubako za mbere za Village Urugwiro zubatswe ku mafaranga ya OCAM nkuko Rucagu Boniface , umwe mu bagize Urwego Ngishwanama rwa Inararibonye yabibwiye IGIHE .
Inama ya OCAM irangiye , inyubako za Village Urugwiro zeguriwe Leta ya u Rwanda nayo izihinduramo hoteli yakiraga abifite muri ibyo bihe .
Nubwo Village Urugwiro yabaye hoteli , mu gihe u Rwanda rwabaga rwakiriye inama zikomeye yakomezaga kwifashishwa mu kwakira abashyitsi ba Leta .
Urugero ni tariki 21 na 22 Gicurasi 1979 ubwo u Rwanda rwakiraga inama ya Gatandatu ihuza u Bufaransa na Afurika yanitabiriwe na Perezida wari uyoboye u Bufaransa icyo gihe , Valéry Marie René Georges Giscard da Estaing .
Mbere ya uko iyo nama iba , u Bufaransa bwari bwatanze amafaranga yo kwagura Village Urugwiro no kuyivugurura kugira ngo ijye ku rwego rwo kwakira inama ikomeye nka iyo , nkuko biri mu nyandiko za ibanga za Ambasade ya Amerika mu Rwanda muri icyo gihe , zashyizwe hanze na WikiLeaks .
Uwo mwaka ni nabwo hubatswe hoteli Novotel Umubano ( Marasa Umubano Hotel kuri ubu ) nabwo ku mafaranga yatanzwe na u Bufaransa .
Rucagu avuga ko nyuma yo kwagura Village Urugwiro , yasigaye igizwe na inyubako ( appartments ) zisaga 20 zirimo amacumbi agezweho , ibyumba bya inama na ibindi .
Amacumbi ya abadepite , ibiro bidahoraho bya Perezida
Juvénal Habyarimana amaze gufata ubutegetsi mu 1973 , yahise asesa Inteko Ishinga Amategeko .
Yongeye kuyisubizaho mu 1981 , abadepite ba mbere 70 ba inzibacyuho batangira imirimo mu 1982 .
Kubera ubuke bwa amacumbi muri Kigali , Leta yemereye buri mudepite icumbi muri Village Urugwiro dore ko abenshi babaga baturuka mu bice bya kure badashobora gukora bataha iwabo .
Mu 1983 habaye amatora ya abadepite , Rucagu Boniface aba umwe muri bo ubwo yatangiraga imirimo mu 1984 na we ahabwa icumbi muri Village Urugwiro .
Umudepite yahabwaga icumbi gusa , ibyo kurya akimenya .
Rucagu avuga ko mu badepite 70 , abasaga 40 babaga muri Village Urugwiro kuko babaga baturuka mu bice bya kure .
Uwabaga yifitiye inzu i Kigali , yayibagamo Leta ikamugenera amafaranga ya icumbi .
Rucagu ati " Uwabaga yifitiye inzu ye bamuhaga amafaranga ariko babanje kubyanga bavuga bati kuki mushaka kurara mu nzu zanyu kandi twarabageneye iza Leta , baraburana ariko byaje gukemuka nyuma .
Icyo gihe abadepite babamo , inzu zasagukaga zakomezaga kuba ibyumba bya hoteli bisanzwe , abashaka kubiraramo bakaza kwishyura .
Nubwo hari hoteli na amacumbi ya abadepite , Perezida Habyarimana na we yahashyize ibiro ariko akajya abizamo rimwe na rimwe kuko ibiro nyamukuru byari mu mujyi rwagati , ahubatse Ibiro bya Umujyi wa Kigali ubu .
Rucagu ati " Iruhande rwa izo nzu haruguru ya ahahoze reception niho hari Ibiro bya Umukuru wa Igihugu .
Muri izo nzu zose ahagana ku rwinjiriro yari yarafashemo inzu ya ibiro bye , izindi zose zikomeza kuba hoteli .
Yari ibiro bya kabiri yazagamo nka rimwe cyangwa kabiri mu kwezi .
Buri nyubako ( apartment ) muri izo zari zigize Hotel Village Urugwiro yabaga ifite icyiciro runaka ibarizwamo .
Rucagu wahabaye mu gihe cya imyaka 10 ari umudepite , avuga ko buri nyubako yabaga ifite ibyumba bitatu , ni ukuvuga A , B na C .
Icyumba A , cyabaga gifite ibyangombwa nkenerwa byose birimo uruganiriro , uburiri , ubwiherero , igikoni , harimo frigo na ibindi , kikaba kigenewe Umukuru wa Igihugu mu gihe habaye inama cyangwa undi muntu wo ku rwego rwo hejuru wakirayemo .
Hafi ya icyo cyumba nyamukuru , habaga ikindi bise B , kikararamo umuganga wa umuntu mukuru waraye muri A .
Ni ukuvuga ko niba haraye Perezida , muri B hararaga umuganga we naho muri C hakarara abarinzi be .
Mu gihe habaga habaye inama zikomeye , abadepite bari barahawe amacumbi muri Village Urugwiro basabwaga kuvamo bakazagaruka inama yarangiye .
Rucagu ati " Batumenyeshaga mbere ya ukwezi , tukavamo bakahakoropa , bakahasukura bakavanamo umwanda wose , tukazagaruka baragiye .
Ubwo mu mirimo ya Inteko twariyeranjaga .
Village Urugwiro yakomeje kuba hoteli kugeza mu 1994 muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Jenoside imaze guhagarikwa , muri Nyakanga uwo mwaka Leta ya Ubumwe imaze kurahira Village Urugwiro aho kuba ibiro bidahoraho bya Umukuru wa Igihugu , yahindutse Ibiro byuzuye bya iminsi yose bya Umukuru wa Igihugu kugeza ubu .

Abakobwa bifuza guhatanira ikamba rya Miss Rwanda 2020 batangiye kwiyandikisha binyuze ku rubuga rwa irushanwa , mu mabwiriza basabwe kuba bujuje harimo impinduka kuko Ikinyarwanda cyashyizwe mu ndimi zemerewe gukoreshwa .

Kuba yiteguye gukurikiza no kubahiriza amahame yose na amabwiriza agenga ba Nyampinga

Ikinyarwanda ni cyo cya ingenzi , izindi ndimi zizakoreshwa ku mahitamo ya uhatana .
Prince Kid yavuze ko mu gutanga amanota hazitabwa cyane kubyo umukobwa avuga , ubwiza ndetse na umuco .
Ubusanzwe umukobwa yasabwaga kuba azi Ikinyarwanda na urundi rurimi rumwe rwa amahanga , uburyo abahatana bitwaraga mu ndimi za amahanga byatumye benshi bibaza impamvu abategura Miss Rwanda bazibandaho nyamara hashobora gukoreshwa ururimi kavukire , aha bagaraazaga ko icyingenzi ari ikiri mu muntu atari ururimi akivugamo .
