Inkomoko ya amazina ya uduce tumwe two muri Kigali nka Nyarugenge , Kacyiru na utundi
Ikigo cya Ingoro za Igihugu za Umurage wa u Rwanda ( INMR ) cyatangaje ko amwe mu mazina yahawe uduce tumwe na tumwe two muri Kigali akoreshwa kugeza ubu , yagiye atangwa hashingiwe ku ihangwa rya igihugu , ibikorwa bya iyubaka gihugu ( Ubuhinzi , ubworozi , intambara ) , ibikorwa byahabereye bigasiga umugani .
Ikigo cya Ingoro za Igihugu za Umurage wa u Rwanda ( INMR ) cyatangaje ko amwe mu mazina yahawe uduce tumwe na tumwe two muri Kigali akoreshwa kugeza ubu , yagiye atangwa hashingiwe ku ihangwa rya igihugu , ibikorwa bya iyubaka gihugu ( Ubuhinzi , ubworozi , intambara ) , ibikorwa byahabereye bigasiga umugani .
Icyo kigo kivuga ko hari amazina yatanzwe hagendewe ku bwoko bwa igiti biri cyangwa byiganje ahantu runaka .
Izina " " " " Nyarugenge " " " " rituruka ku giti cyitwa Imigenge ( Acacia hochii ) .
Ariryo ubu ryitwa Akarere ka Nyarugenge .
Abahanga mu mateka bavuga ko hari ahandi nka Kimironko hiswe hatyo hagendewe ku ishyamba rya ibiti byitwa Imironko ryatewe na Cyilima Rujugira , kugira ngo ajye aritemamo ibiti byo kuramvura imiheto yo guhangana na amahanga adakunda u Rwanda .
Kimihurura habaga ibyatsi bivura byitwa imihurura na ahandi .
Ikigo cya Ingoro za Igihugu za Umurage wa u Rwanda ( INMR ) kivuga ko hari amazina yaturutse ku bantu bakomeye babaga ahantu runaka .
Nka " Kacyiru " " " " bivugwa ko ryatanzwe hagendewe ku mugabo witwaga Cyiru ; wari umutware na " Rwabutabura " " " " ryatanzwe riturutse ku witwaga Rwabutabura wari utuye ahitwa iryo zina muri iki gihe , ubu ni mu Karere ka Nyarugenge .
Umushakashatsi ku muco na amateka Nsanzabera Jean De Dieu avuga ko Kacyiru ( agasozi ka icyiru ) byitiriwe agasozi katangiweho Ibyiru byinshi , bikomotse ku manza zacirwaga Abanyabwanacyambwe banze kuyoboka ingoma ya Mukobanya , nyuma yo kuhigarurira ahasaga mu wa 1378 ubwo yicaga Nkuba ya Nyabakonjo umwami wa u Bwanacyambwe .
Gacuriro hiswe hatyo kubera uruganda rucura amacumu yo kwagura u Rwanda rwubatswe na Kigeli Mukobanya .
Andi mazina yatanzwe afatiwe ku bikorwa byo kubaka u Rwanda nka ubworozi bwa inka .
" Kicukiro " " " " risobanuye umusozi amacukiro ( ibirundo bya amase ya inka ) .
Mu bihe byo hambere , Kicukiro izwi nka kamwe mu turere twa umujyi wa Kigali kororerwagaho inka nyinshi .
Niho hari hubatse ibiraro bya inka za Kigeli Mukobanya na umuhungu we Mibambwe Sekarongoro Mutabazi .
Hari ahazwi nka Kabusunzu hiswe hatyo kubera umupfumu wa umuhanga wari waraturutse i Karagwe witwa Gasunzu nyuma aho atuye bahita Kagasunzu nyuma umunyamakuru wo kuri Radiyo Rwanda yagiye gutara amakuru avugira kuri Radiyo ko ari Kabusunzu rihama rityo .
Hazwi nka i Nyamirambo hiswe hatyo biturutse ku mirambo myinshi yahabonetse ubwo abanyoro bateraga u Rwanda .
Amateka nka ayo aboneka mu nzu ndangamateka yitiriwe Richard Kandt ( Kandt House Museum ) .
Mu busanzwe hari ahandi mu Rwanda hagiye hitwa amazina hagendewe ku bikorwa bitandukanye byagiye bihabera .
Hari nko ku Kivumu cya Mpushi , ahacirwaga abarwaye ibinyoro , ku cya Semakamba habereye urubanza rwa Semakamba na Umwami Kigeli Rwabugiri na ahandi .
Kigali yagizwe umurwa mukuru wa u Rwanda bwa mbere ku bwa Kigeli Mukobanya ahasaga 1378 .
Umurwa mukuru wa Umwami wari mu Mudugudu wa Vugavuge mu Kagali ka Gasabo mu Murenge wa Rutunga ha ubu .
Kurasaga , imyotso , kurumika , kugombora : Uburyo gakondo bwamamaye mu kuvura indwara za amayobera
Kurumika no kurasaga , imyotso no kugombora , ni imigenzo nyarwanda yakorwaga mu buvuzi gakondo no kurinda ibyago Abanyarwanda , bityo uwabikoraga akaba afite imyerere ya uko iyo bikozwe byanze bikunze birinda kandi bikanavura .
Kurumika no kurasaga , imyotso no kugombora , ni imigenzo nyarwanda yakorwaga mu buvuzi gakondo no kurinda ibyago Abanyarwanda , bityo uwabikoraga akaba afite imyerere ya uko iyo bikozwe byanze bikunze birinda kandi bikanavura .
Gusa kuri ubu Abanyarwanda benshi ntibabyemera , ndetse bavuga ko ari imihango ya gipagani , na ubwo hari abaganga bemeza ko iyo migenzo yabaga ari ingirakamaro .
Nka uko tubikesha igitabo " Umuco mu Buvanganzo " cyanditswe na Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , Inzobere ku muco , amateka na ubuvanganzo nyarwanda , tugiye kubataturira imwe mu mihango na imigenzo yakorwaga mu kuvura no kurinda indwara mu muco wa Abanyarwanda .
Kurasaga ( Guca indasago , gukeba gahoro gahoro ku mubiri ) umuntu byaterwaga na uko bashaka nko kumushyiramo imiti yo kumuvura ikintu arwaye , cyangwa kumutsirika bavuga ngo batazamuroga , bakarasaga rero bagashyiramo iyo miti .
Hari na aho bikengeraga ko umwana wavutse azahura na akaga , nako bakagatsirika bakoresheje kumuca indasago , ukazasanga koko bibaye impamo , ibyago baketse , akabicika .
Hari kandi na indasago bacaga ku mugore ugiye gushaka cyangwa umugabo , bagashyiramo imiti ituma bahamya umubano uzira kidobya .
Niyo mpamvu uzasanga abantu bakuru benshi bafite indasago ku mubiri , ku gikanu , mu gatuza , ku bibero ku gahanga , mu biganza na ahandi .
Umumaro wa indasago ahanini , wari uwo gutsirika ushyiramo umuti aho barasaze , bakungikanya na imitongero runaka yo kuvura , imitongero igakurwa na indi maze umuntu akaba mutaraga .
Kurumika ho bacaga indasago nko mu gikanu cyangwa mu mugongo , bagashyiraho ikintu bita ingunga .
Ingunga kari agacuma bakebye katagira ijosi .
Kurumika babikoraga bashaka gusohora amaraso mabi ari mu mubiri .
Hari nka ubwo imitsi yipfundikaga ikabuza umuntu kuba yagenda , ugasanga aho yipfunditse habaye nka umukara , uwo byabayeho agakunda kugira ibinya bimufata bya hato na hato .
Barasagaga ya maraso agasohoka , nyuma bagasigamo imiti yo kugira ngo homoke hasubirane , ariko na none igakiza ubwo burwayi ntibuzagaruke .
Hari na aho barumikaga bakoresheje ihembe rikiyomeka ku mubiri rikajya rikurura amaraso , ryamara kuzura bakarikuraho bakayamena bakongera bagasubizaho .
Kurasaga no kurumika , bifite itandukaniro benshi badakunze kumenya .
Kurasaga byakorerwaga ku ruhu inyuma , basharuragaho gato , hakava amaraso makeya .
Naho kurumika , byakorwaga binjiye mu mubiri imbere ku buryo bashyikira umutsi ujyana amaraso mu mubiri , akaba ariwo bakomeretsa amaraso bashaka kumena akava .
Ubuvuzi gakondo bwo kotsa ( imyotso ) amateka atugaragariza ko bwaba bukomoka mu Gisaka , aho bwadutse ku ngoma ya umwami waho Kimenyi II Shumbusho , watway I Gisaka ahasaga mu wa 1312 .
Muri icyo kibariro , mu Gisaka hadutse indwara ya amaso yafataga abana bakiri bato bakundaga kuvukana bitewe na uburwayi bwafataga Ababyeyi batwite , urukingo rukaba gufata abo bana bakabotsa ku gahanga no mu misaya , bagahita bakira .
Noneho biba nka umugenzo wo muri ako gace , abantu babona ari byiza , uvutse wese kabone na ubwo yaba atarwaye amaso bakamwotsa .
Gushyira imyotso ku gahanga no mu misaya , nibwo buvuzi gakondo bwa Abanyarwanda bifashishaga bavura icyorezo cya uburwayi bwa amaso , haba ku bana no ku bantu bakuru
Uwo mugenzo wo guca imyotso ku bana ba Abanyagisaka , wageze aho uba ikirango mwihariko wabo , uhinduka umugenzo wo guca imanzi za ubwiza ku mwana uwo ariwe wese uvukiye mu Gisaka , ku buryo byabaye na ikimenyetso cyakoreshwaga mu ntambara ya I Gisaka na u Rwanda kugira ngo Abanyagisaka babashe gutandukanya abaturage babo na Abanyarwanda .
Ubuvuzi gakondo bwa Abanyarwanda bugombora uwakomwe ( uwarumwe ) na inzoka , akabasha kuyirokoka , ni bumwe mu buvuzi gakondo bumaze igihe kirekire mu Rwanda , kuko bwahanganywe na u Rwanda rukiri amashyamba ya inzitane adapfa kwisukirwa .
Kugombora , hakoreshwaga uburyo bwo gushyira umuti witwa : a Umukubayoka " ahakomwe ( aharumwe ) na inzoka , cyangwa se bagashyira ifu ya inzoka ya inkazi babaga baraseye ( nka impiri , uruziramire na izindi ) mu gikomere cya aharumwe na inzoka .
Kugombora byaherekezwaga na imitongero ivugwa muri ubu buryo :
Ndakugombora impiri , ndakugombora idubi , Ndakugombora insana na inkomyi , Habyimbirwa imbwa , habyimbirwa impyisi , Ubwo bugomboro nabugomboje Ruganzu , Bwagomboye Rwabugili na Rudahigwa .
Ndakugombora byunga na barihuta , Na inyenzi na buhoma !
Murahura , ntikurya !
urajye kuvoma , Ntikurya !
urajya ku ryama ! ntikurya !
Murahura , ikaraba , ikarabirana , ikabura ubwenge , Ikabura ubwinyo , ikaba imbwa biseseme !
Ubuvuzi gakondo bwa Abanyarwanda bushingiye ku kurumika , kotsa , guca indasago no kugombora , bwari bwuje igenantekerezo zisobetse rwose , ku buryo ritabashaga kugerurwa na abahisi .
Ku buryo na na ubu hari aho bugikoreshwa mu kuvura indwara zimwe na zimwe .
1884 - 1885 : Uko byagenze ubwo Afurika yagabanwaga bugati na Abanyaburayi
Nyuma ya imyaka 300 yo gusahura Afurika abaturage bayo bajyanwa ku ngufu mu mirimo ya agahato na ubucakara muri Amerika , mu 1884 Abanyaburayi bahinduye umuvuno noneho bajya umugambi wo kugira Afurika iyabo .
Nyuma ya imyaka 300 yo gusahura Afurika abaturage bayo bajyanwa ku ngufu mu mirimo ya agahato na ubucakara muri Amerika , mu 1884 Abanyaburayi bahinduye umuvuno noneho bajya umugambi wo kugira Afurika iyabo .
Ni umushinga wakoranywe ubugome nka uwa mbere kuko ubuzima bwa umunyafurika icyo gihe ntacyo bwari buvuze , icyari kibaraje ishinga ni ugukungahaza ibihugu byabo basahura mutungo kamere wa Afurika .
Mu 1884 Abanyaburayi birengagije miliyoni za abanyafurika bapfiriye mu buretwa no mu nzira bajyanywe mu bucakara muri Amerika , bongera kureba ibiri mu nyungu zabo ku Mugabane wari usanzwe uri ukwawo .
Ku gicamunsi cyo kuwa Gatandatu tariki 15 Ugushyingo 1884 , i Berlin mu ngoro ya ubwami bwa u Budage izwi nka Wilhelmstrasse hateraniye inama mpuzamahanga .
Iyo nama yari yatumijwe na uwari Chancelier wa u Budage , Otto von Bismarck .
Intego nyamukuru ya iyi nama yigaragazaga ucyinjira mu cyumba kuko hari hamanitse ikarita ya Afurika ifite uburebure bwa metero eshanu igaragaza ibiyaga bya uwo mugabane , imigezi , imisozi , amazina make ya ahantu hamwe na hamwe na utudomo twa umweru hamwe na hamwe ha ingenzi .
Imbere ya ameza ya uruziga hari hicaye abayobozi ba ibihugu 13 bya i Burayi .
Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika nazo zari zatumiwe ariko zanga kwitabira kuko nta nyungu nyinshi zabonaga muri Afurika .
Iyo nama yamaze amezi atatu kuko yarangiye tariki 26 Gashyantare 1885 , ibihugu byose bimaze kwemeranya uko bizigabanya Afurika , bya umwihariko ibyifataga nka ibikomeye birimo u Budage , u Bufaransa , u Bwongereza , u Buholandi , u Bubiligi , Portugal na Espagne .
Mu kugabana bari bafite amakaramu ya ibiti , buri umwe aca imiringo aho ashaka gufata , bakabanza kubiganiraho , babyemeza ubwo bagakomereza ku wundi .
Iyo nama yamaze iminsi 104 uvanyemo akaruhuko gato bafashe ngo bajye kwizihiza iminsi mikuru ya Noheli na Ubunani .
Nyuma ya inama , ibihugu byose bya Afurika uvanyemo Liberia na Ethiopia ya ubu , byaragabanywe kandi birakolonizwa .
Nubwo ibyagabanwaga ari ubukungu bwa Afurika , nta munyafurika wigeze atumirwa muri iyo nama cyangwa ngo hagire ubahagararira .
Na umuyobozi wa Zanzibar washatse kwitumira ngo ayijyemo yakumiriwe kure na Abongereza .
Inzobere mu mateka ya Afurika , Umunyanijeriya Prof Olyaemi Akinwumi yavuze ko kugabanya Afurika byakozwe hatitawe ku mateka cyangwa imibereho ya abatuye uwo mugabane ari nazo ngorane igihura nazo .
Ati " Benshi muri Afurika twemera ko inkomoko ya amakimbirane akigaragara kuri uyu mugabane , yatangiriye mu nama ya i Berlin .
Akinwumi avuga ko nka ubwoko bwabaga bubumbiye hamwe , bwajyaga kwisanga bwashyizwe mu bihugu bitandukanye , ibihugu bimwe bikagabanyirizwa ubuso na ibindi .
Mu mabwiriza ibihugu byaganiye i Berlin byahawe , harimo ko niba igihugu cyageze ku butaka runaka bwa Afurika , buzitwa ubwacyo ari uko kibimenyesheje bigenzi byacyo i Burayi kandi kuri ubwo butaka hakoherezwayo ingabo nke .
Intego yo kujya muri Afurika kwari ukuhazana ibyo bise iterambere , kuhasakaza ubukirisitu no guteza imbere ubucuruzi bwabo .
Kugira ngo igihugu cyemererwe ko ubutaka cyafashe ari ubwacyo , cyagombaga gisinyana na abategetsi gakondo baho inyandiko yemera ko bemeye abakoloni ariko bakazahabwa uburinzi na icyo gihugu cyabakolonije .
Ibyo ntibyari bigoye dore ko abategetsi benshi muri Afurika batari bazi kwandika cyangwa gusoma .
Mu gihe cyo kugabana Afurika , uduce duke twa uwo mugabane nitwo twari twaragezwemo na Abanyaburayi .
Abenshi bari baragiye bakambika ku nkengero za uwo mugabane ku bice bikora ku nyanja .
Mu 1900 nibwo batangiye kwinjira imbere muri Afurika bashakisha ibyo kwifashisha mu nganda zabo nka amabuye ya agaciro , Caoutchouc yakoreshwaga mu nganda zikora ibinyabiziga mu Burayi na ibindi .
U Bubiligi nibwo bwabyungukiyemo cyane kuko umwami Leopold II yahawe ububasha bwo kugenzura ubutaka bwa Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , gusa ategekwa kuhubaka ku buryo haba ahantu ha ubucuruzi hagati ya Abanyaburayi bose muri Afurika , mbese buri gihugu cya i Burayi gishaka kuhisanzura kikabikora .
Mu bindi yasabwe ni ugukwirakwiza ubukiristu mu bice byose bigize Congo .
Nubwo Leopold II yari yemeye ko Congo izabyazwa umusaruro na abanyaburayi bose , siko byagenze kuko amasezerano yo gucukura no gutwara umutungo kamere wa Congo amenshi yasinyishwaga sosiyete zo mu Bubiligi .
Mu 1908 byaje kumenyekana ko ku mabwiriza ya Leopold II , abaturage ba Congo bategekwaga kujya gushaka ingano runaka ya Caoutchouc bashyira abatware ba Ababiligi , batabikora bagacibwa amaboko cyangwa ibirenge .
Leopold II yaje kwamburwa Congo iherezwa Guverinoma ya u Bubiligi .
Kuva mu 1885 kugeza mu 1908 , miliyoni za abanye - Congo zari zimaze gupfa zishwe , ziciwe amaboko , zikubiswe kubera " " " " ibikorwa bya agakiza " " " " Léopold II yari yavuze ko abazaniye , nyamara byahe byokajya .
Kugeza mu 1914 , nibura 90 % bya ibihugu bya Afurika byari mu maboko ya ibihugu birindwi bya i Burayi .
Afurika yasanze guhindura imipaka byateza ibindi bibazo bidashira
Imipaka yashyizweho na abakoloni niyo ikigenderwaho na uyu munsi .
Mu mabwiriza ibihugu byari byahawe , ni uko abaturage bakolonijwe na igihugu runaka , babaga batemerewe guhahirana na abo badahuje igihugu kibakolonije .
Akinwumi avuga ko kubera ko abenshi mu bagiye bacibwaho imipaka babaga ari abaturage bo mu bwoko bumwe , kubategeka kudahahirana kuko baciriweho imipaka byateje amakimbirane akigaragara na ubu .
Ati " Iriya nama yangije byinshi cyane muri Afurika .
Hari ibihugu bikigerwaho na ingaruka zayo uyu munsi .
Mu myaka ya 1960 , abayobozi ba ibihugu bya Afurika byari bikibona ubwigenge bashatse guhindura imipaka yashyiriweho mu nama ya i Berlin ariko basanga byateza ibibazo byinshi kurusha ibyo byakemura .
Umushakashatsi ku mateka ya ubukoloni muri Afurika , akaba na umwarimu muri Kaminuza ya Erfurt , Michael Pesek , yagize ati " Abayobozi benshi ahagana mu 1960 , bavugaga ko baramutse bayihinduye byaba ari ukwiteza ibibazo byinshi .
Inzobere zivuga ko icyo gihe nibura amakimbirane yari ashingiye hagati mu baturage atari hagati ya ibihugu .
Guhindura imipaka byari kwiyongeraho andi makimbirane hagati ya ibihugu , ibintu bikazamba kurushaho .
Mu mwaka wa 2010 ubwo hizihizwaga imyaka 125 ishize inama ya i Berlin irangiye , abari bahagarariye ibihugu bya Afurika muri uwo munsi wizihirijwe Berlin bavuze ko Afurika ikeneye impozamarira ya ibyangijwe na ubukoloni ndetse bavuga ko ibyakozwe ari ibyaha byibasiye inyokomuntu .
Nubwo basabye impozamarira , nta na kimwe cyakozwe .
Pesek yemeza ko bidatunguranye kuba ntacyo Afurika yahawe .
Ati " Hari ibindi byagiye bivugwa byo guha impozamarira Afurika kubwa ubucakara ndetse na impozamarira kubwa Jenoside yakorewe Abayahudi .
Nyamara ntawe ujya ukomoza ku myaka isaga ijana abanyaburayi bamaze muri Afurika bayikoloniza .
Ghana nicyo gihugu cya Afurika cyabashije kwigobotora bwa mbere ingoyi cyashyizweho na inama ya i Berlin , kibona ubwigenge .
Mu 2000 hafi ibihugu byose byahoze bikolonijwe muri Afurika byari bimaze kubona ubwigenge .
Ikibazo nuko byinshi mu bihugu byakolonije Afurika , na nyuma ya ubwigenge byakomeje kugira akaboko mu miyoborere ya Afurika ndetse rimwe na rimwe ushaka kubibangamira akigizwayo .
Mu kwezi gsuhize inama ya abaminisitiri mu Bufaransa , yemeje umushinga wa itegeko rihindura amasezerano bwagiranye na ibihugu umunani byo mu burengerazuba bwa Afurika ku ikoreshwa rya CFA .
Igihugu gikoresha iryo faranga cyasabwagwa kubika kimwe cya kabiri cya amafaranga na amadevize yacyo muri Banki Nkuru ya u Bufaransa .
Mutaganzwa agiye gusohora igitabo kivuga ku mpanuro za ingenzi Perezida Kagame yagiye atanga
" Tujye twirinda kumera nka isenene aho uwazifashe yazishyize kandi mu kanya zitegereje gukarangirwa hamwe " " " " ni impanuro Perezida Kagame yatanze tariki 5 Ugushyingo 2016 ubwo hizihizwaga imyaka 20 yari ishize umuryango Unity Club ushinzwe .
" Tujye twirinda kumera nka isenene aho uwazifashe yazishyize kandi mu kanya zitegereje gukarangirwa hamwe " " " " ni impanuro Perezida Kagame yatanze tariki 5 Ugushyingo 2016 ubwo hizihizwaga imyaka 20 yari ishize umuryango Unity Club ushinzwe .
Izo mpanuro ni zimwe mu zikubiye mu gitabo gishya " Isoko tuvomaho Impanuro " Mutaganzwa Charles agiye gusohora , kigaruka mu buryo buvunaguye ku mbwiraruhame za Perezida Kagame , zagize uruhare mu kubaka igihugu nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi muri Mata 1994 .
Ni igitabo gikubiyemo uduce twa impanuro Perezida Kagame yagiye atanga mu bihe bitandukanye .
Ni igitabo kirimo izo mpanuro gusa , nta bindi bitekerezo bya umwanditsi byiyongeraho .
Mutaganzwa avuga ko impanuro za Perezida Kagame zagize uruhare rukomeye mu kongera kubaka igihugu haba mu bumwe na ubwiyunge , iterambere , kwihesha agaciro , kurinda igihugu na ibindi .
Yabwiye IGIHE ko yatangiye kwandika icyo gitabo , yifuza ko izo mpanuro zikomeza kuba umusemburo wa impinduka nziza mu Rwanda ku bariho ubu na abazaza nyuma .
Yagize ati " Narebye inama yatanze tukazishingiraho twubaka igihugu nyuma ya Jenoside na uburyo yabanishije Abanyarwanda , mbona atari byiza ko twajya dukurikira imbwiraruhame ze bisanzwe ngo azivuge zigende zitambuke gusa [ … ] Ndavuga nti nubwo nta kwandika impanuro zose yavuze , ariko najya ntoranya amagambo ya ingenzi yagirira abantu akamaro ku buryo abantu basigarana impanuro ze biyubaka ubwabo
banubaka igihugu mu gihe kizaza .
Mutaganzwa yavuze ko impanuro za Perezida Kagame zifitemo ubushobozi bwo gufasha ushaka kubaka igihugu cyangwa umuryango muri rusange ndetse na umuntu ku giti cye , bya umwihariko urubyiruko .
Ati " Ushaka kubaka igihugu mu buryo bwose cyangwa kwiyubaka ubwawe , iki gitabo cyagufasha ugendeye ku mpanuro za Perezida wa Repubulika .
Urubyiruko nirwo Rwanda rwa ejo , rushingiye rero kuri izi mpanuro za nyakubahwa Perezida wa Repubulika , rwaba ari u Rwanda rumeze nkuko turwifuza .
Iki gitabo kigabanyijemo ibice 12 bivuga ko ngingo zitandukanye Perezida Kagame yagiye agarukaho mu mbwirarwaruhame ze nko kwihesha agaciro icyo ari cyo , kurinda igihugu , guteza imbere igihugu bishingiye kuri ba nyiracyo , inyungo na isomo ryo guca mu ngorane na ibindi .
Mutaganzwa yavuze ko igitabo cye " Isoko tuvomaho Impanuro " " " " kizasohoka mu minsi ya vuba ari nabwo kizatangira kuboneka mu maguriro ya ibitabo hirya no hino mu gihugu .
Ububiko bwa amateka : Umudugudu wa Nyirabwana wahoze ari igicumbi cya ingoma ya u Bwanacyambwe
Abantu benshi bakunze kwibaza uko ubutaka bwa u Rwanda bwo mu bice bimwe na bimwe bwari buteye bukiri amashyamba , butaraba igihugu gituwe kandi gihingwa , abandi bagakomeza kwibaza cyane ku bugenge na ubuhanga bukabije buvugwa ku bami bagenganga ibihugu bwa ibikorwa bya ubuhangange bagezeho kandi nta bikoresho bihambaye bari bafite .
Abantu benshi bakunze kwibaza uko ubutaka bwa u Rwanda bwo mu bice bimwe na bimwe bwari buteye bukiri amashyamba , butaraba igihugu gituwe kandi gihingwa , abandi bagakomeza kwibaza cyane ku bugenge na ubuhanga bukabije buvugwa ku bami bagenganga ibihugu bwa ibikorwa bya ubuhangange bagezeho kandi nta bikoresho bihambaye bari bafite .
Muri iki gice , tugiye kubatekerereza bimwe mu bimenyetso ndangamateka , bigaragaza imiterere ya imwe mu misozi ya u Rwanda rwo hambere , rutaraturwa ngo rube insinsiro zisakayemo abantu .
Nkuko tubikesha igitabo " Imizi ya u Rwanda " na igitabo " Intwari za imbanza , zubatse u Rwanda rugahamya igitinyiro " , byombi dukesha umwanditsi na umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , tugiye gutekerereza hamwe amateka ya umudugudu wa Nyirabwana wo mu Kagali ka Kibagabaga mu Murenge wa Kimironko ho mu Karere ka Gasabo ahahoze ari ingoma ngabe ya igihugu cya u Bwanacyambwe mu bihe byo hambere .
Hariho nka kimwe mu bimenyetso bibitse amateka akomeye agaragaza imiterere ya igihugu cya u Bwanacyambwe mbere ya uko gihangwamo igihugu , na ikimenyetso kigaragaza bene cyo uburyo bakuturanyije bakagitunganya kikaba igihugu kiganje .
Ubu butaka butaraba igihugu cya u Bwanacyambwe bwari ubutaka bwa imigina na ibishanga bya imifunzo bya amasanzure ya umugezi wa Nyabugogo na Akagera , na ikiyaga cya Mugesera .
Mu bihe byo hambere , igihugu cya u Bwanacyambwe cyari gikikijwe na ingoma ya i Gisaka cya Abagesera ba Abazirankende mu Burasirazuba , Gasabo ya Abanyiginya mu Majyaruguru , Nduga ya Ababanda mu Burengerazuba bwa Amajyepfo , u Buliza bwa Abongera mu Majyaruguru ya u Burengerazuba na ingoma ya u Bugesera bwa Abahondogo yari mu Majyepfo .
Igihugu cya u Bwanacyambwe kimwe na icy u Buliza , byagengwaga na Ibikomangoma bya Abongera , bakomoka kuri Mwongera wa Rurenge Sekuruza wabo .
Aho cyari giherereye kugeza ubwo aya mateka yandikwaga , ni mu Karere ka Nyarugenge , Akarere ka Kicukiro , Akarere ka Gasabo ya Amajyepfo ( Mu Mirenge ya Gisozi , Kinyinya , Kimihurura , Remera na Kimironko ) hamwe na Akarere ka Rwamagana ya Iburengerazuba ( Mu mirenge ya Karenge , Nyakariro , Nzige , Muyumbu na Gahengeri ) .
Amacishirizo ya ihangwa rya icyo gihugu , akaba agaragaza ko cyahanzwe mu mizo ya mbere ya iyaguka rya ibihugu byagengwaga na Abasinga ba Abasangwabutaka , aho cyahanzwe ahasaga mu wa 450 , nyuma ya Yezu Kirisitu .
Mu ihangwa rya igihugu cya u Bwanacyambwe , ryanzuwe na umuhungu wa Rurenge witwaga Mwongera na umugore we wa inkundwakazi Nyirabwanacyambwe , ari na we wakurijweho kwitirirwa icyo gihugu kikitwa " u Bwanacyambwe .
Agasozi gakuru ari nako kabarwa nka ubutaka gakondo bwa Abongera , kitwaga Nyirabwanacyambwe , niko ubu kabumbye imidugudu ya Nyirabwana , Ramiro , Rindiro na Kageyo yo mu Kagali ka Kibagabaga , mu Murenge wa Kimironko wo mu Karere ka Gasabo .
Ingoma ngabe ya Abongera ikaba yari itetse mu Mudugudu wa Nyirabwana ( Nyirabwanacyambwe ) wiswe izina rya impine , aho kuryuzuza ngo witwe " Nyirabwanacyambwe " " " " .
Nyuma ya imyaka amagana , ingoma ngabe yaje kwimurirwa mu Mudugudu wa Amahoro mu Kagali ka Rukiri II mu Murenge wa Remera wo mu Karere ka Gasabo ko mu Mujyi wa Kigali , ari naho hashyiriweho iherezo ryayo ubwo u Bwanacyambwe bwatsindwaga na u Rwanda mu gitero cyagabwe na Kigeli Mukobanya ahasaga mu wa 1378 , akivugana Nkuba ya Nyabakonjo watwaraga u Bwanacyambwe muri ibyo bihe .
Ubutaka bwa Umudugudu wa Nyirabwana , ni kimwe mu bimenyetso karundura , kigaragaza ko ingoma ya u Bwanacyambwe yabayeho , kandi ikagaragaza na inkomoko ya iryo zina , na aho yatangiriye mu bwaguke bwayo .
Imyaka 26 irashize umwamikazi wa nyuma wa u Rwanda , Rosalie Gicanda yishwe
Tariki 20 Mata 1994 nibwo inkuru mbi yakwirakwiye ko umwamikazi wa nyuma wa u Rwanda , Rosalie Gicanda yishwe na ingabo za Leta yakoraga Jenoside , azizwa ko ari umututsi .
Tariki 20 Mata 1994 nibwo inkuru mbi yakwirakwiye ko umwamikazi wa nyuma wa u Rwanda , Rosalie Gicanda yishwe na ingabo za Leta yakoraga Jenoside , azizwa ko ari umututsi .
Gicanda yashakanye na Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa Charles Léon Pierre Kuwa 13 Mutarama 1942 .
Yabayeho nabi asuzugurwa nyuma ya urupfu rwa umwami Rudahigwa , ubwo yatangiraga i Bujumbura ku buryo bwa amayobera tariki 25 Nyakanga 1959 .
Nyuma yo gutanga kwa umugabo we byajyanye na ihurura rya abarwaniraga Repubulika , ariko barushaho gutesha agaciro ingoma ya Cyami na ibimenyetso byayo .
Mu 1961 Perezida Kayibanda Grégoire yirukanye mu rukari Umwamikazi Gicanda .
Yaje gutura mu Mujyi wa Butare mu Karere ka Huye , ari naho abahoze ari abasirikare ba Habyarimana hamwe na Interahamwe bamusanze bakamwica kuwa 20 Mata 1994 .
Urupfu rwa Umwamikazi Rosali Gicanda
Muri Repubulika ya mbere na iya kabiri , umwamikazi Gicanda nubwo yari mu gihugu , yabayeho nta gaciro afite nka uwahoze mu buyobozi bukuru bwa igihugu .
Gicanda wari umuyoboke ukomeye wa Kiliziya Gatolika , yabayeho mu buzima bworoheje mu mujyi wa Huye , abana na umubyeyi we ndetse na abandi bagore bake bamufashaga mu mirimo itandukanye .
Ubwo Jenoside yatangiraga , Umwamikazi Gicanda yagiye yishingikiriza Jean Baptiste Habyarimana wari Perefe wa Butare , warwanyije cyane umugambi wo gutsemba Abatutsi .
Tariki 17 Mata , Perefe Habyarimana yatawe muri yombi , nyuma aza kwicwa .
Umwamikazi Rosalia Gicanda yatangiye guterwa ubwoba ko nawe agiye kwicwa na umuryango we .
Raporo ya Human Rights Watch yasohotse mu 1999 , ivuga ko Umwamikazi Gicanda wari ufite imyaka 66 yasabye Joseph Kanyabashi wari Burugumesitiri wa Komini ya Ngoma i Butare kumurinda , undi akabyanga .
Tariki 20 Mata ahagana saa tanu za amanywa , abasirikare bayobowe na Lt Pierre Bizimana binjiye mu rugo rwa umwamikazi Gicanda ku mabwiriza yari yatanzwe na Capt Ildephonse Nizeyimana wari umuyobozi ushinzwe ubutasi na ibikorwa mu ishuri rikuru rya gisirikare , ESO ubwo Jenoside yakorwaga .
Abo basirikare bamaze kwinjira mu rugo rwa umwamikazi , baramufashe we na abandi bagore batandatu babanaga barabatwara .
Muri urwo rugo hasigaye mama wa Gicanda wari ufite imyaka 80 na undi mukobwa wo kumwitaho .
Abasirikare bafashe Gicanda na abo bari bafatanywe bajyana inyuma ya ingoro ya inzu ndangamurage ya u Rwanda barabarasa , barapfa .
Ku gicamunsi abasirikare bagarutse mu rugo rwa Gicanda gusahura , hashize iminsi ibiri baragaruka bica umubyeyi we .
Raporo ya Huma Rihgts Watch ivuga ko hari umupadiri wasabye ko umubiri wa Gicanda washyingurwa mu cyubahiro , burugumesitiri Kanyabashi yohereza abagororwa bo kuwujyana bawushyingura hafi ya urugo rwe .
Umwe mu baganiriye na umukobwa wabashije kurokoka witaga ku mubyeyi wa Gicanda , ngo yamubwiye ko mbere ya uko Gicanda na abo bari kumwe bicwa babanje kuvuga isengesho bishyira mu maboko ya Imana .
Muri 2012 , urukiko rwashyiriweho u Rwanda rwakatiye Capt Ildephonse Nizeyimana igifungo cya burundu ashinjwa kwica Umwamikazi Gicanda na abandi batutsi muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Nizeyimana yari yafatiwe muri Uganda mu 2009 .
Mu 1998 Lt Pierre Bizimana yakatiwe urwo gupfa na urukiko rwa gisirikare i Kigali ariko icyo gihano kiza guhindurwamo igifungo cya burundu nyuma ya uko u Rwanda rukuyeho igihano cya urupfu .
Umwamikazi wicishaga bugufi , akagira impuhwe
Ababanye na abazi neza Umwamikazi Gicanda , bavuga ko yari umubyeyi wicisha bugufi kandi agakunda abantu bose atarobanuye .
Mu buhamya Perezida Paul Kagame yatanze mu 2017 avuga ku mateka ya ubuto bwe kuva afite imyaka ine ya amavuko ubwo yatangiraga ubuzima bwa ubuhunzi , yashimiye na Gicanda nka umwe mu bamufashije akabasha kurokoka .
Ubwo buhamya bugaragara mu nimero 2944 ya Jeune Afrique yasohotse ku wa 11 Kamena 2017 , yiswe amabanga ya ubuto [ Secrets de Jeunesse ] bwa abakuru ba ibihugu barimo Perezida Kagame , Ali Bongo Ondimba , Umwami Mohammed VI wa Maroc na Alpha Condé .
Perezida Kagame yasobanuye ko mu 1961 mbere gato ya uko u Rwanda rubona ubwigenge , ubwo yari afite imyaka ine , Abahutu bari batuye ku musozi wa Tambwe bashyigikiwe na ubuyobozi , bigabije aho umuryango we wari utuye batwika inzu zaho ndetse bagirira nabi Abatutsi .
Icyo gihe umubyeyi we yatangiye kumutegura ngo bahunge .
Hahise haza imodoka , umushoferi wayo ashyikiriza umubyeyi wa Perezida Kagame ibaruwa ivuga ko atumwe na Umwamikazi Gicanda wari utuye i Nyanza mu rugendo rwa iminota nka 45 uvuye aho bo bari batuye .
Rosalie Gicanda yari amusabye kubahungisha muri ibyo bihe bya amakuba .
Perezida Kagame na abantu bari baturanye binjiye muri iyo modoka mu gihe igihiriri cya ababahigaga cyaturukaga ku wundi musozi , gihita cyirara mu byo bari batunze .
Icyo gihe ngo basanze Umwamikazi i Nyanza , mbere ya uko bafata inzira bakerekeza mu Mutara aho naho ubwicanyi bwabasanze bakabuhungira muri Uganda .
Gicanda yavukiye i Rwamagana mu 1928 .
Yakuze arangwa na ikinyabupfura ari nabyo byatumye abengukwa na Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa .
Umwamikazi Gicanda aruhukiye i Mwima ya Nyanza ahatabarijwe Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa na Kigeli V Ndahindurwa .
Buri mwaka tariki 20 Mata hategurwa gahunda yo kwibuka Umwamikazi Rosalie Gicanda , itegurwa ku bufatanye bwa umuryango we na ubuyobozi bwa Ikigo cya Igihugu cya Ingoro Ndangamurage za u Rwanda .
Ibigwi na ibirindiro : Amateka na ibigwi bya inka mu Rwanda ( Igice cya mbere )
Abatekereza ba amateka ya u Rwanda na abayatekererezwa , bakunze gutangaza byinshi ku mateka ya ibigwi bya inka mu Rwanda rugari rwa Gasabo , inka yafatiweho ibintu byinshi mu mateka ya u Rwanda no mu ruhando mpuzamahanga .
Abatekereza ba amateka ya u Rwanda na abayatekererezwa , bakunze gutangaza byinshi ku mateka ya ibigwi bya inka mu Rwanda rugari rwa Gasabo , inka yafatiweho ibintu byinshi mu mateka ya u Rwanda no mu ruhando mpuzamahanga .
Muri iki gice tugiye kubavunguriraho gato ku bigwi na ibirindiro bya amateka ya ibigwi bya inka mu Rwanda , dore ko utabikuyeho akamanyu nibura gato gato , utashobora kubiva imuzi ngo ubigere imuzingo .
Nka uko tubikesha igitabo " Intwari za imbanza , zubatse u Rwanda rugahamya igitinyiro " cyanditswe na Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , inzobere ku Muco , ubusizi na amateka , tubimburiye ku iyinjira rya inka mu Rwanda na uko zatejwe imbere zikaba urufatiro rukomeye rwa ibintu byinshi mu mateka .
Inka ifite ibisekuruza byinshi mu mateka ya Afurika , aho bisaga imyaka 3000 .
Inka zahanganywe na u Rwanda , aho zadukanywe na Abasangwabutaka ba Abasinga na Abazigaba ahasaga mu wa 300 .
Abanyiginya bahasesekaye , bateje imbere cyane ubworozi bwa inka bituma inka zose zo mu gihugu bazitirirwa , aho mu mateka bagira bati " Gihanga niwe wahanze inka na ingoma " .
Bikomoye ku kuba Abanyiginya aribo bahaye intera ndende na urwego rwa ikirenga ubworozi bwa inka , ziba nyinshi mu gihugu .
Inka yahawe intera iyingayinga iya umuntu .
Aho mu Bucurabwenge bwa inka , bagiraga bati " Inka ni imfura , kuko upfa ikakurerera , wabumbira ( wabura amashereka ) ikakugoboka , ikakurwanyiriza indwara za ibyorezo na ubujyahabi " " " " .
Inka niyo yarangaga ubukire , Inka niyo yari ipfundo rya ubuhake nka akazi ko hambere , Intwari yo ku rugamba yagororerwaga inka , Inka yungaga inshuti , Inka yahuzaga inshuti ( abahanaga inka , babaga babaye inshuti ) , Inka bayikwaga umugeni nka ikimenyetso cya uburere bwiza .
Mu Kinyejana cya Munani nyuma ya Yezu , ni ukuvuga ahasaga mu wa 700 , nibwo hadutse ishyanga rishya mu Rwanda , ari ryo ryaje kuvamo umuryango mugari wa Abanyiginya , baza na ubundi , bagowe na iyimukayimuka ryabo na umutungo wabo urangajwe imbere na inka bagendaga bashakira inzuri zitoshye kandi ngari .
Mu gusesekara mu Rwanda , binjiriye bwa mbere mu Gihugu cya u Rweya rwa u Mubali ( mu mirenge ya Murundi na Mwili yo mu Karere ka Kayonza na Rwimbogo yo mu Karere ka Gatsibo ) .
Kuko ubutaka bubereye ubworozi bwa inka zabo bari babugezeho , bishimiye umukenke wa Iburasirazuba bwa u Rwanda , ugaragiwe na ubutohe bwa umurambi wa ubutaka bwiganjemo icyogogo cya uruzi rwa Akagera , ibiyaga bya Rwanyakiziga , Nasho , Ihema na ibindi .
Imyaka isaga 300 ( 700 - 1091 ) , umuryango mugari wa Abanyiginya wamaze mu busembere mu ngoma ya u Rweya rwa Abazigaba , nta kindi cyera cyangwa se cyirabura bakoze , usibye guteza imbere ubworozi bwa inka , bakora ubugenge na ubuhanga bwo kuzibangurira kugira ngo zirusheho kororoka , maze nazo zirabakundira ziroroka karahava ! !
Aha akaba ari naho , bakuye umwihariko wa inka zitirirwa u Rwanda za Inyambo aribyo bivuga " Itungo rya intoranywa " .
Imisozi yose bacumbikiwemo , yari yiganjemo inzuri za inka , aho gutura ari hato , ku buryo aribo ba mbere bateje imbere gutura mu nsisiro mu rwego rwo kurinda akajagari mu miturire byari kugabanya ingano ya inzuri za inka zabo .
Mu misozi batuyemo myinshi kuri ubu ibarizwa mu Karere ka Gatsibo ¾ byayo byari inzuri za inka .
Muri yo twavuga Imisozi ya Nyagihanga , Rugarama , Ngarama , Kabarore , Gitoki , Gatsibo na Kageyo
Imisozi batuyemo muri ibyo bihe , ari nayo baremyemo insisiro , ni mu mu Murenge wa Remera na Muhura yo mu Karere ka Gatsibo .
Uko imyaka yashiraga indi igataha , niko Abanyiginya barushagaho guteza imbere ubworozi bwa inka , ari nako butuma bagira ijambo rya icyizerabuhake mu Rweya , kugeza ubwo byabahesheje ijambo mu nzu ya ubwami bwabo , banashakamo abagore ba ibikomangoma .
Muri bo twavuga nka Nyirarukangaga rwa Nyamigezi ya Kabeja , washatswe na Kazi ka Kizira , bakabyarana Gihanga .
Abanyiginya bakomeje kugwiza ubutunzi bwa inka , amashyo na amagana , bibaha imbaraga na icyubahiro cya ikirenga , kugeza ubwo ibwami batangiye kubakeka amababa ko bashobora kuzabambura ingoma , ari nabwo Gihanga yabimenyaga agashyira nzira akabahunga ajya guhanga igihugu cye mu bisigara bya ubutaka Abasangwabutaka banennye , akabuhangaho igihugu cya i Gasabo .
Gihanga , akimara guhanga Gasabo , Umuryango mugari wa Abanyiginya akomokamo akawukura mu busembere mu ngoma ya u Rweya , yashyizeho igenamigambi ryeruye rishingiye ku nka mu kubaka igihugu cye .
Inka ihabwa umwanya ukomeye mu buzima bwose bwa igihugu , aho yifashishwaga muri Politiki za igihugu zitandukanye nko mu Bubanyi na amahanga , mu kubaka ubukungu bwa igihugu , mu mutekano no mu ntambara zo kwigarurira amahanga , mu mibereho myiza ya abaturage , mu mibanire na ubumwe bwa abenegihugu na ibindi .
Inka yayishyize mu igamigambi ry ububanyi na amahanga na ubutwererane na abami ba ibindi bihugu bituranyi bya u Rwanda ku buryo yagombaga guhuza u Rwanda na ibihugu bya inshuti kandi ikagabirwa abami b ibihugu byanga u Rwanda , bityo bikagabanya urwango , ubundi rukabasha gukora ibikorwa bya iterambere rwifuza .
Inka yabaye inkingi ya mwamba yo kurwanya umwanzi wa imbere mu gihugu .
Umwanzi wa imbere mu gihugu , burya ni ubukene .
Iyo umunyarwanda atakennye , nta nabi agira , kandi umwanzi wo hanze ya igihugu ntiyabona aho yinjirira , kuko uwakamubereye icyitso wo mu gihugu hagati , baba baramugushije ruhabo .
Nuko Gihanga , agena gahunda zo kugabira abaturage inka ku buntu , kugira ngo biteze imbere , ubundi amahoro ahinde mu miryango yabo .
Inka yashyizwe mu rwego rwo gufasha igihugu mu kugera ku mutekano na intwaro yo guhashya amahanga adakunda u Rwanda .
Niho Gihanga , yahereyeho ashyiraho gahunda yo kugabira inka Ingabo zose za igihugu , kugira ngo zirusheho kwitabira intambara zo kwivuna abanzi , no kugira imbaduko ku rugamba rwo kwagura igihugu .
Inka yafatiweho umurongo mugari wo kwigarurira imitima ya abaturage ba ibindi bihugu u Rwanda rwashakaga kwigarurira .
Aho buri muturage u Rwanda rwabaga rwanyaze mu bitero byo kurwagura , yahabwaga inka nyinshi zo korora zikamufasha kwikura mu bukene , bityo akinjira muri Paradizo nshya ya igihugu cya u Rwanda , irimo amata na ubuki , umutima akawukura kuri gakondo ya iwabo , akaganza i Rwanda .
Gahunda yo kugabira abaturage ba ibindi bihugu banyazwe na u Rwanda , yatumye benshi mu baturage batoroka ibihugu byabo , biyizira mu Rwanda , bahabwa inka zo korora , ubundi batangira gutanga amakuru ya imbamutima ya uburyo u Rwanda ruzigarurira ibihugu bakomokamo .
Ubukungu bwa ibihugu mu bihe byo hambere , bwari abaturage ku isonga , ubundi butunzi bugakurikiraho , ari nayo mpamvu u Rwanda , rwihatiye kwigarurira abaturage ba ibindi bihugu , rwifashishije inka .
Impamvu igitabo kidakwiriye kubura mu mpano uha uwo ukunda
Mu buzima bwa umuntu bwa buri munsi , akenera kugura ikintu akeneye kimuneza , kimukemurira ibibazo , kimuteza imbere ndetse kinamwubaka .
Mu buzima bwa umuntu bwa buri munsi , akenera kugura ikintu akeneye kimuneza , kimukemurira ibibazo , kimuteza imbere ndetse kinamwubaka .
Abantu bamwe baha agaciro kadakwiye igitabo , ntibazi ko igitabo aricyo shingiro rya iterambere rirambye , ishingiro rya ubuzima bwiza , ishingiro rya ubwenge , ishingiro rya imibereho myiza , ishingiro ryo kubaka igihugu , ishingiro ryo gusigasira igihango ndetse igitabo ni ishingiro ryo kugira igenamigambi rirambye .
Njya nibaza ibibazo bikurikira : Kuki umuntu agura umwenda wa ibihumbi ijana ariko akumva atagura igitabo cya ibihumbi ijana ?
Kuki umuntu agura mudasobwa ya ibihumbi magana atanu ariko akumva atagura igitabo cya ibihumbi magana atanu ?
Kuki umuntu agura ururabo rwo guha inshuti ye ariko akaba atamuha impano ya igitabo ?
Mu mwaka wa 2016 , hari inshuti yanjye yitwa Ken Chartrand twigeze kuganira turi gutembera i New York , ambwira ko mu mpano nziza ashobora guha umuntu akunda ko hadashobora kuburamo igitabo , mubajije impamvu arambwira ngo igitabo ni inshuti nziza muganira ukunguka ubwenge na ubuhanga , kikaba urwibutso rurambye kandi rudashira .
Ken yambwiye ko igitabo ari urwibutso rwa ubushuti , ko buri kwezi agura ibitabo bibiri byo gusoma kandi ko adashobora kuryama adasomye igitabo kuko gituma aruhuka neza , akunguka ubumenyi burushijeho .
Nyuma ya ikiganiro twagiranye , nahise nkunda birushijeho igitabo , mpitamo kwimakaza umuco wo kwandika , kugura ndetse no gusoma ibitabo .
Kugeza ubu maze kwandika ibitabo bine .
Mu biro byanjye harimo ibitabo naguze nsoma kenshi , mu rugo umuryango wanjye nawuguriye ibitabo byo gusoma kandi bamaze kubikunda .
Birakwiye ko twimakaza uyu muco mwiza ufasha kubaka u Rwanda twifuza ndetse na Afurika , tugura ibitabo , tubiha agaciro gakomeye , tubitangamo impano ku nshuti dukunda , tubisoma aho turi hose , bityo bizadufashe kurushaho gutera imbere dufite ubuhanga bwimbitse .
Ibi kandi bizadufasha kwihuta mu iterambere ndetse turusheho kumenya aho tuva , aho tugeze ndetse na icyerekezo cya u Rwanda na Afurika .
Bizadufasha kurushaho kuba abarinzi ba ibyagezweho mu Rwanda no muri Afurika bityo tubisigasire ndetse tunabyubakireho ibindi bikorwa byinshi kandi byiza .

Imiryango yahamije ubuhangange mu mateka : Igicumbi cya Umuryango wa Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka
Mu mateka ya abakurambere mpangarwanda , hari imiryango yagiye ihamya ibirindiro , ikavugwa cyane ku bwa ibigwi na ibirindiro yabaga yarakoreye igihugu , hagati mu muryango mugari ikomokamo .
Mu mateka ya abakurambere mpangarwanda , hari imiryango yagiye ihamya ibirindiro , ikavugwa cyane ku bwa ibigwi na ibirindiro yabaga yarakoreye igihugu , hagati mu muryango mugari ikomokamo .
Muri iki gice tukaba tugiye kubimburira ku mateka ya igicumbi cya umuryango mugari ufite inkomoko ku Mwami Yuhi Mazimpaka twifashishije igitabo " Iyororoka rya Abanyarwanda , inkomoko ya imiryango migari " dukesha Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , inzobere mu Busizi , Umuco na Amateka ya u Rwanda .
Yuhi III Mazimpaka ni mwene Sekarongoro Gisanura cya Kigeli Nyamuheshera , Umunyiginya wo mu nzu ya Abaganzu na Nyamarembo ya Majinya , ukomoka mu muryango mugari wa Abakono , wategetse ahasaga mu wa 1642 kugeza mu wa 1675 .
Ni umwami wa 18 muri 28 bategetse u Rwanda , akaba na umwami wa 18 mu Berekeza 34 ba umushinga wo kubaka u Rwanda , kugeza ubwo aya mateka yandikwaga .
Izina rye rya ubutwari ryari " Insarikanamakuza .
Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka ni umwe mu Bami ba u Rwanda bagize inzu za imiryango nyinshi ugereranyije na abandi bami , akaba akurikira Ndoba na we wagize inzu za imiryango ntabarika .
Amateka atugaragariza ko Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka ya Gisanura , yabyaye abana benshi , biganjemo abahungu 10 barimo Rwaka , Rujugira , Nyarwaya , Gakomba , Mureganshuro , Gapfizi , Mukungu , Mukuku , Rushara na Bukombe .
Umuryango wa Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka wabayemo ingabo za ibikongote ku ngoma ye na iy umuhungu we Cyilima Rujugira wamuzunguye ku ngoma .
Banabaye abagaba ba ingabo ba intahusha mu gihe cye .
Imitwe ya Ingabo yatwarwaga na abahungu be , irimo Indara zatwarwagwa na Mukungu wa Yuhi Mzimpaka ,
Inkoramaraso : Zatwarwaga na Mukungu wa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Abashahuzi : Batwarwaga na Nyarwaya Karuretwa wa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Ababaga : Batwarwaga na Nyarwaya Karuretwa wa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Ababanda : Batwarwaga na Nyarwaya Karuretwa wa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Inkuba : Zatwarwaga na Mureganshuro ya Yuhi Mazimpaka
Abakungu : Batwarwaga na Mureganshuro ya Yuhi Mazimpaka
Abatabaga : Batwarwaga na Yuhi Mazimpaka za Gisanura
Intaremba : Zatwarwaga na Yuhi Mazimpaka ya Gisanura
Hari na ababaye abagaba ba ingabo ku ngoma ya umuhungu we akaba na umuvandimwe wabo Cyilima Rujugira , aribo aba bakurikira :
Abakemba : Batwarwaga na Sharangabo ya Cyilima Rujugira ,
Imvejuru : Zatwarwaga na Sharangabo ya Cyilima Rujugira ,
Indirira ( Rugamba ) : Zatwarwaga na Muciye ya Serutaro rwa Mukuku wa Mazimpaka ,
Abarima : Batwarwaga na Mitunga ya Cyilima Rujugira na umugabo we Seruhuga ,
Abatanyagwa : Batwarwaga na Gihana cya Cyilima Rujugira ,
Intarindwa : Zatwarwaga na Ndabarasa ba Cyilima Rujugira ,
Ababito : Batwarwaga na Ndabarasa ba Cyilima Rujugira ,
Indara : Zatwarwaga na Cyilima Rujugira rwa Yuhi Mazimpaka ,
Ababanda : Batwarwaga na Cyilima Rujugira rwa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Aba bagabo ba Intarumikwa , ni bo babaye inkomoko ya inzu za imiryango zo kwa Mazimpaka zikomoka mu muryango mugari wa Abanyiginya .
Inzu za imiryango zikomoka kwa Yuhi Mazimpaka ni izi zikurikira :
Abanyiginya ba ABAKA bakomoka kuri Karemera Rwaka rwa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Abanyiginya ba ABAYA bakomoka kuri Nyarwaya rwa Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya ba ABASIGAYE bakomoka kuri Nsigaye ya Gakombe ka Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya ba Abahwege bakomoka kuri Segahwege ka Nsigaye ya Gakombe ka Yuhi mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya ba ABAPFIZI bakomoka kuri Gapfizi ka Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya ba ABAREGANSHURO bakomoka kuri Mureganshuro ya Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya ba Abashamakokera bakomoka kuri Shamakokera ya Ndabaramiye wa Bukombe bwa Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya ba ABASAMANZI bakomoka kuri Rwasamanzi rwa Mukungu ya Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya ba Abakuku bakomoka kuri Mukuku wa Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya ba Abashara bakomoka kuri Rushara rwa Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Izindi nzu zihamye mu mateka ya u Rwanda zikomoka kwa Yuhi Mazimpaka , harimo na izo kwa Cyilima Rujugira umuhungu we wa ubuheta wabaye umwami wa Rubanda akamuzungura ku ngoma .
Inzu zimukomokaho zirimo Abanyiginya ba Abadenge bakomoka kuri Mudenge wa Cyilima Rujugira ;
Abanyiginya ba Abakore bakomoka kuri Kanyankore ka Kanyoni ka Baziga ba Cyilima Rujugira ;
Abanyiginya ba Abahabanyi bakomoka kuri Bihabanyi bya Gashikazi ka Cyilima Rujugira ;
Abanyiginya ba Abamo bakomoka kuri Rwamo rwa Gihana cya Cyilima Rujugira ;
Abanyiginya ba Abanana bakomoka kuri Munana wa Gihana cya Cyilima Rujugira ;
Abanyigiya ba Abasharangabo bakomoka kuri Sharangabo ya Cyilima Rujugira .
Abanyabugeni ba abagore bahawe umwihariko mu kwizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wa Ingoro Ndangamurage
U Rwanda ruritegura kwifatanya na Isi mu birori bya Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Ingoro Ndangamurage uzizihizwa hatangizwa imurika rya ibihangano bya ubugeni bya abahanzi ba abari na abategarugori .
U Rwanda ruritegura kwifatanya na Isi mu birori bya Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Ingoro Ndangamurage uzizihizwa hatangizwa imurika rya ibihangano bya ubugeni bya abahanzi ba abari na abategarugori .
Buri mwaka tariki 18 Gicurasi Isi yizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Ingoro Ndangamurage , hazirikanwa umuco , amateka na imibereho gakondo bya abatuye Isi .
U Rwanda narwo rwifatanya na amahanga mu kwizihiza uwo munsi ushimangira agaciro ko guhererekanya amateka no guteza imbere umuco ufatwa nka umusingi wa imibereho ya igihugu .
Urwa Gasabo rubarizwa mu Muryango Mpuzamahanga wa Ingoro Ndangamurage ( ICOM ) uhuriyemo abanyamuryango basaga 44 000 bakora mu ngoro ndangamurage 20 000 zo mu bihugu 138 .
Muri uyu mwaka , uyu munsi wahawe insanganyamatsiko ivuga ku kugira " Ingoro ndangamurage zigamije uburinganire , ubudasa no kudaheza " .
Kuri iyi nshuro iki gikorwa cyateguwe mu buryo bwihariye aho hazifashishwa ikoranabuhanga bitewe na ingamba zashyizweho zo guhangana na ikwirakwira rya icyorezo cya COVID - 19 .
Ni muri urwo rwego Ingoro ndangamurage zo mu bihugu binyamuryango bya ICOM zasabwe kucyizihiza hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga .
Ikigo cya Ingoro za Igihugu za Umurage wa u Rwanda ( INMR ) cyizizihiza ibi birori hafungurwa ku mugaragaro imurika rishya mu Ngoro ya Ubugeni na Ubuhanzi iherereye i Kanombe , ku wa 18 Gicurasi 2020 .
Iri murika rya ibihangano bya ubugeni ryahawe insanganyamatsiko ivuga iti " Ubutumwa bwa abanyabugeni ba Abanyarwandakazi : Uburinganire kuri bose .
Ni insanganyamatsiko yari yagenwe ku Munsi Mpuzamahanga wa Abari na Abategarugori [ yasubitswe kubera ingamba zo guhangana na Coronavirus ] , ariko inahurirana na iyatanzwe na ICOM uyu mwaka wa 2020 .
Iyo urebye mu byiciro bitandukanye bibarizwamo abari na abategarugori mu Rwanda , usanga baragize uruhare mu bikorwa bya iterambere rya ubukungu na imibereho myiza ya abaturage nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 ; ariko basigara inyuma mu bijyanye na ubugeni bitewe na impamvu zirimo ubushobozi buke , kubura amahugurwa ahagije mu bijyanye na ubugeni na izindi mbogamizi zo mu buzima busanzwe .
Ushingiye no ku bihangano bimuritse mu Ngoro ya Ubugeni na Ubuhanzi ya i Kanombe " Hari icyuho kinini hagati ya ibihangano bya abagore na abagabo .
Ibi ntibisobanuye ko badashoboye , bafite impano muri bo kuko na bake bari muri uwo mwuga bakora ibihangano byiza cyane , bimwe muri byo bifite ubwiza burenze ibya basaza babo .
Imurika rizakorwa nka uburyo bwo gukora ubukangurambaga mu bari na abategarugori , binyuze mu butumwa bukubiye mu nsanganyamatsiko ya imurika no mu bihangano byabo byateguwe kandi bizamurikwa , bakangurirwa kwigirira icyizere , gutinyuka no kugaragaza impano bafite mu bya ubugeni .
Iri murika ryateguwe hagamijwe gufasha abahanzikazi bato no kubaharurira inzira zo kungukira mu bikorwa byabo ; gufasha abanyabugeni ba abagore gutegura ibikorwa byo kumurika ibihangano byabo ; kwerekana agaciro ko gushora mu bushobozi bwa umugore no kubafasha kugeza imishinga yabo ku rwego mpuzamahanga , byanafasha abandi kubigiraho .
Rizahuza abanyabugeni ba abari na abategarugori 35 bo mu bihugu bitandatu birimo u Rwanda , Amerika , u Bufaransa , u Bubiligi , Serbia na Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
INMR yateguye iri murika ifatanyije na Ikigo Ndangamuco cya Abadage Goethe Institut - Kigali .
Ibyo bigo byombi byafashije abari na abategarugori ba abanyabugeni mu kuritegura , kubaha amahugurwa na ubushobozi bwo gukora ibihangano byabo no gutunganya imurika riboneye .
Umuhango wo kwizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wa Ingoro Ndangamurage uzanyuzwa kuri murandasi ( Webex ) ku wa 18 Gicurasi 2020 saa Cyenda .
Abifuza kuwukurikirana baziyandikisha bohereza ubutumwa kuri [ email protected ] cyangwa bakandikira ikigo banyuze ku mbuga nkoranyambaga .
Biteganyijwe ko umukozi wa Ingoro ndangamurage azasobanurira abazakurikira iki gikorwa ibijyanye na imurika , ababwira ubutumwa bukubiye mu bihangano bigize imurika nkuko bigenda mu gihe bari gusura bisanzwe .
U Rwanda rufite Ingoro za Umurage umunani zimuritse umurage na amateka bya igihugu ku mibereho ya abagituye , imyemerere , imyidagaduro , imyambarire , imiziro na imiziririzo , amateka yacyo .
Nyuma ya gahunda ya Guma mu rugo yashyizweho mu kwirinda ikwirakwira rya COVID - 19 , ibikorwa byo gufungura imiryango ku basura ingoro ndangamurage byarasubukuwe ku wa 5 Gicurasi 2020 .
Imihango na imigenzo yakorwaga na Abanyarwanda mu kwirukana ibiza na ibyorezo
Mu bihe byo ha mbere mu Rwanda iyo hadukaga ibiza bya umwuzure na amapfa na ibyorezo bya indwara za abantu na amatungo bikayogoza igihugu , habagaho imihango na imigenzo yakorwaga kugira ngo ibyo byorezo bigende .
Mu bihe byo ha mbere mu Rwanda iyo hadukaga ibiza bya umwuzure na amapfa na ibyorezo bya indwara za abantu na amatungo bikayogoza igihugu , habagaho imihango na imigenzo yakorwaga kugira ngo ibyo byorezo bigende .
Imihango yakorwaga ahanini yabaga ishingiye ku biteganywa na Ubwiru , umwuga wa Ubupfumu , Ubuvubyi Ubuhennyi , Ubuhoryo na Ubuhaditsi .
Igitabo " Imizi ya u Rwanda " " " " cyanditswe na Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , inzobere mu muco , amateka na Ubuvanganzo , havugwamo ko buri cyorezo cyateraga u Rwanda , habaga hari uburyo bwateguwe bwo kucyohera cyangwa kukirukana bakoreshejwe imwe muri iyo migenzo na imihango yashyizwe u Rwanda rwahangwaga .
Inzira ya Kivu : Ni inzira yabagamo urwunge rwa imihango yakorwaga mu gihe mu gihugu habaga hateye umwuzure ukangiza byinshi mu gihugu .
Bakoraga imihango yo kwirunka uwo mwuzure .
Inzira ya Muhekenyi : Ni inzira yabagamo urwunge rwa imihango yakorwaga mu gihe habaga hateye ibyonnyi na indwara za amatungo , bityo hagakorwa imihango na imigenzo yo kuyohera .
Nyuma ya imihango ya ibwami ijyanye na ubwiru bwo kohera ibiza na ibyorezo , hakurikiragaho abahanga gakondo mu kuvura icyateye icyo cyorezo no kucyohera ntikizagaruke .
Bamwe muri bo bakoraga iyo mihango , ni aba bakurikira :
Abavubyi : Mu Rwanda rwo ha mbere , abavubyi bari bafite umumaro uhanitse mu mibereho myiza ya abaturage cyane cyane mu buhinzi .
Umwuga wabo gakondo wari uwo kuvuba imvura ikagwa iyo yabaga yahagamye , no kuyohera ikagenda iyo yabaga yaciye ibintu .
Iyo habaga hateye amapfa cyangwa se umwuzure , icyo gihe nibwo abavubyi nka inzobere mu kumanura imvura bahagurukaga bagakora imihango yo kuyimanura ikagwa , amapfa akagenda .
Iyo yabaga yaciye ibintu hakaba umwuzure , nabwo bakoraga imihango yo kuyohera .
Abahoryo : Abahoryo nabo ni bamwe mu banyamihango ba ibwami bagiraga uruhare runini ku gukurikirana ibihingwa mu murima no kuvura ibyonnyi bya indwara zabaga zadutse mu myaka .
Barahagurukaga bagakora imihango yo kuvuma ibyo byonnyi no kuvuguta imiti yo kubyamurura ku butaka bwa u Rwanda .
Abahaditsi : Ni bamwe mu banyamihango ba ibwami bari bagiraga uruhare runini ku gukurikirana indwara za amatungo zabaga zadutse mu bworozi bwa I Rwanda .
Icyo gihe nibwo Abahaditsi barahagurukaga bagakora imihango yo kuvuguta imiti yo kubyamurura mu Rwanda .
Abahennyi : Abahennyi nabo bari bamwe mu banyamihango ba ibwami bifashishwaga mu kuvura indwara za ibyorezo zibasiye abantu no kuvuma ababisha banga u Rwanda .
Iyo habaga hateye ibyorezo bya indwara , icya mbere bakoraga ni ukumenya inkomoko yabyo , basanga ari ibirogano bagahenera uwabikoze akaba ikivume , basanga ari icyorezo cya inzaduka bakagishakira amasubyo yo kucyohera .
Nibo batangaga amasubyo yo kuvura amahumane , ibinyoro , ubushita na izindi .
Mu kwamurura no kohera ibyozezo bya indwara za abantu na amatungo , Abanyarwanda bifashishaga kandi amazi ya ubuhoro , yeza igihugu agakiza ubwandure akamurura ibiza bya indwara na umuze byazengereje igihugu .
Bigaragaza ko kuva kera Abanyarwanda bari bafite ubuhanga na ubushobozi bifashishaga mu guhashya umwanzi wa ubuzima bwabo na ibyabo .
Ni abantu bakoresheje ubwenge bwa umwimerere mu kwirwanaho bahagarara ku buzima bwabo ngo butaganzwa na ibyorezo bya indwara na ibiza bya amapfa na imyuzure .
Gukena Afurika yabihisemo : Ibidasanzwe mu gitabo gishya cya Apôtre Mutabazi
Apôtre Mutabazi Kabarira ( Brain ) yasohoye igitabo " " " " African Poverty is a Choice " " " " cyinjira mu mizi ya ubukene bwa Afurika na inkomoko yabwo na uburyo Abanyafurika babwivanamo baramutse babishatse .
Apôtre Mutabazi Kabarira ( Brain ) yasohoye igitabo " " " " African Poverty is a Choice " " " " cyinjira mu mizi ya ubukene bwa Afurika na inkomoko yabwo na uburyo Abanyafurika babwivanamo baramutse babishatse .
Iki gitabo cyagiye hanze mu minsi ishize , gikubiyemo ingingo zitandukanye zigaragaza ibyahejeje Afurika mu bukene , uko ibindi bihugu byabashije kwiteza imbere na uburyo buri munyafurika abigize ibye akiheraho , uyu mugabane warenga indi yose mu bukire .
Apôtre Mutabazi mu gitabo cye " " " " African Poverty is a Choice " " " " avuga ko ikibazo gikomeye Abanyafurika bafite ari uko bataramenya aho ikibazo bafite gituruka , bagashaka buri gihe guhirikira ibibazo ku bandi , batarebye bo ubwabo icyo bakora ngo bikemuke .
Yagize ati " Buri muntu afite ubushobozi buri muri we na impano arusha abandi bantu , ariko abantu benshi babaho ubuzima bwo kutayimenya no kutayikoresha mu mwuzuro wayo , ari nacyo kibazo Afurika ifite , ntabwo bajya bizera ubushobozi bifitemo .
" Usanga Umunyafurika yarageze ahantu yiyakira .
Umuntu akavuga ngo njye ndi umucuruzi ukomeye , nzajya njya kurangura mu Bushinwa nze mbicuruze bagenzi banjye njye hariya ngagare kandi aho uvuye kubirangura ababikora bavukiye icyenda nka ayo wavukiye .
Mutabazi yagaragaje ko abantu benshi batekereza ko ubukene bwa Afurika buterwa na ubuyobozi , nyamara we iyo asesenguye avuga ko ubuyobozi atari cyo kibazo kuko nta wakoze ibifitiye Afurika inyungu ngo asubizwe inyuma .
Ati " Abantu benshi baravuga ngo muri Afurika haba igitugu , ibyo nzapfa ntabyemeye .
Muri politiki wenda harimo gukanira kandi nabyo bifite impamvu kuko Abanyafurika kubera inzara bafite barashonje kandi bararakaye .
Ikibazo ni uko barakariye umuntu utari we .
Yavuze ko abayobozi icyo bashinzwe ari ugushyiraho imirongo migari no gufasha abagize igitekerezo kizima ariko badashinzwe gutekerereza umuntu .
Mutabazi yagaragaje ko ikibazo kiri ahantu hatandukanye harimo na uburezi , aho umwarimu atanga bike ku munyeshuri cyangwa se umwanya munini bakawumara biga ibyo batazakoresha mu buzima .
Mu gitabo " " " " African Poverty is a Choice " " " " kandi Mutabazi anenga uburyo abanyabwenge ba Afurika basa nka aho ntacyo bayimariye , aho barangiza kuminuza bakaza baje gusaba akazi aho gukoresha ibyo bize bafasha Afurika kuvumbura no gukemura ibibazo bihari .
Yanenze na Guverinoma za Afurika uburyo zifata abitwa ko ari abahanga ( aba - génies ) bagashyirwa mu myanya ya ubuyobozi itabafasha gushyira mu bikorwa ibyo bize .
Kuri we asanga mu buyobozi , abahanga badakwiriye kurenga 30 % , abandi bakajya gukora ibyo bize .
Ku bitwaza abakoloni ngo nibo bahejeje Afurika inyuma , Apôtre Mutabazi yabihakanye avuga ko ibyo biri mu nyungu zabo nta kosa ririmo , ahubwo ikosa riri ku banyafurika batamenya icyo bakeneye ngo babikumire .
Ati " Inzira abanyafurika turi gucamo ngo tuve mu bukene , si iyo ibihugu biri kudutera inkunga byaciyemo .
U Burayi na Amerika bizahora iteka bihari kugira ngo biduhe intwaro nituvuga ko turambiwe abayobozi twita abanyagitugu ariko nituvuga ko dukeneye Kaminuza ya Harvard cyangwa MIT ngo bayitwubakire , na aho wababwira ko ari ku ideni bazakubwira ngo cira birarura .
Mutabazi kandi yerekana ko Abanyafurika ubwabo bakomeza kudakoresha ubushobozi bifitemo , aho atanga urugero rwa umuntu wumva ko akomeye akajya kurangura mu mahanga , nyamara atabasha gukopera ibyo ajya kurangura ngo umunsi umwe nawe azabikorere mu gihugu cye , mu gihe ariyo nzira ibihugu byinshi nka u Bushinwa na u Buyapani byagiye bikoresha ngo bitere imbere .
Ikindi atangaho inama kizavana Afurika mu bukene , ni ukudatekereza amafaranga mbere ya ibindi byose kuko bituma badashyira umwanya ku byagira akamaro ka igihe kirekire .
Ati " Ibintu bituma abantu bakena ni uguhora iteka batekereza babanjirije ku mafaranga .
Umurwa mukuru wa Portugal uzakira imikino ya ¼ , ½ na umukino wa nyuma , yose izakinwa hagati ya tariki ya 12 na iya 23 Kanama uyu mwaka .
Imikino yose isigaye izajya ikinwa ari umwe ( nta mukino wo kwishyura ) mu byiciro bitandukanye , izabera ku bibuga bibiri byo muri Lisbon - Estadio da Luz na Estadio Jose Alvalade .
Byitezwe ko iyi gahunda yo gukina imikino isigaye nka irushanwa rito , izemezwa na Komite Nyobozi ya UEFA mu nama izaba ku wa Gatatu tariki ya 17 Kamena 2020 .
Imikino ya ¼ izaba hagati ya tariki ya 12 na iya 15 Kanama , iya ½ ibe hagati ya tariki y 18 na iya 19 Kanama mu gihe umukino wa nyuma uzaba tariki ya 23 Kanama .
Uburyo imikino ine isigaye ya 1 / 8 izakinwa na byo bigomba kwemezwa .

Nta cyemezo kirafatwa ku irushanwa rya Europa League rya uyu mwaka , ariko byitezwe ko naryo rizakinwa muri ubu buryo , rigasorezwa mu Mujyi wa Frankfurt cyangwa uwa Düsseldorf mu Budage .
Ku bijyanye na irushanwa rya umwaka utaha wa imikino , UEFA iri kwiga uburyo imikino ya amatsinda yatangira mu Ukwakira hagati mu gihe ubusanzwe habaga hari gusozwa imikino ibanza yo mu matsinda .
Simba SC ikinamo Kagere Meddie yegukanye Shampiyona ya Tanzania ku nshuro ya gatatu yikurikiranya
Simba SC ikinamo Umunyarwanda Kagere Meddie , yegukanye igikombe cya gatatu cyikurikiranya cya Shampiyona ya Icyiciro cya Mbere muri Tanzania nyuma yo kunganya ubusa ku busa na Tanzania Prisons mu mukino wabaye kuri iki Cyumweru kuri Stade Sokoine i Mbeya .
Simba SC ikinamo Umunyarwanda Kagere Meddie , yegukanye igikombe cya gatatu cyikurikiranya cya Shampiyona ya Icyiciro cya Mbere muri Tanzania nyuma yo kunganya ubusa ku busa na Tanzania Prisons mu mukino wabaye kuri iki Cyumweru kuri Stade Sokoine i Mbeya .
Muri uyu mukino wa umunsi wa 32 , umuholandi Sven Vandenbroeck yari yagiriye icyizere Kagere Meddie wakinnye iminota yose ya umukino .
Simba SC yari ikeneye inota rimwe kugira ngo yegukanye igikombe nyuma ya uko Azam FC yanganyije na Biashara United igitego 1 - 1 ikagira amanota 59 mu gihe Yanga SC yatsinze Ndanda FC ibitego 3 - 2 ku wa Gatanu , ikagira amanota 60 .
Umunyezamu wa Tanzania Prisons , Jeremiah Kasubi na Aishi Manula urinda izamu rya Simba SC bagize uruhare rukomeye mu gutuma uyu mukino urangira nta gitego kiwubonetsemo .
Kunganya byatumye Simba SC igira amanota 79 mu mikino 32 , yegukana igikombe harimo ikinyuranyo cya amanota 19 mu gihe hasigaye imikino itandatu .
Ni ku nshuro ya gatatu yikurikiranya iyi kipe yegukanye iki gikombe mu gihe ari ku nshuro ya 21 yegukanye shampiyona ya Tanzania , irushwa inshuro eshanu na Yanga SC igifite inshuro 26 .
Kuri Kagere Meddie , ni igikombe cya kabiri cya shampiyona yegukanye ari kumwe na Simba SC nyuma yo kuyigeramo mu mwaka wa imikino wa 2018 / 19 , avuye muri Gor Mahia FC yo muri Kenya .
Biteganyijwe ko Simba SC izashyikirizwa igikombe mu mikino iri imbere bitewe na ibiganiro bizahuza ubuyobozi bwayo na abayobora Ishyirahamwe rya Umupira wa Amaguru muri Tanzania ( TFF ) .
AS Muhanga yabonye umutoza mushya wa Umurundi
Umurundi Nduwantare Ismail Jean Marie Vianney ni we wemejwe nka umutoza mushya wa AS Muhanga , ku masezerano ya umwaka umwe ushobora kongerwa .
Umurundi Nduwantare Ismail Jean Marie Vianney ni we wemejwe nka umutoza mushya wa AS Muhanga , ku masezerano ya umwaka umwe ushobora kongerwa .
AS Muhanga nta mutoza yari ifite nyuma ya uko Mbarushimana Abdu wayitozaga yerekeje muri Bugesera FC mu kwezi gushize .
Iyi kipe yabaye iya 11 mu mwaka ushize wa imikino wa 2019 / 20 , yari imaze iminsi iri mu biganiro na abarimo Ruremesha Emmanuel nyuma wasinyiye Gorilla FC , Nduwantare Ismail na Bisengimana Justin .
Umunyamabanga Mukuru wa AS Muhanga , Bisangwabagabo Youssuf , yabwiye IGIHE ko bamaze kwemeza Nduwantare Ismail nka umutoza mushya ku masezerano ya umwaka umwe .
Ati " Nibyo umutoza twamaze kumubona , ni Nduwantare Jean Ismail Marie Vianney , twamuhaye amasezerano ya umwaka umwe ushobora kongerwa mu gihe byaba bigenze neza .
" Intego yacu ni ugukomeza kuzamura abakinnyi bakiri bato kandi beza ariko tukaguma mu cyiciro cya mbere .
Nduwantare yaherukaga mu Rwanda mu mwaka ushize ubwo yatozaga Gicumbi FC , ariko akaba yarirukanwe mu Ugushyingo nyuma ya amezi abiri gusa , kubera umusaruro muke .
Ni ku nshuro ya gatatu , Nduwantare aje gutoza mu Rwanda nyuma yo kuba umutoza Aspor FC mu 2008 mbere ya uko asubira muri Prince Louis , ayifasha gusubira mu cyiciro cya mbere .
Yatoje kandi amakipe arimo Inter Stars , Flambeau de la Est , Kayanza United , Delta Star na Les Jeunes Athletics za iwabo mu Burundi .
Hatangajwe igihe Shampiyona ya NBA izasubukurirwa ikinwa mu buryo bwihariye
Shampiyona ya Basketball muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ( NBA ) ikunzwe kurusha izindi ku Isi , yatangaje ko izasubukurwa tariki ya 30 Nyakanga nyuma ya uko ihagaze guhera muri Werurwe kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Shampiyona ya Basketball muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ( NBA ) ikunzwe kurusha izindi ku Isi , yatangaje ko izasubukurwa tariki ya 30 Nyakanga nyuma ya uko ihagaze guhera muri Werurwe kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Kuri iki Cyumweru tariki ya 27 Kamena nibwo hashyizwe ahagaragara imikino izakinwa hagati ya tariki ya 30 Nyakanga na iya 14 Kanama 2020 .
Amakipe 22 azitabira isubukurwa rya NBA , azakina imikino umunani ( kuri buri imwe ) izabera ku bibuga bya ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex i Walt Disney World Resort muri Florida .
Imikino ibiri izabimburira indi ku wa Kane tariki ya 30 Nyakanga ni uzahuza Utah Jazz na New Orleans Pelicans , ndetse na uzahuza LA Clippers na Los Angeles Lakers mu gihe bukeye bwaho , tariki ya 31 Nyakanga , hazaba imikino itandatu irimo uwo Boston Celtics izakinamo na Milwaukee Bucks naho Houston Rockets ihure Dallas Mavericks .
Muri iri subukurwa rya NBA , buri munsi hazajya hakinwa imikino igera kuri irindwi ku bibuga bitatu bitandukanye byo muri ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex .
Buri kipe izabarwa nka iyakiriye imikino ine ndetse yongere kugirwa nka iyakiniye hanze mu yindi mikino ine .
Ubwo NBA yasubikwagwa tariki ya 11 Werurwe , hari hasigaye imikino 259 mu mwaka usanzwe wa imikino ariko hazakinwa 88 gusa .
Amakipe 22 azakina iyi mikino ni umunani yari aya mbere muri buri gace ( conference ) [ ni ukuvuga ane muri buri gace ] kongeraho andi atandatu ( atanu yo mu Burengerazuba na imwe yo mu Burasirazuba ) hagendewe ku manota yari afite .
Iyi mikino izasozwa tariki ya 14 Kanama mu gihe biteganyijwe ko hazabaho play - in izahuza ikipe ya munani na iya cyenda muri buri gace hagati ya tariki ya 15 na iya 16 Kanama mu gihe byaba bibaye ngombwa .
Iya Play - offs yitabirwa na amakipe umunani ya mbere muri buri gace , izatangira tariki ya 17 Kanama 2020 ikageza mu Ukwakira .
Rayon Sports yavuze ku isinyishwa rya Nishimwe Blaise na abandi bakinnyi
Ubuyobozi bwa Rayon Sports buvuga ko butarasinyisha Nishimwe Blaise ukina muri Marines FC gusa bwemeza ko ari mu bakinnyi bari kuganirizwa kugira ngo bazayikinire mu mwaka utaha wa imikino .
Ubuyobozi bwa Rayon Sports buvuga ko butarasinyisha Nishimwe Blaise ukina muri Marines FC gusa bwemeza ko ari mu bakinnyi bari kuganirizwa kugira ngo bazayikinire mu mwaka utaha wa imikino .
Bivugwa ko Nishimwe Blaise yasinye amasezerano ya imyaka itatu ku wa Gatanu ndetse ari mu bakinnyi bashya Rayon Sports yamaze kugura .
Umuvugizi wa Rayon Sports , Nkurunziza Jean Paul , yabwiye IGIHE ko bari kuganira na abakinnyi batandukanye ariko hari abatarasinya .
Ati " Hari komisiyo ishinzwe kugura abakinnyi , hari benshi iri kuganira nabo ariko nta gusinya birabaho .
Uwo [ Nishimwe ] ntabwo nakubwira ngo arimo cyangwa ntabwo ari mu bari kuganirizwa ariko igihe nikigera muzamenya abakinnyi bashya ba Rayon Sports .
Ku wa Gatanu wa icyumweru gishize , ubuyobozi bwa Rayon Sports bwavuze ko hari abakinnyi batanu bwamaze kugura mu gihe hari na abandi batandatu bakiri bato bazatizwa andi makipe .
Nkurunziza yakomeje agira ati " Abo barahari tuzabatangaza tariki ya 21 Kamena kandi tuzatangaza abakomeye .
Mugheni Fabrice wari wasezeye Rayon Sports , Michael Sarpong wari wirukanywe na Hakizimana Muhadjiri watandukanye na Emirates FC , bari mu bavugwa muri iyi kipe yambara ubururu na umweru nubwo ubuyobozi bwayo bwirinda kugira icyo bubivugaho .
Imikino isigaye ya UEFA Champions League na Europa League izaba muri Kanama , ikinwe nka Igikombe cya Isi
Inama ya Komite Nyobozi ya Impuzamashyirahamwe ya Umupira wa Amaguru ku Mugabane wa Uburayi ( UEFA ) yabaye kuri uyu wa Gatatu , yanzuye ko amarushanwa yayo ya Champions League na Europa League azasubukurwa mu ntangiriro za Kanama nyuma ya uko ahagaritswe muri Werurwe kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Inama ya Komite Nyobozi ya Impuzamashyirahamwe ya Umupira wa Amaguru ku Mugabane wa Uburayi ( UEFA ) yabaye kuri uyu wa Gatatu , yanzuye ko amarushanwa yayo ya Champions League na Europa League azasubukurwa mu ntangiriro za Kanama nyuma ya uko ahagaritswe muri Werurwe kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
UEFA yemeje ko aya marushanwa yombi ahuza amakipe akomeye i Burayi , azasozwa akinwa mu buryo bwa Igikombe cya Isi .
Hemejwe ko imikino isigaye kugira ngo irushanwa rya Champions League rirangire izakinirwa mu Mujyi wa Lisbon .
Umurwa mukuru wa Portugal uzakira imikino ya kimwe cya kane , iya kimwe cya kabiri na umukino wa nyuma , yose izakinwa hagati ya tariki ya 12 na iya 23 Kanama uyu mwaka mu gihe imikino ya kimwe cya umunani yo kwishyura yari isigaye , izakinirwa aho yagombaga kubera cyangwa muri Portugal kuri Est á dio do Drag ã o ya i Porto na Est á dio D .
Afonso Henriques ya i Guimar ã es hagati ya tariki ya 7 na iya 8 Kanama .
Imikino yose isigaye muri kimwe cya kane na kimwe cya kabiri izajya ikinwa ari umwe ( nta mukino wo kwishyura ) , izabera ku bibuga bibiri byo muri Lisbon - Estadio da Luz na Estadio Jose Alvalade .
Champions League yakomwe mu nkokora na Coronavirus kuva tariki ya 11 Werurwe , ubwo imikino ya kimwe cya umunani yari igeze hagati .
Manchester City yagombaga kwakira Real Madrid mu mukino wo kwishyura wari kuba tariki ya 17 Werurwe nyuma ya uko yari yatsindiye muri Espagne ibitego 2 - 1 .
Bayern Munich yari yatsinze Chelsea ibitego 3 - 0 , Juventus itsindwa na Lyon igitego 1 - 0 mu gihe FC Barcelone yari yanganyije na Napoli igitego 1 - 1 .
Amakipe ya Paris Saint - Germain , Atalanta , Atlético Madrid na RB Leipzig yari yamaze kubona itike ya kimwe cya kane .
Umujyi wa Istanbul ( Atatürk Olympic Stadium ) wagombaga kwakira umukino wa nyuma wa UEFA Champions League uyu mwaka , wahawe kwakira uwa umwaka utaha .
Europa League izakinirwa mu Budage
UEFA yemeje ko kandi irushanwa rya Europa League naryo rizakinwa muri ubu buryo bumeze nka Igikombe cya Isi , aho guhera muri kimwe cya kane imikino izabera mu Budage mu Mijyi ya Cologne , Duisburg , Düsseldorf na Gelsenkirchen muri Kanama , haba umukino umwe .
Imikino yo kwishyura yari isigaye nayo izakinirwa aho yagombaga kubera cyangwa mu Budage mu gihe Inter Milan na Getafe , Seville FC na AS Roma zitakinnye umukino na umwe , zizahura inshuro imwe ( nta mukino wo kwishyura uzabaho ) .
Umujyi wa Gda ń sk wo muri Pologne wagombaga kwakira umukino wa nyuma wa uyu mwaka , wahawe kwakira uwa irushanwa rya umwaka utaha .
Europa League yahagaze tariki ya 12 Werurwe , izasubukurwa tariki ya 5 na iya 6 Kanama haba imikino yo kwishyura ( ahabaye imikino ibanza ) mu gihe umukino wa nyuma uzakinwa tariki ya 21 Kanama 2020 .
Siporo zikorwa abantu bategeranye zakomorewe : Ni ryari amakipe ashobora gutangira imyitozo ?
Inama ya Abaminisitiri yateranye ku wa Kabiri tariki ya 16 Werurwe yafatiwemo umwanzuro uvuga ko ibikorwa bya siporo zikorerwa hanze abantu bategeranye zemerewe gukomeza .
Icyakora siporo ikorerwa mu nyubako za imyidagaduro irabujijwe .
Inama ya Abaminisitiri yateranye ku wa Kabiri tariki ya 16 Werurwe yafatiwemo umwanzuro uvuga ko ibikorwa bya siporo zikorerwa hanze abantu bategeranye zemerewe gukomeza .
Icyakora siporo ikorerwa mu nyubako za imyidagaduro irabujijwe .
Imyanzuro ya iyi nama ivuga ko " " " " Amabwiriza arambuye kuri iyi ngingo azatangwa na Minisiteri ya Siporo .
Ni amabwiriza yitezweho kureba niba ashobora gutanga umurongo nka amakipe ashobora gukoramo imyitozo , abakinnyi bategeranye , mbere ya uko imikino imwe na imwe yazasubukurwa .
Tariki ya 15 Werurwe 2020 nibwo ibikorwa byose bya imikino byahagaritswe mu Rwanda , umunsi umwe nyuma ya uko Minisiteri ya Ubuzima itangaje ko hari umurwayi wa mbere wa Coronavirus wabonetse mu gihugu .
Tariki ya 5 Gicurasi , Minisiteri ya Siporo yagiranye inama na Komite Olempike na abahagarariye imikino , hemezwa ko hafi imikino ishobora gusubukurwa ari muri Nzeri mu gihe imyitozo yatangira muri Kanama .
Ku wa 4 Kamena Minisiteri ya Siporo yatangaje ko guhera ku wa 8 Kamena , imikino ikorwa abantu bategeranye irimo uwo kunyoga igare , gutwara imodoka , Tennis , Golf , kugenda na amaguru ( Hiking ) na imikino ngororamubiri ishobora gusubukurwa ariko hakurikizwa amabwiriza yo kwirinda .
Amwe mu bwiriza yari yashyizweho yarimo kuba nka abasiganwa ku maguru bagomba guhana intera mu gihe bakorera muri Stade Amahoro na ahandi haba inzira ya abasiganwa no kuba buri wese akoresha ibikoresho bye ku bajugunya .
Muri Tennis hemejwe ko buri mukinnyi azajya azana imipira ye , akaba ariyo akina ( ashobora gufata mu ntoki ) itari iye akayitanga kuri mugenzi we akoresheje ikirenge cyangwa racket , kuba abakinnyi batemerewe guhinduranya ibibuga no gusiga intera ya metero eshatu hagati yabo ( Tennis ikinwa na babiri ntiyemewe ) .
Hari na abibajije impamvu umukino wa Cricket utabamo kwegerana , utigeze ushyirwa mu yemerewe gusubukura .

Amakipe ashobora kongera gusubukura imyitozo ?
Nka uko no mu bindi bihugu birimo ibya i Burayi biri gukorwa muri iyi minsi , hari ibyiciro bacamo mu kongera gusubukura ibikorwa bya imikino .
Ni intambwe amakipe yo mu Rwanda ategereje kuzahabwaho umurongo .
Mu Bwongereza , u Budage , Espagne na ahandi imikino yasubukuwe , babanje kwemerera abakinnyi gukora ku giti cyabo imikino irimo ngorangingo nko kwiruka .
Icyiciro cya kabiri cyabaye kwemerera amakipe gusubukura imyitozo , bigakorwa abakinnyi bategerena , aho mu cyumweru cya mbere imyitozo yakorwaga mu matsinda ku buryo mu kibuga hatarenga abakinnyi batanu mu gihe mu cyumweru cya kabiri batarengaga 10 .
Iki cyiciro cyakurikiwe no kwemerera amakipe gukorera imyitozo hamwe , ariko hakagira ingamba zo kwirinda zubahirizwa zirimo no gupimwa kenshi kwa abakinnyi dore ko ibi bihugu byo mu Burayi biri mu byazahajwe cyane na Coronavirus .
Hari icyo byafasha amakipe yitegura amarushanwa
Lomami Marcel utoza Gorilla FC yo mu cyiciro cya kabiri izakina imikino ya Playoffs yo guhatanira kuzamuka mu cyiciro cya mbere , yabwiye IGIHE ko nyuma ya amezi atatu imikino imaze ihagaze hari abakinnyi biyongereye ibiro ku buryo baramutse bemerewe gusubukura imyitozo hubahirizwa gusiga intera hagati ya abantu , hari icyo byafasha amakipe .
